{2.49}

[2.49,0]

"na jātīnāṃ kevalānāmadarśanāt | vyaktigrahe ca tacchrabdarūpādanyanna dṛśyate || 49 ||"

[2.49,1]

"jātī"nāntu duśyābhimatānāṃ "kevalānāṃ" vyaktisvarūpavyatiriktānāma"darśanā" eva | "vyaktigrahe" tasyā vyakteḥ | "śabdasya" gaurityasya "rūpādanyat" sāmānyaṃ "na dṛśyate" | (49)

{2.50}

[2.50,0]

"jñānamātrārthakaraṇepyayogyamat eva tat | tadayogyatayā'rūpaṃ taddhyavastuṣu lakṣaṇam || 50 ||"

[2.50,1]

"ata evā"dṛśyamānatvāt "jñānamātra"syārthasyārthakriyāyāḥ "karaṇepyayogyameva tat" | antyā hīyaṃ bhāvānāmarthakriyā yaduta svajñānajananaṃ | tatrāpya"yogyatayā" tatsāmānyama"rūpaṃ" niḥsvabhāvaṃ | hiryasmāt sarvvārthakriyāyāmaśaktatva"mavastuṣu lakṣaṇaṃ" sarvasāmarthyarahitaṃ hyavastviṣyate | (50)

{2.51}

[2.51,0]

tathā ca sāmānyamiti na vastu |

[2.51,1]

"yathoktaviparītaṃ yat tat svalakṣaṇamiṣyate |"

[2.51,2]

"yatho"ktātsāmānyā"dviparītaṃ" yatta"tsvalakṣaṇa"mucyate | idañca vaiparītyaṃ | anabhidheyatvaṃ | tatvānyatvābhyāṃ vācyatvaṃ | asadarthapratyayāviśiṣṭapratibhāsaviṣayatvaṃ | asādhāraṇatvaṃ | saṃketasmaraṇānapekṣapratipattikatvaṃ | anyarūpaviviktasvarūpapratibhāsavattvaṃ | arthakriyākṣamatvañca | etadyuktaṃ svalakṣaṇamiṣyate | etadviparyayasyāvastutvasādhanasya sāmānyalakṣaṇatvāt |

[2.51,3]

yaccātatkāryavyavacchedalakṣaṇamuktaṃ |

[2.51,4]

"sāmānyaṃ trividhaṃ, tacca bhāvābhāvobhayāśrayāt || 51 ||"

[2.51,5]

"sāmānyaṃ tacca trividhaṃ" boddhavyaṃ "bhāvābhāvobhayāśrayāt" | kiñcid bhāvopādānaṃ sāmānyaṃ yathā rūpādīn bhāvānāśritya kṛtakatvādiśabdavācyaṃ liṅgaṃ | abhāvopādānaṃ yathopalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptasyāsato'nupalabdhiranutpattimattvādi ca | taddhyabhāvāśrayaṃ sāmānyaṃ liṅgaṃ | ubhayāśrayamanupalabdhimātraṃjñeyatvādi ca bhāvābhāvasādharaṇatvāt | (51)

{2.52}

[2.52,0]

"yadi bhāvāśrayaṃ jñānaṃ bhāve bhāvānubandhataḥ || noktottaratvād dṛṣṭatvād; atītādiṣu cānyathā || 52 ||"

[2.52,1]

"yadi" kiñcitsāmānyaṃ "bhā" tat "jñānaṃ tadbhāve" bhāvaviṣayaṃ prāpnoti | bhāvānubandhato bhāvānvayavyatirekānuvidhānāt | naitadyuktaṃ na tadvastu | abhidheyatvādinoktottaratvāt | niṣiddhaṃ hi sāmānyasya vastutvamanantarameva prapañcenetyanumānabādhitatvaṃ pratijñāyāḥ | dṛṣṭatvāt | "atītādiṣu cānyathā" vastuvyatirekeṇaivāsīd ghaṭo bhaviṣyati ceti sāmānyabuddhirutpadyate ityasiddhatāpi bhāvānubandhata iti hetoḥ | (52)

{2.53}

[2.53,0]

"bhāvadharmatvahāniśced bhāvagrahaṇapūrvakam | tajjñānamityadoṣoyaṃ;"

[2.53,1]

vastu vinā sāmānyabuddhyutpāde "bhāvadha" sāmānyasya prasajyate cet | "bhāva"sya rūpāde"rgrahaṇapūrvvakaṃ" tasya sāmānyasya sādhāraṇabāhyarūpatayā'dhyavasitabuddhyākāralakṣaṇasyādhyavasāyena "jñānamitya"yamavastudharmatvalakṣaṇo'doṣo "doṣo" na bhavati | na hi sāmānyaṃ rūpādiriva bhāvarūpatayā jñānaviṣaya iti bhāvadharma iṣṭaṃ |

[2.53,2]

"meyaṃ tvekaṃ svalakṣaṇām || 53 ||"

[2.53,3]

kintu bhāvavāsanāprabodhaprasūtavikalpakalpitatvāt | paramārthato "meyaṃ tvekaṃ " | tasyaiva rūpabuddhyutpādakatvāt | (53)

{2.54}

[2.54,0]

"tasmādarthakriyāsiddheḥ sadasattāvicāraṇāt ||"

[2.54,1]

"sāmānyasya" tu kalpitatvāt | sāmarthyābhāvātsvalakṣaṇamekaṃ prameyaṃ "tasmāda" | arthakriyārthibhiḥ "sadasattābhyāṃ" tasyaiva "vicāraṇāt" | asattvamapi svalakṣaṇasyaiva vicintyate |

[2.54,2]

yadyekameva prameyaṃ tadācāryeṇa prameyadvaividhyaṃ yaduktaṃ na svasāmānyalakṣaṇābhyāmanyatprameyamastīti tad virudhyate ityāha |

[2.54,3]

"tasya svapararūpābhyāṃ gatermeyadvayaṃ matam || 54 ||"

[2.54,4]

"tasya" svalakṣaṇasya pratyakṣataḥ "sva"rūpeṇānumānataḥ "pararūpeṇa" sāmānyākāreṇa "gatermeyadvayaṃ mataṃ" na tu bhūtasāmānyasya sattvāt (54) |

{ii.iv}

<4. anumānacintā>

<(1) anumānasiddhiḥ>

<ka. bhrāntamanumānaṃ pramāṇām>

{2.55}

[2.55,0]

"ayathābhiniveśena dvitīyā bhrāntiriṣyate |"

[2.55,1]

yā ca "dvitīyā" pararūpeṇa gati"rayathābhiniveśena bhrāntiriṣyate" sā'numānaṃ yathā'rthosti yathā vā svākārastathā nābhiniviśate kintu svākāraṃ bāhyaṃ sādhāraṇatayā manyate |

[2.55,2]

"gatiścet pararūpeṇa na ca bhrānteḥ pramāṇatā || 55 ||"

[2.55,3]

nanvanumānaṃ "pararūpeṇa gatiścet" tadā bhrāntireva | "na ca bhrānteḥ pramāṇate"ṣyate mṛgatṛṣṇāderiva | (55)

{2.56}

[2.56,0]

atrocyate |

[2.56,1]

"abhiprāyāvisaṃvādādapi bhrānteḥ pramāṇatā ||"

[2.56,2]

"gatirapyanyathā dṛṣṭā;"

[2.56,3]

"bhrānterapi pramāṇatā | abhiprāyasyā"rthakriyārthibhiḥ jñānagocaratayā'bhiprāyaviṣayīkṛtasyārthakriyāsamarthasyārthasya "saṃvādāt" | arthakriyārthino hi tatsādhanasamarthārthaprāpakaṃ pramāṇamicchanti | "anyathā" pararūpeṇa "gatirapi" kācidabhipretārthasamvādikā "dṛṣṭe"ti pramāṇameva |

[2.56,4]

nanvanumānaṃ vastveva gṛhṇat pramāṇamastu kiṃ bhrāntiriṣyate ityāha |

[2.56,5]

"pakṣaścāyaṃ kṛtottaraḥ || 56 ||"

[2.56,6]

"pakṣaścāyaṃ" prāgeva na tadvastu abhidheyatvādityādinā (2 | 11) "kṛtottaraḥ" | (56)

{2.57}

[2.57,0]

nanu bhrāntamapi yadyanumānaṃ pramāṇaṃ tadā sarvvaiva bhrāntiḥ pramāṇaṃ syādityāha |

[2.57,1]

"maṇipradīpaprabhayormaṇibuddhyābhidhāvatoḥ | mithyājñānāviśeṣepi viśeṣorthakriyāṃ prāti || 57 ||"

[2.57,2]

"maṇipradīpayo"rye "prabhe" tayo"rmaṇibuddhyā" maṇirevāyamityadhyavasāyena tadgrahaṇārthaṃ "dhāvato mithyājñānasya" bhrāntatvasyā"viśeṣepi viśeṣo'rthakriyāmprati" | maṇiprabhāyāṃmapyadhyavasāyī maṇisādhyāmarthakriyāṃ prāpnoti | (57)

{2.58}

[2.58,0]

"yathā tathā'yathārthatvepyanumānatadābhayoḥ | arthakriyānurodhena pramāṇatvaṃ vyavasthitam || 58 ||"

[2.58,1]

dīpaprabhāyāntu maṇivyavasāyī tanna prāpnotīti "yathā tathā" trirūpaliṅgaja"manu"bhañca tanna na tathā | tayoḥ svākāre bāhyadhyavasāyapravṛttatvāt ayathārthatvepi "pramāṇa"tvaṃ "vyavasthitaṃ" | viśeṣeṇāvasthita"marthakriyānurodhenā"numānameva pramāṇaṃ | paramparayā'rthādutpatteḥ tatprāpakatvāt | netaradviparyayāt | tasmātprameyadvitvaṃ gatibhedāt | (58)

{2.59–2.60}

[2.59–2.60,0]

tayorlakṣaṇaṃ grahaṇañcākhyātumāha |

[2.59–2.60,1]

"buddhiryatrārthasāmarthyādanvayavyatirekiṇī | tasya svatatraṃ grahaṇamato'nyad vastvatīndriyam || 59 ||"

[2.59–2.60,2]

arthasāmarthyājjāyamānā buddhiryatrānvayavyatirekiṇī tatsvalakṣaṇantasya grahaṇamaparāśrayaṃ svarūpagrahaṇaṃ svajanyayā'rthasvarūpayā buddhyā sākṣāttasya grahaṇāt | ataḥ svalakṣaṇatvādanyadvastu yadanvayavyatirekau nānukaroti buddhiḥ sākṣādapratibhāsamānaṃ kevalamadhyavasāyaviṣayaḥ tatsāmānyalakṣaṇa"matīndriyaṃ" buddhiṣvapratibhāsanāt (59) |

[2.59–2.60,3]

kathantatpratyetavyamityāha |

[2.59–2.60,4]

"tasyādṛṣṭātmarūpasya gateranyortha āśrayaḥ | tadāśrayeṇa sambandhī yadi syād gamakastadā || 60 ||"

[2.59–2.60,5]

"tasya" sāmānyasya svalakṣaṇaviśeṣeṇa svalakṣaṇavivekenā"dṛṣṭātmarūpasya" gateḥ pratīteḥ tasmāda"nyo'rtho" liṅgabhūta "āśrayaḥ" siddhinimittaṃ "yadi" tataḥ pratyetavyenānagnivyavacchedādinā "tadāśrayeṇa" ca dharmiṇā "sambandhī" sambandhavān "syāttadā " nānyathā | anane sādhyapratibandho'nvayavyatirekarūpaḥ pakṣadharmatā ca liṅgasyoktā (60) |

{2.61}

[2.61,0]

nanvanyāśrayeṇa ca svarūpapratītirbhaviṣyati tathāpi parokṣatā kathamityāha |

[2.61,1]

"gamakānugasāmānyarūpeṇaiva tadā gatiḥ | tasmāt sarvaḥ parokṣortho viśeṣeṇa na gamyate || 61 ||"

[2.61,2]

"tadā'rthā"ntarātpratītikāle "gamakaṃ" pakṣasapakṣānuyāyi liṅgaṃ | tadanuyāyinā tadvyāpakena "sāmānyarūpeṇaiva" parokṣortho gamyate | na tu sarvvato vyāvṛttena viśiṣṭena rūpeṇa | "tasmātsarvaḥ parokṣo'rthaḥ" pratīyamāno "na viśeṣeṇa" kathañcid "gamyate" yena parokṣatāhāniḥ syāt | (61)

{2.62}

[2.62,0]

"yā ca sambandhino dharmād bhūtirdharmiṇi jñāyate | sānumānaṃ parokṣāṇāmekāntenaiva sādhanam || 62 ||"

[2.62,1]

"yā ca sambandhino dharmāda"nvayavyatirekato liṅgāt tadāśraye "dharmiṇi jñāyate" parokṣārthapratītiḥ | "sānumānaṃ" trirūpaliṅgaprabhavattvāt | tadevānumānaṃ "parokṣāṇā" | pratyakṣasya tatrāvṛtteḥ | (62)

{2.63}

[2.63,0]

"na pratyakṣaparokṣābhyāṃ meyasyānyasya sambhavaḥ | tasmāt prameyadvitvena pramāṇadvitvamiṣyate || 63 ||"

[2.63,1]

"na" ca "pratyakṣaparokṣābhyāmanyasya prameyasya sambhava" iti darśitaṃ prāk | "tasmātprame" | prameyamadhigacchat pramāṇamucyate | (63)

{2.64}

<kha. dvitīyaṃ pramāṇamanumānam>

[2.64,0]

"tryekasaṃkhyānirāso vā prameyadvayadarśanāt ||"

[2.64,1]

tacca dvidhamiti tadgrāhakaṃ dvayamapi pramāṇameva || "prameyadvayasya darśanāt" | "tryekasaṃkhyānirāso vā" boddhavyaḥ | tṛtīyādikaṃ na pramāṇaṃ tṛtīyādiprameyābhāvāt | nāpyekaṃ dvitīyasya prameyasya tenānadhigateḥ | na hi pratyakṣaṃ svalakṣaṇasāmarthyāt tadākāragrāhi jātaṃ sāmānyaṃ pratyeti kalpanāgamyatvāttasya ||

[2.64,2]

"ekamevāprameyatvādasataścenmataṃ ca naḥ || 64 ||"

[2.64,3]

nanu pratyakṣa"mekameva" pramāṇamasato"'prameyatvāt" | asacca sāmānyamatrāha | "asato'prameyatvaṃ matañca naḥ" | (64)

{2.65–2.66}

[2.65–2.66,0]

"anekānto'prameyatve'sadbhāvasya viniścayaḥ | tanniścayapramāṇāṃ vā dvitīyaṃ;"

[2.65–2.66,1]

kimaniṣṭamāpadyate | svalakṣaṇameva tu pararūpeṇa gateḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇamiṣṭaṃ | tacca sadeveti kathamaprameyaṃ tatastatsādhanamapi pramāṇameva || tathā'sato'"prameyatve" sādhye'sattvāditi hetura"nekāntopi" | tathā hi paralokāderasattayā cā rvvā ke ṇāpīṣyata eva kenāpi pramāṇena niścayaḥ | athavā prameyatvābhāvasyāpyasattvahetunaiva niścaya iti vyaktamanaikāntikatvaṃ | ataśca yata eva pramāṇāttasyā"bhāvasya niścaya"stadevadvitīyampramāṇamanumānaṃ nādhyakṣaṃ |

[2.65–2.66,2]

kasmādevamityāha |

[2.65–2.66,3]

"nākṣajā matiḥ || 35 ||"

[2.65–2.66,4]

"abhāve'rthabalājjāterarthaśaktyanapekṣaṇo | vyavadhānādibhāvepi jāyetendriyajā matiḥ || 66 ||"

[2.65–2.66,5]

"nākṣajā mati"rabhāve viṣaye pravartate'rthasya grāhyasya balājjāteḥ | yadbalena pratyakṣaṃ pravartate tadevapratipadyate na cābhāvasya sāmarthya nāma | yadi punararthasāmarthyānapekṣaṇamasya tadā grāhyasyārthasya śaktyanapekṣaṇe tadvyavadhānādibhāvepīndriyajā matirjāyeta | na caitadasti | tato'rthasāmarthyāpekṣi nābhāvaviṣayaṃ bhavitumarhati | (65,66)

{2.67}

[2.67,0]

syādetat |

[2.67,1]

"abhāve vinivṛttiścet pratyakṣasyaiva niścayaḥ | viruddhaṃ saiva vā liṅgamanvayavyatirekiṇī || 67 ||"

[2.67,2]

"pratyakṣasyaiva" pravṛttirbhāve sattvaniścayo "vinivṛttiścābhāve" niścayo na tu pramāṇāntaravṛttiriti cet | viruddhamidaṃ yaḥ pratyakṣābhāvānniścayaḥ sa pratyakṣāditi | na hi pratyakṣatanivṛttyoraikātmyaṃ tathā hyabhāvo bhāva eva syāt | bhāvopi cābhāvaḥ | na ca pratyakṣatanivṛttāvapyavaśyamabhāvaḥ | vyavadhānādiṣvarthasattvepi tasyābhāvāt | athārthānvayavyatirekānuvidhāyinī pratyakṣanivṛttirekajñānasaṃsargipadārthāntaropalabdhirūpā'bhāvaniścayahetustadā "saiva" pratyakṣanivṛttiranupalabdhyākhyā"nvayavyatirekiṇī " tajjā pratītiranumānameveti kathaṃ nāpratyakṣaṃ pramāṇaṃ | (67)

{2.68}

<ga. pramāṇādvayasiddhiḥ>

[2.68,0]

kiñca |

[2.68,1]

"siddhaṃ ca paracaitanyapratipatteḥ pramādvayam |"

[2.68,2]

"paracaitanyapratipatteḥ pramāṇadvayaṃ siddhaṃ" | na hi pratyakṣādarvvāgdarśanaḥ paracaitanyamavaiti | kintu svasantāne buddhipūrvakatvenopalabdhaceṣṭādidarśanāttadanumānaṃ paracittaniścayaḥ kimastītyāha |

[2.68,3]

"vyavahārādau pravṛtteśca siddhastadbhāvaniścayaḥ || 68 ||"

[2.68,4]

parasparapreṣaṇādhyeṣaṇavyavahārādau "pravṛtteśca siddhaśca" tasyāḥ paracaitanyapratipatte"rbhāvaniścayaḥ" | (68)

{2.69}

<gha. avisaṃvādādanumānaṃ pramāṇam>

[2.69,0]

nanvanumānābhimatā pratītirnāstyeveti na brūmaḥ | kintu prāmāṇye tasyāḥ vipratipadyāmaha ityāha |

[2.69,1]

"pramāṇamavisaṃvādāt tat kvacid vyabhicārataḥ | nāśvāsa iti celliṅgaṃ durdṛṣṭiratadīdṛśam || 69 ||"

[2.69,2]

"pramāṇanta"danumānama"visamvādāt" | pratyakṣamapi hi samvādakatvāt pramāṇaṃ taccānumānasyāpi samānaṃ | "kvaci"cchyāmatādisādhanārthamupātte tatputrādau liṅge "vyabhicārataḥ" samvāde'"nāśvāsa" iti cet | liṅgasya "durvṛṣṭi"rbhrāntiraliṅga eva liṅgabuddhistasyā etalli"ṅgamīdṛśaṃ" vyabhicāri bhavataḥ pratibhāti | na khalu trividhaṃ liṅgaṃ sādhyavyabhicāri | yacca vyabhicāri tattrividhameva na bhavati | (69)

{2.70}

[2.70,0]

etadevāha |

[2.70,1]

"yataḥ kadācitsiddhā'sya pratītirvastunaḥ kvacit | tadavaśyaṃ tato jātaṃ tatsvabhāvopi vā bhavet || 70 ||"

[2.70,2]

"yato vastuno" dhūmaśiṃśapādeḥ liṅgā"dasya" sādhyasya vahrivṛkṣādeḥ "kvaciddharmiṇi "numānakāle "pratītiḥ siddhā tad" dhūmādikaṃ "tato" vahnyādera"vaśyaṃ jātaṃ" | tacchiṃśapādikaṃ tasya vṛkṣasya "svabhāvopi vā'vaśyambhavet" | (70)

{2.71}

[2.71,0]

na ca kāryasvabhāvayoḥ kāraṇavyāpakavyabhicāro yasmāt |

[2.71,1]

"svanimittāt svabhāvād vā vinā nārthasya sambhavaḥ || yacca rūpaṃ tayordṛṣṭaṃ tedavānyatra lakṣaṇam || 71 ||"

[2.71,2]

"svasya nimittā"tkāraṇādvinā, "svabhāvād" vyāpakādvā "vinā'rthasya" kāryasyavyāpyasya ca na "sambhavaḥ" | tadutpādyatvāttadrūpatvācca | tatastadāśrayeṇotpannā'numānapratītiravyabhicāriṇyeva "yacca tayordhū"maśiṃśapayo "rūpaṃ" sādhyakāryasvabhāvatvasyāvyabhicāranimittaṃ "dṛṣṭaṃ tadevānya"trāpi hetau "lakṣaṇaṃ" boddhavyaṃ | na ca tatputratvaṃ śyāmatvasya kāryaṃ svabhāvo vā | tato yad vyabhicāri tadaliṅgameva | (71)

{2.72}

<ṅa. anupalabdheḥ pratibandhaḥ>

[2.72,0]

anupalabdheravyabhicāraṃ darśayitumāha |

[2.72,1]

"svabhāve svanimitte vā dṛśye darśanahetuṣu | anyeṣu satsvadṛśye ca sattā vā tadvataḥ katham || 72 ||"

[2.72,2]

pratiṣedhasya "sva" svasya niṣedhyātmano "nimitte" kāraṇe | "dṛśye" darśanayogye "darśana"sya hetuṣvindriyamanaskārādiṣvanyeṣu satsu vidyamāneṣudṛśye'nupalabhyamāne ca "tadvato" dṛśyānupalambhavato bhāvasya "sattā vā kathaṃ" yujyate | na hi "satsvanyeṣū"palambhapratyayeṣu dṛśyasya sataḥ kadācidanupalambhasambhavaḥ | tasmād dṛśyānupalabdhirarthābhāva eva bhavatīti tatprabhavā'bhāvapratītiravisamvādinī | tasmātsādhyapratibaddhaliṅgaprasūtatvāt trividhaliṅgajepyanumāne nāstyanāśvāsaḥ | (72)

{2.73}

<naḥ anumānaṃ trividham>

<chaḥ tatra vārvākamatanirāsaḥ>

[2.73,0]

"aprāmāṇye ca sāmānyabuddhestallopa āgataḥ | pretyabhāvavad;"

[2.73,1]

evamapi "tvaprāmāṇye" sāmānyabuddheriṣyamāṇe tasya parokṣasyārthasyānumānavyavasthāpyamānasya "lopo"'bhāva "āgataḥ" | "pretyabhāvavat" paralokasyeva | yadi hi pratyakṣamekaṃ pramāṇaṃ tadā yatra tanna pravartate tasyāpyabhāva eva syāt | na caitadasti | na hi cārvvāko deśāntarasthaṃ svapitaramanupalabhamānastabhāvaṃ vyavasthāpayitumarhati |

[2.73,2]

syādetat |

[2.73,3]

"akṣaistat paryāyeṇa pratīyate || 73 ||"

[2.73,4]

nopalabhyamānamevāsti kintu "paryyāyeṇa" paripāṭyā'kṣairyat "pratīyate" tadapyasti cet | pitrādayaścopalabdhā upalapsyante ceti santyeva | (73)

{2.74}

[2.74,0]

"tacca nendriyaśaktyādāvakṣabuddherasambhavāt | abhāvapratipattau syād buddherjanmānimittakam || 74 ||"

[2.74,1]

"tacca na yuktaṃ" indriyākhyāyāṃ "śaktā"vādigrahaṇādāhārādeḥ kṣudupaghātādisāmarthye ca paryyāyeṇāpīndriya"buddherasambhavādabhāvapratītau" satyāṃ pratyakṣāyā "buddherjanmānimittakaṃ " | na hi dṛṣṭamātrebhyo viṣayālokamanaskāracakṣurgolakebhyo'dhyakṣajanma satsvapi teṣvabhāvāt vyatirekādatiriktaṃ kiñcidadṛśyaṃ kāraṇamiṣyate yasyendriyamiti vyapadeśaḥ | tasya paryyāyeṇāpi nādhyakṣaṃ grāhakamastītyabhāvaḥ syāt | tataścākāraṇakaṃ pratyakṣajanma prāptaṃ | ahetośca nityaṃ satvamasattvamvā syādi (1 | 82)tyuktaṃ || (74)

{2.75}

<jaḥ pratyakṣānna sāmānyapratītiḥ>

[2.75,0]

syādetat | pratyakṣādeva sāmānyapratītirbhaviṣyati kimanumānenetyāha |

[2.75,1]

"svalakṣaṇe ca pratyakṣamavikalpatayā vinā | vikalpena na sāmānyagrahastasmistato'numā || 75 ||"

[2.75,2]

"svalakṣaṇe ca pratyakṣamavikalpatayā pravartate" bhavati | "tataḥ" kāraṇā"ttasmin" sāmānye'numaiva vikalpikā | nādhyakṣamavikalpakaṃ || (75)

{2.76}

[2.76,0]

nanu |

[2.76,1]

"prameyaniyame varṇānityatā na pratīyate | pramāṇamanyat tadbuddhirvinā liṅgena saṃbhavāt || 76 ||"

[2.76,2]

pratyakṣaṃ svalakṣaṇaviṣayamanumānaṃ sāmānyaviṣayamiti prameyasya "niyame" svīkriyamāṇe "varṇṇa"sya nīlādervviṣayasyā"nityatā"'nityatāsāmānyātmatā "na pratīyata" iti prāptaṃ | na hi sāmānyaviśeṣātmakaṃ prameyaṃ viśeṣamātraviṣayeṇādhyakṣeṇa sāmānyamātraviṣayeṇānumānena vā pratyetuṃ śakyaṃ | pratīyate cāta"stadbuddhirpramāṇamanyat" syāt | na pratyakṣaṃ sāmānyasya grahaṇāt | nāpyanumānaṃ "vinā liṅgena sambhavāt" | viśeṣasyāpi grahaṇācca | (76)

{2.77}

[2.77,0]

tathā |

[2.77,1]

"viśeṣadṛṣṭe liṅgasya sambandhasyāprasiddhitaḥ | tatpramāṇāntaraṃ meyabahutvād bahutāpi vā || 77 ||"

[2.77,2]

"viśeṣadṛṣṭe" pratyakṣeṇāgniṃ dṛṣṭvā kramāttameva dhūmālliṅgāt sa evāyaṃ vahniriti niścinotyanumānena | "liṅgasya sambandhāsiddhitaḥ tatpramāṇāntaraṃ"syāt | na hi tatpratyakṣaṃ liṅgaṃ balādutpatteḥ | nāpyanumānaṃ dahanadhūmaviśeṣayoḥ sambandhāgrahaṇāt | tasmāt "meyā"nāṃ pratyakṣaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ sāmānyaṃ sāmānyaviśeṣāṇāṃ "bahutvāt bahutāpi vā" (77)

{2.78}

[2.78,0]

"pramāṇānāmanekasya vṛtterekatra vā yathā | viśeṣadṛṣṭerekatrisaṃkhyāpoho na vā bhavet || 78 ||"

[2.78,1]

"pramāṇānāṃ syāt | anekasya" vā pramāṇasyaikatra viṣaye vṛtteḥ pramāṇabahutā syāt | yathaikameva svalakṣaṇaṃ pratyakṣeṇa viśeṣadṛṣṭena cānumānena pratīyate | prameyasya dvitvagrahaṇayorniyame pramādvitvaṃ syāt nānyathā | tryekasaṃkhyāyā apoho ya uktaḥ prameyadvitvāt sa "na vā bhavet" || (78)

{2.79}

[2.79,0]

"viṣayāniyamādanyaprameyasya ca sambhavāt |"

[2.79,1]

"viṣayasya" grahaṇā"niyamāt" yadā hyekenāpi pramāṇenānekaṃ gṛhyate tadā prameyadvitvepyekameva pramāṇaṃ syāt | prameyadvayā"danyasya ca" sāmānyaviśeṣasya "meyasya sambha" | tryādikamvā tadgrāhakaṃ mānaṃ bhavet |

[2.79,2]

atrocyate |

[2.79,3]

"yojanād varṇasāmānye nāyaṃ doṣaḥ prasajyate || 79 ||"

[2.79,4]

vikalpakena jñānenānityatāyā "varṇṇasāmānye yojanādayaṃ" sāmānyaviśeṣātmakaprameyagrāhakapramāṇāntarābhyupagamalakṣaṇo "doṣo na prasaṃ" | na hi viśeṣo'nityatayā yojyate | vikalpānāmatadviṣayatvasyoktervvakṣyamāṇatvācca | (79)

{2.80}

<pha. anityādayo nāvastudharmāḥ>

[2.80,0]

nanu varṇṇasāmānyasyāvastutvāttadyojitā'nityatādayo'vastudharmāḥ syurityāha |

[2.80,1]

"nāvasturūpaṃ tasyaiva tathā siddhe prasādhanāt | anyatra nānyasiddhiścenna tasyaiva prasiddhitaḥ || 80 ||"

[2.80,2]

"nāvastuno" rūpamanityatvādi | "tasyaiva" vastunastathā'nityatvādibhirākāraiḥ "siddhe" rniścayasya prāk "prasādhanāt" | adhyavasāyānurodhena hi vikalpānāṃ viṣayavyavasthā | yadyapi caite svākāragrāhiṇastathāpi bāhyameva viṣayatayā vyavasthāpyante anādyabhyāsaviśeṣāt | anumānantu vastupratibaddhaliṅgaprabhavatvādyathāvasthitameva vastu vyavasyatīti vastveva kṣaṇasthitidharmakamasmātsiddhaṃ | tato nāvasturūpamanityatvādi ||

[2.80,3]

syādetad | anyatrāvastuni sāmānye'nityatādisambandhini sidhyatyanyasya vastuno'nityarūpasya na siddhiriti cet | naitadyuktaṃ "tasyaiva" vastunaḥ tasyaivānityarūpasyādhyavasāyavaśenānumānāt "prasiddhitaḥ" | (80)

{2.81}

<ña. liṅgadhīsaṃvādakatā>

[2.81,0]

kathaṃ punarvvastvadhyavasāye'pi tatsamvādakatetyāha |

[2.81,1]

"yo hi bhāvo yathābhūto sa tādṛgliṅgacetasaḥ | hetustajjā tathābhūte tasmād vastuni liṅgidhīḥ || 81 ||"

[2.81,2]

"yo hi" sādhyadharmo "yathābhūtaḥ" kāraṇavyāpakasvabhāvaḥ"sa tādṛśaḥ" kāraṇakāryatayā vyāpakavyāpyatayā gṛhītavyāptikasya "liṅgasya cetasaḥ" paraṃparāhetuḥ |"tajjā tasmā"lliṅgacetaso jātā | "tathābhūte vastuni" kāraṇavyāpakarūpe sādhyadharme "liṅgidhīḥ" | tasmātparaṃparayā sādhyapratibandhāt liṅgidhīḥ satyeva vastuni bhavantī tatsamvādātpramāṇameva | (81)

{2.82}

[2.82,0]

nanu liṅgamapi liṅgivatsāmānyameva | tathā dhūmaḥ kṛtakaṃ vetyeva na liṅgaṃ kintarhi vahnikāryatayā'nityatvavyāpyatayā ca gṛhītaṃ | na ca viśeṣe vyāptigrahaḥ | sāmānyañca nādhyakṣagamyaṃ | vikalpamātreṇa tatpratītāvanāśvāsaḥ | naiṣa doṣaḥ | pratyakṣeṇa kāraṇakāryayorvyāvṛttidvayaviśiṣṭayorgṛ hītayorvvijātīyavyāvṛttyāśrayeṇotpannavikalpena kvacidanumānena vyāptiṃ gṛhītavataḥ paścād dhūmakṛtakatvādidarśanāttādrūpye kāryavyāpyabuddhirliṅgabuddhiḥ | sā ca tatpratibandhādanumānameveti nāstyanāśvāsaḥ | etadevāha |

[2.82,1]

"liṅgaliṅgidhiyorevaṃ pāramparyeṇa vastuni | pratibandhāt tadābhāsaśūnyayorapyavaṃcanam || 82 ||"

[2.82,2]

liṅgaliṅgi"dhiyorevamukta"kramāt "pāramparyeṇa vastuni pratibandhātta"yorliṅgaliṅgino"rābhāsaḥ" sākṣāt svarūpapratibhāsaḥ | "tacchūnyayorapi" liṅgaliṅgivastuni "avañcanaṃ" samvādanaṃ | (82)

{2.83}

[2.83,0]

nanu liṅgabuddherapi liṅgibuddhitvāt pṛthak upādānamanarthakaṃ | nānarthakaṃ | pratyakṣamudbhūtavikalpo vā tadbuddhiriti vipratipattinirāsārthatvāt | yadi pramāṇe liṅgaliṅgidhiyau tadā pratyakṣavadabhrānte syātāmityāha |

[2.83,1]

"tadrūpādhyavasāyācca tayostadrūpaśūnyayoḥ | tadrūpāvañcakatvepi kṛtā bhrāntivyavasthitiḥ || 83 ||"

[2.83,2]

"tayo"rdvayoḥ "tadrūpa"sya liṅgaliṅgi"rūpa"syā"dhyavasāyāt" pravartane sati vastuni paramparayā tatpratibaddhatayā ca "tadrūpa"syā"vañcakatve" samvādakatve"pi bhrāntivyavasthitiḥ" kṛtā | kasmādityāha"tadrūpaśūnyayoḥ" | na hi liṅgaliṅgisvarūpapratibhāsinyau dhiyāvime svapratibhāse'narthe'rthādhyāvasāyena pravṛttatvāt | (83)

{2.84}

[2.84,0]

"tasmād vastuni boddhavye vyāpakaṃ vyāpyacetasaḥnimittaṃ tatsvabhāvo vā kāraṇaṃ, tacca taddhiyaḥ || 84 ||"

[2.84,1]

"tasmādvastuni" vidhinā "boddhavye vyāpakaṃ" sādhyaṃ | "vyāpyacetaso" liṅgabuddhe"rnimitte" paramparayā | yasmā"tsvabhāvo" vā tad vyāpakaṃ | vyāpyasya yathānityatvaṃ kṛtakatvasya | "kāraṇa"mvā dahano "dhūmasya | tacca" vyāpyacetasa"staddhiyaḥ" svabhāvakāraṇadhiyo nimittamiti tayādhyavasitasya samvādaniyamaḥ samvāditvamevaṃ pratyakṣasyāpi prāmāṇyalakṣaṇaṃ | (84)

{2.85}

<(2) anupalavdhicintā>

[2.85,0]

"pratiṣedhastu sarvatra sādhyate'nupalambhataḥ | siddhiṃ pramāṇairvadatāmarthādeva viparyayāt || 85 ||"

[2.85,1]

"pratiṣedha"stu yatra sākṣānniṣedhyānupalabdhirvviruddhā hyupalabdhirvvā darśyate "tatra " | yasmā"tpramāṇai"rarthasya "siddhiṃ vadatāmarthā"tsāmārthyā"deva "tpramāṇābhāvādarthābhāvaḥ sidhyati | (85)

{2.86}

[2.86,0]

nanu viruddhādyupalabdhāvanupalambhaḥ kathaṃ niṣedhasādhaka ityāha |

[2.86,1]

"dṛṣṭā viruddhadharmoktistasya tatkāraṇasya vā | niṣedhe yāpi tasyaiva sā'pramāṇatvasūcanā || 86 ||"

[2.86,2]

dṛṣṭā viruddhadharmasyoktiryā "tasya" niṣedhyasya "tatkāraṇasya" kartavye yathā nātra śītasparśo na vā romaharṣayuktapuruṣavānayaṃ pradeśo vahneriti | "sāpi " niṣedhyasyaivā"pramāṇatvasya" pramāṇarahitatvasya "sūcanā" | viruddhasya kāraṇaviruddhatvasya copalambhena niṣedhyānupalambha eva khyāpyate | (86)

{2.87–2.88}

[2.87–2.88,0]

"anyathaikasya dharmasya svabhāvoktyā parasya tat | nāstitvaṃ kena gamyeta;"

[2.87–2.88,1]

"anyathaikasya" viruddhāde"rdharmasya svabhāvoktyā" sattāpratipādanena "parasya" niṣedhyasya tannāstitvaṃ sisādhayiṣitaṃ "kena" kāraṇena "gamyeta" | na hyanyasattve'parasya satvābhāvotiprasaṅgāt | aniṣiddhopalabdherabhāvāsiddheḥ ||

[2.87–2.88,2]

"virodhāccedasāvapi || 87 ||"

[2.87–2.88,3]

"siddhaḥ kena;"

[2.87–2.88,4]

atha yanniṣidhyate yaccopadarśyate tayo"rvvirodhāt" sahānavasthānalakṣaṇādekabhāve'nyābhāva iti "cet" | nanva"sāvapi" (87) virodhaḥ "kena" prakāreṇa "siddhaḥ" ||

[2.87–2.88,5]

"asahasthānāditi cet tat kuto matam || dṛśyasya darśanābhāvāditi cet sā'pramāṇatā || 88 ||"

[2.87–2.88,6]

dvayoḥ sahānavasthānādvirodhaḥ siddha iti cet | tatsahānavasthānaṃ kuto hetormataṃ yena virodhavyavasthā || avikalakāraṇasya pravartamānasya "dṛśyasyā"nyabhāve'"darśanāt" sahānavasthānagati"riti cet" | nanu yadevādarśanaṃ "sā(')pramāṇatā" pramāṇarahitatā'nupalabdhirityarthaḥ | (88)

{2.89}

[2.89,0]

"tasmāt svaśabdenoktā'pi sā'bhāvasya prasādhikā | yasyāpramāṇaṃ sā'vācyo niṣedhastena sarvathā || 89 ||"

[2.89,1]

yasmādavaśyaṃ paramparayānupalabdhereva pratiṣedhaḥ | "tasmātsvaśabdenā"nupalambhasvarūpa vācakaśabdeno"ktā" svabhāvānupalambhādā"vapi" śabdādanuktāpi viruddhopalabdhyādau "sānu"palabdhira"bhāvasādhikā" | tasyā eva pratipādyatvāt | "yasya" tu cā rvvā ka sya sā'nupalabdhira"pramāṇaṃ" pratiṣedhe sādhye "tena sarvvathā niṣedho'vācyaḥ" pratyakṣasya bhāvamātraviṣayatvāt | pramāṇāntarasya cābhāvāt | (89)

{2.90}

[2.90,0]

"etena tadviruddhārthakāryoktirupavarṇitā | prayogaḥ kevalaṃ bhinnaḥ sarvatrārtho na bhidyate || 90 ||"

[2.90,1]

"etena" svabhāva"ta"tkāraṇaviruddhopalabdhyoranupalabdhitvapratipādanena tayoḥ svabhāvatatkāraṇayorvviruddhārthasya "kāryoktirupavarṇṇi" boddhavyā | yathā nātra śītasparśo romaharṣavānvā puruṣo dhūmāditi | atrāpi niṣedhyānupalambhasya paraṃparayā pratipādanāt | upalakṣaṇañcaitad vyāpakaviruddhatatkāryopalabdhī api boddhavye | yathā nātra tuṣārasparśo vahnerdhūmāditi | etāsu svabhāvānupalabdhiviruddhopalabdhyādiṣu "prayogaḥ" śabdābhidhāvyāpāraḥ paramanupalambhopalambhapratipādakatvena bhidyate | "sarvvatrārtho" niṣedhyānupalambhalakṣaṇo "na bhi" tasyaiva sarvvatra pratipādyatvāt | (90)

{2.91}

[2.91,0]

"viruddhaṃ tacca sopāyamavidhāyāpidhāya ca | pramāṇoktirniṣedhe yā na sāmnāyānusāriṇī || 91 ||"

[2.91,1]

yā punardvividhenāpi virodhena viruddhamarthamabhidhā ya yaṃ kañcidarthamupadarśyate tanniṣedhyañca sahābhāvaniścayopāyena kāraṇavyāpakakāryānupalambhe vartamānama"vidhāyā"ta evā"pidhāya" ca pidhānamiva pidhānaṃ svarūpapratītivirodhitvādanupalambhaḥ | tamakṛtvā kāraṇādyanupalambhāpradarśanāttadupalambhasaṃbhāvanā na vyāhataiva | evaṃ niṣedhyopalambhasambhāvanāmanivāryānyavidhinā "niṣedhe" kartavye "pramāṇoktiryā " | (91)

{2.92}

[2.92,0]

"uktyādeḥ sarvavitpretyabhāvādipratiṣedhavat |"

[2.92,1]

"uktyāderhetoḥ | sarvvavidaḥ pretyabhāvasya" paralokasya "niṣedhavat" | yathā na sarvvajñatvamasya puruṣasya vaktṛtvāt pretyabhāvo puruṣatvādityādi |

[2.92,2]

kasmātpunariyaṃ viruddhoktireva netyāha |

[2.92,3]

"atīndriyāṇāmarthānāṃ virodhasyāprasiddhitaḥ || 92 ||"

[2.92,4]

"atīndriyāṇāṃ" sārvvajñaparalokādīnā"marthānāṃ" kenacit vaktṛtvādinā "virodhasyā" | jñānotkarṣāpakarṣayorvvacanāpakarṣotkarṣādarśanādviparyayadarśanācca | (92)

{2.93}

[2.93,0]

"bādhyabādhakabhāvaḥ kaḥ syātāṃ yadyuktisaṃvidau | tādṛśo'nupalabdheśced ucyatāṃ saiva sādhanam || 93 ||"

[2.93,1]

yadi co"ktisamvidau" saha "syātāṃ ka"stayoḥ parasparaṃ "bādhyabādhakabhāvaḥ" | na hi jñānavacanayorvvirodhaḥ siddhaḥ yenaikasatve'parasyābhāvaḥ | avirodhopi na siddha iticet satyaṃ kintu saṃśayepi na vaktṛtvamanaikāntikaṃ | "tādṛśaḥ" sarvvajñasya "vakturanupa"rabhāvaścet "ucyatāṃ" niṣedhe sādhye saivānupalabdhiḥ"sādhanaṃ" nātrānyasya śaktiḥ | (93)

{2.94}

[2.94,0]

"aniścayakaraṃ proktamīdṛk kvānupalambhanam | tannātyantaparokṣeṣu sadasattāviniścayau || 94 ||"

[2.94,1]

kintvīdṛgatīndriyārthaviṣaya"manupalambhanamaniścayakaraṃ proktaṃ" satyapyarthe sambhavāt | "tat" tasmā"vatyantaparokṣeṣu sadasattāniścayau na sataḥ" | satyapi pramāṇāvṛtteḥ | pramāṇanivṛttāvapyarthābhāvāsiddheḥ | tasmānnānupalabdheḥ kutaścidanyasmādabhāvasiddhiḥ | kintu viruddhādeva | (94)

{2.95}

[2.95,0]

"bhinno'bhinnopi vā dharmaḥ sa viruddhaḥ prayujyate | yathā'gnirahime sādhye sattā vā janmabādhanī || 95 ||"

[2.95,1]

"sa ca viruddho dharmaḥ" kvacid "bhinno vā prayujyate yathāgnirahime" himābhāve "sādhye" | "kvacidabhinno vā yathā sattā janmano bādhanī" mahadādīnāṃ janmābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ sattvāditi sattājanmanoścābhedaḥ sāṃkhyābhyupagamāducyate | na tu paramārthataḥ tādātmyaṃ viruddhayorasti | viruddhe ca sattājanmanī prāgasattayā hi abhivyaktirūpatāya lābho janmocyate | sattā tu vidyamānatā | tato yena rūpeṇa sattvaṃ na tena janma | yena ca janma tena na sattvamiti vyaktaḥ parasparaparihārasthitirvvirodhaḥ | (95)

{2.96}

[2.96,0]

"yathā vastveva vastūnāṃ sādhane sādhanaṃ matam | tathā vastveva vastūnāṃ svanivṛttau nivarttakam || 96 ||"

[2.96,1]

"yathā" ca "vastūnāṃ" sādhyānāṃ "sādhane sādhanaṃ vastveva mataṃ" nāvastu | "tathā vastveva " nāvastu | (96)

{2.97}

[2.97,0]

"etena kalpanānyasto yatra kvacana sambhavāt | dharmaḥ pakṣasapakṣānyataratvādirapoditaḥ || 97 ||"

[2.97,1]

"etena" vastunaḥ sādhanatvapratipādanena "vikalpanānyasto dharmaḥ pakṣasapakṣānyatara" | ādiśabdānmadupagamādiścā"poditaḥ" pratikṣipto boddhavyaḥ | tādṛśasya sādhanasya "yatra kvacana" sādhye "sambhavāt" | na hi pakṣatvaṃ sapakṣatvamvā jātiniyataṃ kintu vāñchādhīnamavastu | ataḥ samīhitasiddhau sarvva sarvvasya sidhyet | (97)

{2.98}

[2.98,0]

"tatrāpi vyāpako dharmo nivṛttergamako mataḥ | vyāpyasya svanivṛttiścet paricchinnā kathañcana || 98 ||"

[2.98,1]

"tatra vastunyapi vyāpako dharmaḥ" kāraṇaṃ svabhāvo vā | "vyāpyasya" kāryasya "svabhā"vasya "nivṛttergamako mataḥ" | vyāpakasya kāraṇasvabhāvasya svanivṛttiḥ "kathañcana" sākṣātparamparayā vā "paricchinnā" cet syāt | (98)

{2.99}

[2.99,0]

"yadapramāṇatābhāve liṅgaṃ tasyaiva kathyate | tadatyantavimūḍhārthaṃ;"

[2.99,1]

tathā yasyārthasya ekajñānasaṃsarggiṇo'"pramāṇatā" pramāṇanivṛttistasyaivā"bhāve"'bhāvavyavahāre ca sādhye sā pramāṇanivṛttiḥ svabhāvānupalambhākhyā "liṅgaṃ "bhāvānupalabdhiliṅgama"tyantavimūḍhārtha" | ye hyanupalabhyamānamapi dṛśyamasattayā mohānna vyavaharanti tān prati vyavahārasādhakaṃ talliṅgaṃ |

[2.99,2]

kasmātpunaramūḍhārthamapi tannetyāha |

[2.99,3]

"āgopālamasaṃvṛtteḥ || 99 ||"

[2.99,4]

"āgopālama"syārthasyā"saṃvṛtte"ragūḍhatvāt prasiddherityarthaḥ | (99)

{2.100}

[2.100,0]

"etāvanniścayaphalamabhāvenupalambhanam | tacca hetau svabhāve vā'dṛśye dṛśyatayā mate || 100 ||"

[2.100,1]

"etāva"ttrividham | kāraṇavyāpakasvabhā"vānupalambhanaṃ |" abhāve'bhāvavyavahāre ca "niścayaphalaṃ" | kāraṇaviruddhopalambhādayastu kāraṇādyanupalambhopalakṣaṇatvāt trividha evāntarbhūtāḥ | "taccā"bhāvaniścayaphalatvamanupalambhasya "hetau svabhāve ca" vyāpake niṣedhyarūpe ca "dṛśyatayā" darśanayogyatayā mate'"dṛśye"'nupalabhyamāne sati nānyathā |

[2.100,2]

tadevaṃ trividhaliṅgajamanumānaṃ pramāṇaṃ vastusamvādāt | tatastatprasiddhasyānityatāderna vastudharmateti sthitaṃ | (100)

{2.101}

[2.101,0]

nanvanityo'yaṃ varṇṇa iti svalakṣaṇe yojanā tatkathaṃ yojanādvarṇṇasāmānya(2 | 79) ityuktaṃ | atrāha |

[2.101,1]

"anumānādanityādergrahaṇe'yaṃ kramo mataḥ | prāmāṇyameva nānyatra gṛhītagrahaṇānmatam || 101 ||"

[2.101,2]

"anumānā"tparokṣasyā"nityāde"rdharmasya "grahaṇe" vastusāmānyamanityatvena gṛhyata ityayaṃ "kramo mataḥ" | varṇṇasāmānyañca pratyakṣataḥ siddhaṃ tadbalabhāvinā vikalpena vijātīyavyāvṛttyāśrayeṇa vyavasthāpanāt | yastu vinaśvaraṃ varṇṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā'nityo'yamiti viśeṣaviṣayaḥ anumānādanyatra | tatra "prāmāṇyameva na mataṃ gṛhīta" | (101)

{2.102}

[2.102,0]

kathaṃ gṛhītagrāhitvamityāha |

[2.102,1]

"nānyāsyānityatā bhāvāt pūrvasiddhaḥ sa caindriyāt | nānekarūpo vācyo'sau;"

[2.102,2]

"nānyā bhāvādvarṇṇāderanityatā" tasyaiva kṣaṇakṣayisvabhāvatvāt | "sa ca bhāva " | pūrvva vikalpāt | tatastameva yathāgṛhītaṃ vikalpayan vikalpo gṛhītagrāhī | yata eva nānyābhāvādanityatā | ata evābhāvo'sau dharmidharmarūpatayā "nānekarūpaḥ" | tathā na "vācyo'sau" śabdānāṃ dharmidharmābhāvasya tairvvacanāt | tasya ca vastunyasambhavāt |

[2.102,3]

kastarhi vācya ityāha |

[2.102,4]

"vācyo dharmo vikalpajaḥ || 102 ||"

[2.102,5]

"vikalpajo" vijātīyāśrayeṇa vikalpakalpito "dharmaḥ" parasparaṃ yathāsaṃketamasaṃkīrṇṇaḥ śabdānāṃ "vācyaḥ" | (102)

{2.103}

[2.103,0]

"sāmānyāśrayasaṃsiddhau sāmānyaṃ siddhameva tat | tadasiddhau tathāsyaiva hyanumānaṃ pravartate || 103 ||"

[2.103,1]

tasmātsāmānyasyānityāderāśrayasya varṇṇādeḥ pratyakṣāt "saṃsiddhau siddhameva " | yadi tvabhyāsādyabhāvādanurūpaniścayābhāvādajñānaṃ tadā pratyakṣā"ttadasiddhāvasyaiva" hi varṇṇādestathā nityatvena tadavyabhicārili"ṅgadanumānaṃ pravartate" | (103)

{2.104}

[2.104,0]

kasmātpunargṛhītepyaparijñānamityāha |

[2.104,1]

"kvacittadaparijñānaṃ sadṛśāparasambhavāt | bhrānterapaśyato bhedaṃ māyāgolakabhedavat || 104 ||"

[2.104,2]

"kvacida"nityatādau gṛhītepyanurūpaniścayābhāvāda"parijñānaṃ" | pūrvvakṣaṇavināśakāle tatsadṛśasyāparasya "sambhavāt" | bhāvaśūnyāntarā lakṣaṇābhāvāt | sa evāyamiti bhrānteḥ sthairyagrāhiṇyāḥ kṣaṇānāṃ "bhedama"'niścicanvataḥ puṃso dṛṣṭāntamāha | "māyāgolakabhedavat" | māyākāradarśitau golakau bhinnāvadhyakṣeṇa gṛhītvāpi sādṛśyāllāghavācca vipralabdhabuddhirekatvenādhyavasyati yathā tathā sthirādhyavasāyaḥ | (104)

{2.105}

[2.105,0]

nanu yadi kvacinnāśo dṛśyeṃta tadāsyāhetukasya svabhāvatvāt kṣaṇakṣayiṣu bhāveṣu ekatābuddherbhrāntatvaṃ bhavedityāha |

[2.105,1]

"tathā hyaliṅgamābālamasaṃśliṣṭottarodayam | paśyan paricchinattyeva dīpādiṃ nāśinaṃ janaḥ || 105 ||"

[2.105,2]

"tathā" hi "dīpādi" | ādiśabdātturaṅgadisantānavicchedakāle'"saṃśliṣṭottaro"dayamaghaṭita uttarasya udayo janma yasmin tamekasya svarasanirodhitve'parasya kāraṇābhāvāt | anutpattau "nāśinama"dhyakṣataḥ "paśyanna"liṅgaṅgamakaliṅgarahitamābālaṃ bālaparyantaṃ janaḥ "paricchinattyeva" | tataḥ prāgapi sataḥ svarasanirodhāt sadṛśāparāparakṣaṇapracaye sa evāyamiti buddhibhrāntireva | (105)

{2.106}

[2.106,0]

yathā |

[2.106,1]

"bhāvasvabhāvabhūtāyāmapi śaktau phale'dṛśaḥ | anānantaryato moho viniśceturapāṭavāt || 106 ||"

[2.106,2]

"bhāvasya"bījādeḥ "svabhāvabhūtāyāmapi" aṅkurādijanikāyāṃ "śaktau phale'ṅkurādau "'darśanāt "viniścetuḥ" punso'"pāṭavāt moho"'śaktabhramaḥ | tathā kṣaṇikeṣu bhāveṣu sadṛśāparāparotpatterbhāvaśūnyakṣaṇādarśanācca sthirabhramaḥ | (106)

{2.107}

[2.107,0]

"tasyaiva vinivṛtyarthamanumānopavarṇanam | vyavasyantīkṣaṇādeva sarvākārān mahādhiyaḥ || 107 ||"

[2.107,1]

tasyaikatvabhramasyaiva "nivṛttyartha" samvādiliṅgajasya kṣaṇikatā viṣayasyānu"mānasyopavarṇṇanaṃ" niścayāropamanasorbbādhyabādhakabhāvata (1 | 50) iti nyāyāt | ye tu"mahādhiyo" viparītavyavasāyānākrāntapratyakṣā yoginaste padārthasya "īkṣaṇādeva " niścinvanti | (107)

{2.108}

[2.108,0]

evañca |

[2.108,1]

"vyāvṛtte sarvatastasmin vyāvṛttivinibandhanāḥ | buddhayo'rthe pravarttante'bhinne bhinnāśrayā iva || 108 ||"

[2.108,2]

"tasminnarthe" vastuto'bhinne niraṃśe "sarvvataḥ" sajātīyād vijātīyācca "vyāvṛtte" yāvattyo vyāvṛttayaḥ santi tāvad "vyāvṛttivinibandhanā" niścayātmikā "buddhayo bhinnāśrayā " tattadvyāvṛttimātraviṣayatvena bhinnadharmidharmmādigocarā iva "pravartante" | (108)

{2.109}

[2.109,0]

"yathācodanamākhyāśca | so'sati bhrāntikāraṇe | pratibhāḥ pratisandhatte svānurūpāḥ svabhāvataḥ || 109 ||"

[2.109,1]

"yathāco" yathāsaṃketa"mākhyāḥ" śabdā"śca" pravartante | yatra vyāvṛttau yaḥ śabdo viniveśitaḥ | "sa" ca tasyāṃ niścitāyāṃ pravartate sa bhāvo'"sati bhrāntikāraṇe" yathābhyāsaṃ "svānurūpāḥ" svavyāvṛttisamucitāḥ "pratibhā" niścayabuddhīḥ "svabhāvataḥ prati""saṃdhatte" utpādayati | tasmādabhyāsavatāmīkṣaṇādevānityādiniścayaḥ anyeṣāntu sthirāropaṇārthamanumānamiti sthitametat | (109)

{2.110}

[2.110,0]

anye tvācāryāḥ prāhuḥ |

[2.110,1]

"siddho'trāpyathavā dhvaṃso liṅgādanupalambhanāt |"

[2.110,2]

"atra" varṇṇasantānavicchedakālepi santānavicchedalakṣaṇo dhvaṃso'nityatā na bhāvasvabhāvātmikā | sa "cānupalambhanālliṅgatsiddhaḥ" | nādhyakṣād bhāvaviṣayatvāttasya |

[2.110,3]

kasmātpunardhvaṃso'nityatā ityāha |

[2.110,4]

"prāg bhūtvā hyabhavadbhāvonitya ityabhidhīyate || 110 ||"

[2.110,5]

"prāg bhūtvā hi bhāvaḥ" paścāda"bhavannanitya ityabhidhīyate" na tu bhāva ityeva | tathā dhvaṃsa evānityatā sā cānupalabdhiliṅgajā'numānagamyā | (110)

{2.111}

[2.111,0]

nanu prāk paścādabhāvayorvyavadhāyakaḥ sattāsambandho'nityatā na pradhvaṃsābhāva ityāha |

[2.111,1]

"yasyobhayāntavyavadhisattāsambandhavācinī | anityatāśrutistena tāvantāviti kau smṛtau || 111 ||"

[2.111,2]

"yasya" nai yā yi kā deru"bhaya"sya prāk paścādabhāvasyā"nta"rasya yo "vyavadhā"yakaḥ sattā"sambandha"stadvācinyanityatā "śruti"riṣṭā "tena" vādinā "tāva"ntāviti kau"smṛtau" | (111)

{2.112}

[2.112,0]

"prāk paścādapyabhāvaścet sa evānityatā na kim | ṣaṣṭhyādyayogāditi ced antayoḥ sa kathaṃ bhavet || 112 ||"

[2.112,1]

"prāg"bhāvaḥ "paścādabhāvopi cet sa eva" prāgabhāvaḥ paścādabhāvo'"nityatā ki"nneṣyate | sattāviśeṣaṇatvenāpi tadabhyupagamasyeṣṭatvāt || paṭasya ghaṭe cābhāva iti "ṣaṣṭyā"divibhaktyayogāt pradhvaṃsābhāvo nānityatā | na hi bhāvābhāvayoḥ saṃyogādiḥ kaścitsambandhosti ya ucyeta ṣaṣṭyādibhiriti "cet evantarhyantayoḥ" sa ṣaṣṭyādiyogaḥ "kathaṃ bhavet" | abhāvayorvyavadhibhūtā sattetyādi | (112)

{2.113}

[2.113,0]

kiñca |

[2.113,1]

"sattāsambandhayordhrauvyādantābhyāṃ na viśeṣaṇam |"

[2.113,2]

"sattā tatsambandhe" paramate "dhrauvyādantābhyāṃ" prākpradhvaṃsābhāvābhyāṃ "na viśeṣaṇaṃ" syādantadvayaviśiṣṭā sattā tatsambandho veti | na hi niṃtyasya sarvakālavyāpino'ntasambhavaḥ |

[2.113,3]

"aviśeṣaṇameva syādantau cet kāryakāraṇe || 113 ||"

[2.113,4]

"kāryakāraṇe antā"vabhimate iti "cet" tadā tābhyāṃ sattāsa"mbandhayoraviśeṣaṇa" | (113)

{2.114}

[2.114,0]

"asambandhānna bhāvasya prāgabhāvaṃ sa vāṃchati || tadupādhisamākhyāne tepyasya ca na sidhyataḥ || 114 ||"

[2.114,1]

yasmāt sa nai yā yi kā dirbhāvasyā"sambandhāt prāga"bhāvaṃ sambandhinaṃ "na vāñchati" | tathā ca "tadupādhisamākhyāne" prāgabhāvaviśeṣaṇaṃ kāryakāraṇamiti samākhyānaṃ vyapadeśo yayoste tathā te kāryakāraṇe"pyasya na sidhyataḥ" | yasya hi prāgabhāvaḥ sa bhavan kāryaṃ syāt | na ca tatsambandho bhāvasyeti kāryābhāvaḥ | kāryābhāvācca kāraṇābhāvaḥ | tadutpādakasya kāraṇatvāt | (114)

{2.115}

[2.115,0]

kiñca |

[2.115,1]

"sattā svakāraṇaśleṣakaraṇāt kāraṇaṃ kila | sā sattā sa ca sambandho nityau kāryamatheha kim || 115 ||"

[2.115,2]

janma sattāśleṣaḥ "sattā"samavāyaḥ svakāraṇena samavāyinā saha nityaḥ | tayoḥ "karaṇāt kila" tvayeṣṭaṃ "kāraṇaṃ | sā ca sattā sa ca sambandho nityau" dvāvapi "kāryamatheha" dvayormadhye "kiṃ" yuktaṃ | (115)

{2.116}

[2.116,0]

api ca |

[2.116,1]

"yasyābhāvaḥ kriyetāsau na bhāvaḥ prāgabhāvavān | sambandhānabhyupagamānnityaṃ viśvamidaṃ tataḥ || 116 ||"

[2.116,2]

"yasyābhāvasyo"tpatteḥ prāgabhāvaḥ kāraṇairasau "kriyate | na" ca kaścid "bhāvaḥ "vānana"bhyupagamāt | tataḥ" kāryābhāvā"nnityaṃ viśvamidaṃ" prāptaṃ | (116)

{2.117}

[2.117,0]

kathantarhyabhāvena sambandhaḥ | na kathañcit | kintu buddhiparikalpita evāsāvityāha |

[2.117,1]

"tasmādanarthāskandinyo'bhinnārthābhimateṣvapi | śabdeṣu vācyabhedinyo vyatirekāspadaṃ dhiyaḥ || 117 ||"

[2.117,2]

yasmādvāstavasambandhābhyupagame doṣastasmād bhāvasya prāgabhāva itya"bhinnārtha"tvenābhimateṣvapi śabdād bhinnārthābhimateṣu ca bījasyāṅkura ityādiṣu "śabdeṣu dhiyo" kalpitasambandhaviṣayā "vācyabhedinyaḥ" | saṃketānurodhādupakalpitasambandhisambandhalakṣaṇavācyabhedavatyo "vyati"rekasya sambandhisambandhasyā"spadaṃ" nimittaṃbhavanti | alaṃ vāstavasambandhānubandhena doṣāśrayeṇa | (117)

{2.118}

[2.118,0]

tadevaṃ meyabahutvādvahutāpi cetyatra sānuṣaṅgaṃ prativihitaṃ | anekasya vṛtterekatra vā yathā viśeṣadṛṣṭenetyatrāha |

[2.118,1]

"viśeṣapratyabhijñānaṃ na pratikṣaṇabhedataḥ |"

[2.118,2]

agniṃ dṛṣṭvā krameṇa dhūmālliṅgāt tasyaiva "viśeṣa"sya sa evāyaṃ vahniriti "yatpratyabhijñānaṃ na" tatpramāṇaṃ | "pratikṣaṇaṃ" bhāvasya "bhedataḥ" ekārthasādhyārthakriyāyāḥ samvādābhāvāt |

[2.118,3]

syādetanna yathā dṛṣṭa eva viśeṣo gṛhyate kintu tatsāmānyamityāha |

[2.118,4]

"na vā viśeṣaviṣayaṃ dṛṣṭasāmyena tadgrahāt || 118 ||"

[2.118,5]

"na vā viśeṣaviṣayaṃ" tadviśeṣa"dṛṣṭa"manumānaṃ vaktavyaṃ prāgdṛṣṭasya viśeṣasya "sāmye"na tasyottarasya "grahaṇāt" | (118)

{2.119}

[2.119,0]

syādetadatra | yatra dṛṣṭāntadārṣṭāntikayorbhedastatra sāmānyato dṛṣṭamanumānaṃ iha tu |

[2.119,1]

"nidarśanaṃ tadeveti sāmānyāgrahaṇaṃ yadi | nidarśanatvāt siddhasya pramāṇenāsya kiṃ punaḥ || 119 ||"

[2.119,2]

"tadeva" dārṣṭāntikaṃ "nidarśanamiti sāmānyāgrahaṇaṃ" yadyucyate tadā "nidarśanatvā" niścitasyā"sya" dārṣṭāntikasya "pramāṇena kiṃ" kartavyaṃ | (119)

{2.120–2.121}

[2.120–2.121,0]

"vismṛtatvādadoṣaścet tata evānidarśanam || dṛṣṭe tadbhāvasiddhiścet pramāṇād;"

[2.120–2.121,1]

nāprasiddho dṛṣṭāntaḥ sa cet siddhaḥ kimanumānena gṛhītasyāpi"vismṛtatvāt" | punaranumānapratītāva"doṣaścet | tato" vismṛtatvā"devānidarśanaṃ" | na hi gṛhītavismṛtasya dṛṣṭāntatā | pūrvvapratyayena "dṛṣṭe"'rtha "pramāṇādvi"śeṣadṛṣṭānumānādya eva prāgdṛṣṭaḥ sa evāyamiti "tadbhāva"sya pūrvvasya "siddhiścedi"ṣyate |

[2.120–2.121,2]

nanvayaṃ tadbhāvaḥ kimanyavastuni sādhyate uta tatraiva |

[2.120–2.121,3]

"anyavastuni || 120 ||"

[2.120–2.121,4]

"tattvārope viparyāsastatsiddharepramāṇatā | pratyakṣetarayoraikyādekasiddhirdvayorapi || 121 ||"

[2.120–2.121,5]

tatrānyavastuni (120) vartamāne "tattva"syātītavastvātmaka"syārope" svīkriyamāṇe "viparyāso"'yathārthatvaṃ syāt | na hyanyasyānyātmatvamasti tadaśakyaprāpaṇamupadarśayadapramāṇaṃ syāt | atha tatraiva tadbhāvasiddhiriti dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ | tadā "tatsiddhe"rekasiddhervviśeṣadṛṣṭasyānumānasyā"pramāṇatā" gṛhītagrāhitvāt | na hyekasya nirbhāgasya kiñcidagṛhītaṃ nāma | tathā hi "pratyakṣetarayo"radhyakṣānumānaviṣayayaurai"kyāt dvayorapi" pratyakṣe'numāne ca "ekasyārthasya siddhiḥ" | (121)

{2.122}

[2.122,0]

tataśca dṛṣṭāntagrāhiṇaivābhraṣṭasmṛtisaṃskāreṇa pratyakṣeṇa siddhatvāt viphalamanumānaṃ | pratyakṣasaṃskārabhraṃśe tu nādṛṣṭāntamanumānamasti | tasmād |

[2.122,1]

"sandhīyamānaṃ cānyena vyavasāyaṃ smṛtiṃ viduḥ | talliṅgāpekṣaṇānno cet smṛtirna vyabhicārataḥ || 122 ||"

[2.122,2]

anyenātītadarśanena ekaviṣayatayā "sandhīya mānaṃ" ghaṭyamānaṃ paraṃ "vyavasāyaṃ""smṛtiṃ vidu"rvvidvāṃsaḥ | gṛhītārthavikalpena smṛtitvaṃ taccehāvikalaṃ | tasya pratipattavyasya cihnamavyabhicāri "liṅgaṃ" nta"dapekṣaṇānnoce"dviśeṣadṛṣṭamanumānaṃ "smṛtiḥ" sā tu liṅganirapekṣyā | naitadyuktaṃ"vyabhicāra taḥ" | tathā hi yadi liṅgantrirūpantadā vyāptigrahaṇaviṣayatvenaiva tatsiddhervyarthamanumānaṃ | atha na trirūpantadā nāvya bhicāraniścayaḥ | tasmādviśeṣadṛṣṭasyāpramāṇatvādekatrānekavṛtterapi tryekasaṃkhyāpohanābhāvo nirastaḥ | tasmātsthitametanmānaṃ dvividhaṃ meyadvaividhyāditi || (122) ||

{ii.v}

<5. pratyakṣacintā>

<(1) pratyakṣalakṣaṇavipratipattinirāsaḥ>

<ka. kalpanāpoḍhaṃ pratyakṣam>

{2.123}

[2.123,0]

idānīmavasaraprāptāṃ pratyakṣasya lakṣaṇavipratipattiṃ nirākarttumāha |

[2.123,1]

"pratyakṣaṃ kalpanāpoḍhaṃ pratyakṣeṇaiva sidhyati | pratyātmavedyaḥ sarveṣāṃ vikalpo nāmasaṃśrayaḥ || 123 ||"

[2.123,2]

yatta"tpratyakṣa"miti prasiddhaṃtat "kalpanāyā apoḍhaṃ" draṣṭavyaṃ kalpanārtharahitamityarthaḥ | taccaitadīdṛśaṃ "pratyakṣeṇaiva" svasamvedanenaiva "sidhyati" | kalpanārahitasyārthasya rūpasya samvedanasyāparokṣatvāt | yadi tu kalpanāsvabhāvatvamasya syāttathaiva prakāśeta | vikalpasyāparokṣatvāt | tathā hi "pratyātmavedyaḥ sarvveṣāṃ" prāṇināṃ "vikalpo nāma" śabdasaṃsargavān | sa yadi syādupalabhya eva bhavet | (123)

{2.124}

[2.124,0]

tasmāt |

[2.124,1]

"saṃhṛtya sarvataścintāṃ stimitenāntarātmanā | sthitopi cakṣuṣā rūpamīkṣate sākṣajā matiḥ || 124 ||"

[2.124,2]

"saṃhṛtyā"kṛṣya "sarvvato" vikalpanīyā"ccintāṃ stimitena" sarvvāvikalpavigamāt adhikṣiptenā"ntarātmanā" cetasā "sthito'pi" puruṣa"ścakṣu"rvvijñānena "rūpa"jā nirvvikalpā "matiḥ" sarva samviditaiva | (124)

{2.125}

[2.125,0]

santyevendriyadhiyaḥ kalpanāstāstu nopalabhyanta ityapyasat | tathā hi |

[2.125,1]

"punarvikalpayan kiñcidāsīnme kalpanedṛśī | vetti ceti na pūrvvoktāvasthāyāmindriyād gatau || 125 ||"

[2.125,2]

vikalpāvasthāyā ūrdhvaṃ "punarvvikalpayan" pumānā"sīnme kalpanedṛśīti" veti "nendri"tpannāyāṃ "gatau" buddhau saṃhṛtyetyādinā "pūrvvamuktāvasthā" yasyāstasyāḥ kalpanāṃ veti | yadi sā tatra syādatatsaṃskārasya smṛtirjāyate | tasmānnāstīti niścīyate | (125)

{2.126}

[2.126,0]

kiñca | vācyavācakākārasaṃsargavatī pratītiḥ kalpanā | na cendriyaviṣaye'nanvayāt saṃketā'sambhavācca śabdayojanāsti | tathāhi |

[2.126,1]

"ekatra dṛṣṭo bhedo hi kvacinnānyatra dṛśyate || na tasmād bhinnamastyanyat sāmānyaṃ buddhayabhedataḥ || 126 ||"

[2.126,2]

"ekatra" deśādau "na dṛśyate" na cānanuyāyini śabdasaṃketaḥ | sāmānyamanuyāyīti cet | "tasmā"d bhedādanyad "bhinnaṃ sāmānyaṃ nāsti buddherabhedataḥ" | (126)

{2.127}

[2.127,0]

yadi hi sāmānyaṃ sāmānyaṃ syāt dvyākārā buddhirbhavet | viśeṣamātrākāraiva tu pratyakṣabuddhirupalabhyate |

[2.127,1]

"tasmād viśeṣaviṣayā sarvaivendriyajā matiḥ || na viśeṣeṣu śabdānāṃ pravṛttāvasti sambhavaḥ || 127 ||"

[2.127,2]

"tasmātsarvvaivendriyajā matirvviśeṣa"mātra"viṣayā"'nyasyānupalabdheḥ | "na ca viśeṣeṣu " (127)

{2.128}

[2.128,0]

"ananvayād viśeṣāṇāṃ saṅketasyāpravṛttitaḥ || viṣayo yaśca śabdānāṃ saṃyojyeta sa eva taiḥ || 128 ||"

[2.128,1]

"viśeṣāṇāmananvayāt" tatra "saṃketasyā" | uttarakālaṃ śabdārthapratipattyarthaṃ saṃketakriyā | na ca viśeṣāḥ kālāntaramanuvartante | tasmādya eva "śabdānāṃ viṣayo"vyavacchedaḥ "sa eva taiḥ saṃyojyeta" | na svalakṣaṇaṃ || (128)

{2.129}

[2.129,0]

"asyedamiti sambandhe yāvarthau pratibhāsinautayoreva hi sambandho na tadendriyagocaraḥ || 129 ||"

[2.129,1]

tasmādasyā"rthasyeda"mvācaka"miti sambandhe" vācyavācakabhāvalakṣaṇe "yāvarthau prati" vaktavyaḥ | yadā cārthandṛṣṭvā saketaṃ tatra pravartayati | "tadendriyagocaro'rtho" nāsti | (129)

{2.130}

[2.130,0]

"viśadapratibhāsasya tadārthasyāvibhāvanāt | vijñānābhāsabhedaśca padārthānāṃ viśeṣakaḥ || 130 ||"

[2.130,1]

saṃhṛtendriyavyāpārasya tadā saṃketasaṃkalpakāle "viśadaprati" | yadi tatrārthaḥ pratibhāti tadendriyajñānavat sphuṭaḥ pratīyate | na ca pratibhāsabhedepi śabdendriyajñānayorekaviṣayatvaṃ yasmā"dvijñāna"syā"bhāsabheda" ākārabhedaḥ "padārthānāṃ" grāhyānāṃ "viśeṣako" bhedakaḥ | yadi tu pratibhāsabhedepyarthābhedastadā viśvamekaṃ dravyaṃ syāt || (130)

{2.131}

[2.131,0]

syādetat | yadā svalakṣaṇamupadarśya śabdo niveśyate tadā svalakṣaṇameva vācyavācakamityāha |

[2.131,1]

"cakṣuṣā'rthāvabhāse'pi yaṃ paro'syeti śaṃsati | sa eva yojyate śabdairna khalvindriyagocaraḥ || 131 ||"

[2.131,2]

"cakṣuṣārthavabhāse" jāte tathā śrotrācchābdāvabhāsepi yamarthamanyavyavacchedaṃ buddhiparivarttinaṃ paraḥ pratipādako'syārthasyāyaṃ vācaka iti "śaṃsati" kathayati "sa evā"nyavyavacchedaḥ "śabdairyojyate na khalvindriyagocaraḥ" svalakṣaṇamananvayāttasya | taddarśanāntaraṃ saṃketasaṃkalpe ca vināśācca | (131)

{2.132}

[2.132,0]

"avyāpṛtendriyasyānyavāṅgamātreṇāvibhāvanāt |"

[2.132,1]

"tathā'vyāpṛtendriyasyānyavāṅmātreṇa" svalakṣaṇā"vibhāvanāt" pratyakṣa iva |

[2.132,2]

syādetat | saṃketāviṣayatvepi śabdasaṃsṛṣṭameva svalakṣaṇamadhyakṣaṃ prakṛtyā pratyeṣyatītyāha |

[2.132,3]

"na cānuditasaṃbandhaḥ svayaṃ jñānaprasaṅgataḥ || 132 ||"

[2.132,4]

"na cānuditasambandho" vācyavācakabhāvo yasya sa śabdaḥ pratyāyako dṛṣṭa iti śeṣaḥ | tathābhyupagame tu "svayaṃ" saṃketamanapekṣyaiva śrutācchabdādarthasya "jñāna" | (132)

{2.133}

[2.133,0]

nanvindriyavyāpārasamakālamahirahiriti dhārāvāhisavikalpakamadhyakṣaṃ pravartate | yadi tu tatra vikalpakamavikalpakañca dvayamiṣyate tadā vikalpena nirvvikalpasya vyavadhānād darśanaṃ vicchinnaṃ syāt | na caitadasti | na yugapajjñānasambhavaḥ | atrāha |

[2.133,1]

"manaso yugapadvṛtteḥ savikalpāvikalpayoḥvimūḍho laghuvṛttervvā tayoraikyaṃ vyavasyati || 133 ||"

[2.133,2]

"manasoḥ savikalpāvikalpayo"rekasmātsamanantarā"dyugapad vṛtteḥ" kāraṇāttayoraikyaṃ "vimūḍhaḥ" pratipattā vyavasyati | nirvvikalpakaṃ hi svalakṣaṇaviṣayaṃ vikalpaśca vastuto'tadviṣayatvepyavasāyānurodhāttadviṣayaḥ | sahotpattiścānubhavasiddhatvāt durapahnavā | tataḥ sahotpannayorekaviṣayayoraikyabhrama eṣaḥ | parābhimatāyāṃ yugapadanutpattāvapi savikalpāvikalpayorlaghuvṛtteḥ śīghra"vṛtte"rvvā kāraṇāt "tayormū"ḍhamatiḥ pratipattā "aikyaṃ " alātabhrāntau cakramiva | (133)

{2.134}

[2.134,0]

yadi darśanamavikalpaṃ tadanantarantu vikalpaḥ punastadanantaraṃ darśanaṃ tadā |

[2.134,1]

"vikalpavyavadhānena vicchinnaṃ darśanambhavet | iti ced bhinnajātīyavikalpenyasya vā katham || 134 ||"

[2.134,2]

"vikalpena" vyavadhānā"dvicchinnaṃ darśanaṃ bhavet" | na dhārāvāhīti cet | "nanvasya" parasyāpi gāṃ paśyato nirvvikalpena pratyakṣeṇa bhinnajātīyasyāśvādervvikalpe jāyamāne darśanaṃ kathamavicchinnaṃ | na hyaśvavācakaśabdena saṃyojya gaurgṛhyate | yenaikameva savikalpaṃ tadadhyakṣaṃ bhavet | ekatve vāśvapratītirna syāt | goviṣayatvāttasya | (134)

{2.135}

[2.135,0]

syādetat |

[2.135,1]

"alātadṛṣṭivad bhāvapakṣaśced balavān mataḥ | anyatrāpi samānaṃ tad varṇayorvvā sakṛcchṛ tiḥ || 135 ||"

[2.135,2]

alātasya bhramyamānasya nānādeśeṣu lāghavād bhāvapakṣabalavatvācca darśanapratisandhānena cakradṛ"ṣṭivat" vijātīyavyavakīryamāṇasya darśanasyāntarā abhāvepi"bhāvapakṣo balavān mata" iti darśanāvicchedabuddhirati "cet | anyatrābhāvapakṣepi" tadbalavattve lāghavasāmarthyāt "samānaṃ" | tato darśanavicchedalāghavādvicchedadhīrevāstu | saro rasa ityādau "varṇṇayo"rvā lāghavā"tsakṛtśrutiḥ" prāptā || (135)

{2.136}

<kha. paramatadūṣaṇam>

[2.136,0]

kiñca |

[2.136,1]

"sakṛt saṅgataśabdārtheṣvindriyeṣviha satsvapi | pañcabhirvyavadhānepi bhātyavyavahiteva yā || 136 ||"

[2.136,2]

"sakṛt" yugapa"tsaṃgatāḥ" svasvagocarībhūtāḥ sarvve'"rthā" yeṣu te"ṣvindriyeṣu" cakṣurādiṣu manaḥparyanteṣu "satsvapīha" saṅkrāntakāntāvadanapratibimbasya sahakārasugandhinaḥ śītasya bhramadbhramaropagītasya svādruno madhunaḥ sārvvaguṇānubhavakāle prasaratsaṃkalpajanmanāṃ yūnāṃ yā matiḥ "pañcabhi"rindriyabuddhi"bhirvyavadhānepi" tvatpakṣe"'vyava"hiteva samakāleva "bhāti" | (136)

{2.137}

[2.137,0]

"sā matirnāmaparyantakṣaṇikajñānamiśraṇāt | vicchinnābheti taccitraṃ tasmāt santu sakṛddhiyaḥ || 137 ||"

[2.137,1]

"sendriyamatirnāmnaḥ" śabdasya "paryanto" varṇṇastasya "kṣaṇikaṃ jñānaṃ" tena "miśraṇāt" saro rasa ityādiṣvavicchinnā prāpnoti | vijātīyavijñānāntarāvyavadhānāt | tathāpi "vicchinnābhā" kramavatī | yattu "citramā"ścaryaṃ yadi lāghavakṛtaḥ sakṛdgrahābhimānaḥ tadā varṇṇajñāne sa nitarāṃ yukto vijātīyāvyavadhānāt | indriyajñāneṣu tu na yuktaḥ pañcabhirvyavadhānāt | tasmā"tsakṛddhiyaḥ santu" yathoktaṃ manaso yugapadvṛtteri (2 | 133) ti || (137)

{2.138}

[2.138,0]

anyathā |

[2.138,1]

"pratibhāsāviśeṣaśca sāntarānantare katham | śuddhe manovikalpe ca na kramagrahaṇambhavet || 138 ||"

[2.138,2]

"sāntare" pañcabhirindriyajñānairvyavahitatvāt | "anantare" saro rasa ityādike jñāne vijātīyāvyavadhānāt "pratibhāsa"syā"viśeṣa"ścāprasaktaḥ | sa cānubhavabādhitatvāt "kathama"bhyupagama iti śeṣaḥ | yadi laghuvṛttitvāt sakṛdgrahastadā "śu" vijātīyāvyavakīrṇṇe "manovikalpe ca" prābandhike "kramagrahaṇamanu"bhavasiddhaṃ na "bhavet" | (138)

{2.139}

[2.139,0]

"yo'grahaḥ saṅgatepyarthe kvacidāsaktacetasaḥ |"

[2.139,1]

nanu yadi yugapat jñānotpattistadaikatrāsaktaṃ punarutpattidharmakaṃ ceto yasya tasyā"saktacetasaḥ kvacidarthe" svendriyeṇa "saṅgatepi" yo'graho vijñānānutpattiḥ sa kathaṃ |

[2.139,2]

āha |

[2.139,3]

"saktyā notpattivaiguṇyāccodyaṃ vai taddvayorapi || 139 ||"

[2.139,4]

ekatra "saktyā" viṣayāsañcāralakṣaṇayā'nyasya bhinnaviṣayasya jñānasyo"tpatti" | aviguṇo hi samanantarapratyayaḥ svakāryamārabhate | na tvāsaktiviguṇaḥ | "yaccaitaccodyaṃ" parihṛtamasmābhistad "dvayorapi" samānaṃ yugapadvijñānānutpattivādinopi mate sarvvatrevaindriyasaṃgame samāne kvacideva "jñānaṃ kvacinneti" kutaḥ | (139)

{2.140}

[2.140,0]

tatrāsaktivaiguṇyameva manasa uttaraṃ tacca samānamasmākamalātadṛṣṭivaditi dṛṣṭāntasyāsiddhimāha |

[2.140,1]

"śīghravṛtteralātāderanvayapratidhātinī | cakrabhrāntiṃ dṛgādhatte na dṛśāṃ ghaṭanena sā || 140 ||"

[2.140,2]

"śīghrā" pra"vṛttirbhra"maṇaṃ yasyā"lātā"desta"syā" upahatatvaṃ tadvatī dṛg dṛṣṭi"ścakrā"kārāṃ "bhrānti"mindriyajāṃ "dhatte | na dṛśāṃ" bhinnabhinnadeśālātadarśanānāṃ "ghaṭanena" yojanayā "sā" mānasī bhrāntiḥ sphuṭapratibhāsatvāt | "mānasasya" na viparyayāt | tasmādahirahiriti vikalpasamakālamadhyakṣaṃ vastu sphuṭamavaiti na tu vikalpa iti sthitaṃ | (140)

{2.141}

[2.141,0]

"kecidindriyajatvāderbāladhīvadakalpanām | āhurbālāvikalpe ca hetuṃ saṅketamandatām || 141 ||"

[2.141,1]

"keci"dācāryīyāḥ śa ṅka ra svā mi prabhṛtayaḥ "indriyajatvā"dādiśabdādamānasatvānubhavākārapravṛttattvāderhetoḥ pratyakṣabuddhi"makalpanāṃ bāladhīvadāhuḥ" | dṛṣṭāntasiddhayarthaṃ | bālasyā"vikalpe" vikalpābhāve ca "saṃketamaṃdatāṃ" hetumāhuḥ | vācyavācakayojanā hi vikalpaḥ | sā ca saṃketapūrvvikā tadabhāvād bālasya kalpanābhāvaḥ | (141)

{2.142}

[2.142,0]

"teṣāṃ pratyakṣameva syād bālānāmavikalpanāt | saṅketopāyavigamāt paścādapi bhavenna saḥ || 142 ||"

[2.142,1]

"teṣāmevaṃ" vādināṃ mate "bālānāṃ pratyakṣameva" jñānaṃ "syānna" vicārakaṃ | kiṃ kāraṇamavikalpanāt | bhavatu ko doṣa iti cet | āha "saṃketopāyasya" vicārasya "viga"bālānāṃ "paścādapi" sa saṅketo "na bhavet" | tadabhāvādvikalpābhāvaśca | (142)

{2.143}

[2.143,0]

"mano vyutpannasaṅketamasti tena sa cenmataḥ | evamindriyajepi syād śeṣavaccedamīdṛśam || 143 ||"

[2.143,1]

janmāntarāgataṃ "vyutpannaṃ saṃketaṃ manosti" bālānāṃ "tena" saṃketaḥ teṣāṃ mataścet | "evaṃ" satī"ndriyajepi" jñāne "syāt" kalpanā tannivartakahetvabhidhānāt tato dṛṣṭāsiddhireva | "ida"mindriyajatvādi "īdṛśaṃ" niṣedhyena sahāsiddhavirodhaṃ | śeṣavaccoktaṃ | (143)

{2.144}

[2.144,0]

athānyena liṅgenāvyabhicāriṇā bālajñānamavikalpanaṃ prasādhya dṛṣṭāntīkriyate tadā |

[2.144,1]

[2.144,2]

"yadevā"vyabhicāri "bāle" bālasyendriyajñāne "sādhanaṃ tadevātra" vyutpannasaṃketānāmindriyajñānepi "kathyatāṃ" kimindrijatvādinopanyastena | vyutpannāvyutpannayo"rakṣa"śabdasaṃsṛṣṭatvamātrānukaraṇena "sāmyāt | anene"ndriyajatvadūṣaṇenā"nubhava" ādiryasya mānasattvādestaduktaṃ doṣavattayā boddhavyaṃ | (144)

{2.145}

<(2) sāmānyanirāsaḥ>

<ka. varṇasaṃsthānarāhityādasiddhiḥ>

[2.145,0]

avikalpasiddhau paramataṃ dūṣayitvā svayaṃ upapattyantaramāha |

[2.145,1]

"viśeṣaṇaṃ viśeṣyañca sambandhaṃ laukikīṃ sthitim | gṛhītvā saṅkalayyaitat tathā pratyeti nānyathā || 145 ||"

[2.145,2]

"viśeṣaṇaṃ" vyavacchedakaṃ "viśeṣyaṃ" vyavacchedyaṃ tayoḥ "sambandhaṃ" yathāsambhavaṃ samavāyādikaṃ "laukikīṃ" lokaprasiddhāṃ "sthitiṃ" vyavasthāñca jātyādikaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ viśeṣyaṃ dravyādi viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyaśabdayośca pūrvvāparaniyama iti pṛthak pratyekaṃ svarūpeṇa "gṛhītvā" tadanantara"metat" sarvva "saṅkalayya" saṃyojya "tathā" viśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭatvena "pratyeti" viśiṣṭabuddhi"rnānyathā" | viśeṣaṇādyagrahaṇe | (145)

{2.146}

[2.146,0]

"yathā daṇḍini | jātyādervvivekenānirūpaṇāt | tadvatā yojanā nāsti kalpanāpyatra nāstyataḥ || 146 ||"

[2.146,1]

"yathā daṇḍini" daṇḍīti viśiṣṭabuddhiḥ daṇḍapuruṣatatsambandhādigrahaṇapūrvvikā tadagrahe ca na bhavati | jātirādiryasya guṇakarmādeḥ "svarūpasya " jātimatā "yojanā" viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvo "nāsti | ato" yojanāvirahāt "atra" jātimadādau "kalpanāpi nāstīti" tasmājjātyādiyojanātmikā kalpanā nāsti | śabdayojanātmikā tu "sambhāvyeta" | sāpi svalakṣaṇe saṃketābhāvānnirastā prāk || (146)

{2.147}

[2.147,0]

nanu yadi sāmānyābhāvastadā vibhinnāsu vyaktiṣu kathamanvayipratyaya ityāha |

[2.147,1]

"yadapyanvayivijñānaṃ śabdavyaktyavabhāsi tat |"

[2.147,2]

"yadapyanvayivijñānamu"tpadyate, tacca "śabda"sya gaurityāde"rvyakte"śca varṇṇasaṃsthānaviśeṣasya ābhāsa ākārastadvatpratīyate na jātyābhāsavat |

[2.147,3]

kiṃ punaḥ sāmānyābhāsameva netyāha |

[2.147,4]

"varṇṇākṛtyakṣarākāraśūnyaṃ gotvaṃ hi varṇṇyate || 147 ||"

[2.147,5]

"varṇṇo" nīlādirā"kṛtiḥ" saṃsthāna"makṣaraṃ" gavādiśabdaḥ | teṣāmākāro yathā pratītaḥ tena "śūnyaṃ gotvaṃ hi" sāmānyavādibhi"rvvarṇyate" (147)

{2.148}

[2.148,0]

ato'nvayivijñāne yadvarṇṇasaṃsthānādi pratibhāsate na tatsāmānyaṃ |

[2.148,1]

"samānatvepi tasyaiva nekṣaṇaṃ netragocare | pratibhāsadvayābhāvāt buddhe rbhedaśca durlabhaḥ || 148 ||"

[2.148,2]

"tasyaiva samānatve" vā svīkriyamāṇe "netragoca"re'rthe nāṅgīkartavyamīkṣaṇaṃ | vikalpapratibhāsinaḥ "pratibhāsadvayasya" sphuṭāsphuṭavarṇṇasaṃsthānavato"'bhāvāt" | ekākārameva jñānaṃ yadyubhayābhāsamaṅgīkriyate tadā "buddhe"rbhedaḥ pratyakṣatvāpratyakṣatvādinā durlabhaḥ | yadapi spaṣṭapratibhāsamadhyakṣaṃ tadapyanakṣajaṃ syāt | aspaṣṭapratibhāsatvāt | evamanakṣajamadhyakṣaṃ syāt | spaṣṭapratibhāsatvāt | tasmādadṛṣṭena sāmānyādinā na yojayatītyakalpanamadhyakṣaṃ | (148)

{2.149}

<kha. samavāyasyātīndriyatvādasiddhiḥ>

[2.149,0]

kiñca |

[2.149,1]

"samavāyāgrahādakṣaiḥ sambandhādarśanaṃ sthitam |"

[2.149,2]

"samavāya"syātīndriyasyā"grahādakṣai"rakṣabhavairvvijñānairjātitadvatoḥ "sambandha"syāviśiṣṭapratītyā"'darśanaṃ sthitaṃ" niścitaṃ yadbalena yatpratītistadagrahe na yuktā sā |

[2.149,3]

yadi nāsti samavāyastadeha tantuṣu paṭa ityādayo buddhayo na syurityāha |

[2.149,4]

"paṭastantuṣvihetyādiśabdāśceme svayaṃ kṛtāḥ || 149 ||"

[2.149,5]

iha "tantuṣu paṭa ityādi śabdāḥ" samayānulocanaiḥ "kṛtā" na vastuparādhīnāḥ | (149)

{2.150}

[2.150,0]

tathā hi |

[2.150,1]

"śṛṅgaṃ gavīti loke syāt śṛṅge gaurityalaukikam |"

[2.150,2]

"śṛṅgaṃ gavi" tiṣṭa"tīti loke syāt" pramāṇaprasiddhyoranurodhāt | "śṛṅge gauriti " tadupakalpita"malaukikaṃ" pramāṇaprasiddhibahirbhāvāt |

<(3) avayavinirāsaḥ>

[2.150,3]

yadyavayavebhyo na gaurbhinnastadā gavi śṛṅgamityapi na syādityāha |

[2.150,4]

"gavākhyapariśiṣṭāṅgavicchedānupalambhanāt || 150 ||"

[2.150,5]

śṛṅgasya "gavākhyaiḥ pariśiṣṭāṅgairvvicchedesya" viyogasyā"nupalambhanāt" śṛṅgaṃ gavītyucyate na tvavayavātiriktagosadbhāvāt | (150)

{2.151}

[2.151,0]

nanu tantuṣu paṭa iti bhavatyeva pratītiriti cet | āha |

[2.151,1]

"taistantubhiriyaṃ śāṭītyuttaraṃ kāryamucyate | tantusaṃskārasambhūtaṃ naikakālaṃ kathañcana || 151 ||"

[2.151,2]

"taistantubhiḥ" paṭāvasthāprāgbhāvibhi"riyaṃ śāṭīti" kāraṇabhūtatantūttarakālabhāvi"tantū"nāṃ "saṃskāra"sturīvemakuvindakarādisahakārī prabhavāvasthāviśeṣalābhaḥ | tasmātsvarasena nirudhyamānātsaṃ"bhūtaṃkāryamucyate" | na tu tantubhiḥ sahai"kakālaṃ" kāryaṃ tantupaṭa iti "kathañcana kathyate" kāryakāraṇayoḥ samakālatvābhāvāt | (151)

{2.152}

[2.152,0]

yadi nāsti tantupaṭayorbhedastadā kathamete tantavaḥ paṭaścāyamiti vyapadeśa ityāha |

[2.152,1]

"kāraṇāropataḥ kaścit ekāpoddhāratopi vā | tantvākhyāṃ varttayet kārye darśayan nāśrayaṃ śruteḥ || 152 ||"

[2.152,2]

"kāraṇā"nāntantūnāmā"ropataḥ" | "eka"sya tantora"poddhārato" buddhyā niḥkarṣaṇāt vā "kaścid" vyavaharttā kārye paṭe "tantvākhyāṃ" tantuśrutiṃ "vartayet" | paṭaśruterāśrayaṃ kāraṇaṃ "darśayen na" tantubhyo vyatiriktaḥ "paṭosti" evamākārapariṇatāstantavaḥ paṭa ityarthaḥ | (152)

{2.153}

[2.153,0]

yadi tantavaḥ kevalā na tebhyaḥ paṭo'nyastadā paṭavyapadeśo nirnibandhanaḥ syādityāha |

[2.153,1]

"upakāryopakāritvaṃ vicchedād dṛṣṭireva vā |"

[2.153,2]

tantūnāṃ parasparaṃ śītādyapanodakṣamaṃ sāhitya"mupakāryopakāritvaṃ" | anyonyasya "vicchedād dṛṣṭireva vā" paṭavyapadeśanibandhanamiti śeṣaḥ ||

[2.153,3]

yadi vyatiriktaṃ vyapadeśanibandhanaṃ nāsti tadā paṭa iti vyapadeśo na mukhyaḥ syāt | bā hī ke govyapadeśavadityāha |

[2.153,4]

"mukhyaṃ yadaskhalajjñānamādisaṃketagocaraḥ || 153 ||"

[2.153,5]

"mukhya"ntaducyate "yadādisaṃketa"sya "gocaro" na vyatirikta ityeva parasparāvicchedāvastheṣu ca paṭaśruteḥ saṃketā"daskhala"dgatigocaratvānmukhyatvaṃ | tasmātpratyakṣato jāteranupalambhādyojanāvirahaḥ | (153)

{2.154}

<(4) nānumānataḥ sāmānyasiddhiḥ>

[2.154,0]

syādetat | viśiṣṭapratītirvviśeṣaṇapratītipūrvvikā yathā daṇḍipratītiḥ | viśiṣṭapratītiśca śāvaleyādiṣu gauriti viśeṣaṇañca śāvaleyādiṣu gotvamevetyanumānato jātisiddhirityāha |

[2.154,1]

"anumānañca jātyādau vastuno nāsti bhedini |"

[2.154,2]

"anumānaṃ vastunaḥ" śābaleyāde"rbhedini jātyādau nāsti" | na hi vyaktivyatiriktaṃ viśeṣaṇamupalabhyate śṛṅgādyavayavasanniveśa eva tvabhinno viśeṣaṇamastu | tathā ca nābhimatasiddhiḥ |

[2.154,3]

dṛṣṭāntāsiddhimapyāha |

[2.154,4]

"sarvvatra vyapadeśo hi daṇḍāderapi sāṃvṛtāt || 154 ||"

[2.154,5]

"sarvvatra puruṣādau" daṇḍītyādi"vyapadeśo"pi "hi" na "daṇḍāde"rvvastunaḥ kintu "sāṃvṛtāt" | daṇḍasvalakṣaṇasya vyupadeśe hetutve sarvvatra puruṣe syāt | sambandhinyevānyatreti cet | tarhi sambandho daṇḍaḥ kāraṇaṃ daṇḍi vyapadeśasya sambandhaśca saṃyogādirnāstīti paraṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ pariśiṣyate | tasya nimittatve yathā daṇḍī puruṣastathā puruṣī daṇḍa ityapi syāt | samānatvānnimittasya | tasmāt kalpitaviśeṣaṇabhāvaniyamo daṇḍaḥ sambandhī sāṃvṛta eva viśeṣaṇaṃ | (154)

{2.155}

[2.155,0]

kiñca |

[2.155,1]

"vastuprāsādamālādiśabdāścānyānapekṣiṇaḥ | geho yadyapi saṃyogastanmālā kintu tadbhavet || 155 ||"

[2.155,2]

ṣaṭsu padārtheṣu "vastu" vastviti sarvvānuyāyī śabdaḥ prāsādeṣu "prāsādamāle"ti śabdo gṛheṣu bahuṣu nagaramityā"diśabdāścānyānapekṣiṇo"'rthāntarabhūtaviśeṣaṇarahitā iti vyabhicāritā hetoḥ | na hi padārtheṣu vyatiriktaṃ sāmānyaṃ vastutātvamabhyupagamyate vai śe ṣi kaiḥ | na ca prāsādo dravyaṃ vijātīyānāṃ dravyānārambhāt | tataśca mālāguṇopi "geho yadyapi saṃyogasta"sya "mālā kintu tad bhavet" | na bhāvaguṇo nirguṇatvāt guṇānāṃ | (155)

{2.156}

<ka. sāmānyasvīkāre doṣaḥ>

[2.156,0]

"jātiśced geha ekopi māletyucyeta vṛkṣavat | mālābahutve tacchabdaḥ kathaṃ jāterajātitaḥ || 156 ||"

[2.156,1]

"jātiśceda"bhyupagamyate "eko geho māletyucyeta vṛkṣavat" | yathā vṛkṣatvajātiyogādeko vṛkṣo vṛkṣa ityucyate evamekopi geho mālā syāt | tathā gehamālānāṃ bahutve "tacchabdo" māletyanugāmiśabdaḥ "kathaṃ jāte" rmālāyāṃ "ajātito" jātyantaravirahāt | (156)

{2.157}

[2.157,0]

kiñca |

[2.157,1]

"mālādau ca mahatvādiriṣṭo yaścaupacārikaḥ | mukhyāviśiṣṭavijñānagrāhyatvānnaupacārikaḥ || 157 ||"

[2.157,2]

mahatī prāsādamāleti kathaṃ vyapadeśaḥ | mahatvaṃ parimāṇaṃ guṇaḥ | tasya mālāyāṃ na sattvaṃ | na hi prāsādamālā kiñcidityuktaṃ | nāpi saṃyogalakṣaṇe prāsāde mahattvaṃ nirguṇatvā(t) guṇānāṃ | kāṣṭhādiṣu dravyeṣu prāsādārambhakeṣu mahattvasattvādvṛkṣeṣu kusumasambhavād vanasaṃkhyālakṣaṇaṃ kusumitamiti yathocyate | tathā prāsāda"mālā" yaśceṣṭaḥ sa cāyuktaḥ kāṣṭhādiṣvapi tādṛśasya mahattvasyābhāvāt |

[2.157,3]

kiñca | mahān parvvata iti"mu"khyamahattvagrāhakajñānenāskhaladvṛttitvādaviśiṣṭena jñānena grāhyatvāt prāsādamālāmahatvādi"raupacāriko" na yuktaḥ | na hi māṇavaka iva siṃhabuddhirmahattvabuddhiśca mālāyāṃ skhalati | (157)

{2.158}

[2.158,0]

kiñca | bhinnaviśeṣaṇaṃ "mukhya"mabhinnaviśeṣaṇañcāmukhyamiti yaducyate tadapyayuktamityāha |

[2.158,1]

"ananyahetutā tulyā sā mukhyābhimateṣvapi || padārthaśabdaḥ kaṃ hetumanyaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ samīkṣate || 158 ||"

[2.158,2]

"mukhyābhimateṣvapi" daṇḍyādiṣva"nanyahetutā" bhinnaviśeṣaṇanimittarahitatā "tulyā" gauṇena sarvvatra vyapadeśo hi daṇḍāderapi sāṃvṛtādi(2 | 154)tyukteḥ | kiñcānuyāyī "padārthaśabdaḥ" ṣaṣṭhyā padārtheṣu "kamanyaṃ hetuṃ" nimittaṃ pravṛttau "samīkṣyate" | na hi ṣaṭpadārthātiriktaṃ kiñcidasti | (158)

{2.159}

[2.159,0]

"yo yathā rūḍhitaḥ siddhaḥ tatsāmyādyastathocyate |"

[2.159,1]

tasmādyo'rtho yena prakāreṇa rūḍhitaḥ ādisaṃketānusāreṇa siddhaḥ sa mukhyaḥ | yaśca tasya mukhyasya sāmyāttathāmukhyavācakaśabdenocyate sa gauṇaḥ |

[2.159,2]

kuta etadityāha |

[2.159,3]

"yatra gauṇaśca bhāveṣyapyabhāvasyopacārataḥ || 159 ||"

[2.159,4]

"bhāveṣvapi" kuputrādiṣu putrādirityabhāvo"pacārataḥ" | paramate tu bhāve vṛttatvānmukhyatvaṃ bhavet | (159)

{2.160}

<kha. vivakṣānvayisaṃketānugamatvād rūḍheḥ>

[2.160,0]

syādetad | rūḍhyaiva mukhyatā kintu sāpi bhinne viśeṣaṇe satītyāha | na |

[2.160,1]

"saṃketānvayinī rūḍhirvakturicchānvayī ca saḥ | kriyate vyavahārārtha chandaḥ śabdāṃśanābhavat || 160 ||"

[2.160,2]

"saṃketānvayinī" yathāsaṃketaṃ "rūḍhiḥ sa ca" saṃketo "vaktuḥ" saṃketayitu"ricchānvayī " gāyatryādeḥ "śabdāṃ"śasya prakṛtipratyayāde"rnāmavat" | na hi viśiṣṭānupūrvvīkeṣu varṇṇeṣu pṛthagbhūtaṃ gāyatryādiśūbdanimittaṃ kiñcidasti | śabdāṃśeṣu vā'pi tu saṃketayituricchānurodhādeva tathā vyapadeśaḥ | (160)

{2.161}

[2.161,0]

yadi vyaktibhyo na bhinnaṃ sāmānyaṃ tadā kathamanugāmī pratyaya ityāha |

[2.161,1]

"vastudharmatayaivārthāstādṛgvijñānakāraṇam | bhedepi yatra tajjñānāṃttāntathā pratipadyate || 161 ||"

[2.161,2]

"vastudharmatayā" prakṛ"tyaiva" keci"darthāḥ" parasparaṃ "bhedepi tādṛ"śasyānugāmino'tatkāryaṃvyāvṛttiviṣayasya "vijñānasya kāraṇaṃ" | yatra yeṣvartheṣvanugāmi jñānaṃ tānabhedino'rthān "tathā" ekatve"na pratipadyate" na tvekasāmānyaṃ balāttathā jñānaṃ | (161)

{2.162}

[2.162,0]

syādetat | prativyakti jñānānyapi bhinnānīti kathamanugāmi jñānamityāha |

[2.162,1]

"jñānānyapi tathā bhede'bhedapratyavamarśane | ityatatkāryaviśleṣasyānvayo naikavastunaḥ || 162 ||"

[2.162,2]

"jñānānyapi" parasparato "bhede tathā"'rthavadvastudharmitayā"'bhedapratyavamarśane" nimittaṃ tato jñānānyapi tadekaparāmarśagocaratayā'nugāmipratyaya ucyante ityanena prakāreṇa bhediṣvartheṣvata"tkāryā"darthasya "viśleṣo" vyavacchedastasyā"nvayo" vidyate | "na tvekasya""vastunaḥ" sāmānyasya | (162)

{2.163}

[2.163,0]

"vastūnāṃ vidyate tasmāttanniṣṭhā vastuni śrutiḥ |"

[2.163,1]

"vastūnāṃ" viśeṣāṇāmanvayo "vidyate"'nupalambhabādhitatvāttasya | "tasmāt tanniṣṭhā" vyāvṛttiviṣayā "vastu"ni "śrutiḥ" pravartate |

<(5) anyāpohacintā>

<ka. atatkāryavyāvṛttiḥ>

[2.163,2]

nanvatatkāryavyāvṛttirvastunaḥ svabhāvabhūtā tato vyāvṛttiviṣayatve "vastuviṣaya" syādityāha |

[2.163,3]

"bāhyaśaktivyavacchedaniṣṭhābhāvepi tacchrutiḥ || 163 ||"

[2.163,4]

"bāhya"sya vastunaḥ "śakte"ratatkāryādyo "vyavaccheda"statra "niṣṭhā" viṣayitvaṃ tasyābhāvepi "tacchruti"rvyavacchedavācinī śrutiḥ | (163)

{2.164}

[2.164,0]

"vikalpapratibimbeṣu tanniṣṭheṣu nibadhyate | tatonyāpohaniṣṭhatvāduktānyāpohakṛcchrutiḥ || 164 ||"

[2.164,1]

vika"lpānāṃ pratibimbe"ṣvākāreṣu "tanniṣṭheṣu" tadvyāvṛttivastutvena vyavasthāviṣayatayā tadvyavahāravyavasthitiṣu saṃketakāle "nibadhyate | tato" vikalpapratibimbānāṃ bāhyavyāvṛttātmatvena vyavahāraviṣayatvādanyā"pohaniṣṭhatvā"tkāraṇā"duktā śrutiranyāpohakṛt" | anyavyāvṛttākāravikalpajananāt anyavyāvṛtteṣu pravartanācca śabdo'nyāpohakṛduktaḥ | (164)

{2.165}

[2.165,0]

nanu śābde jñāne grāhyaṃ bāhyatayaiva pratīyate na jñānākāratayetyāha |

[2.165,1]

"vyatirekīva yajjñāne bhātyarthapratibimbakam | śabdāttadapi nārthātmā bhrāntiḥ sā vāsanodbhavā || 165 ||"

[2.165,2]

"śabdādu"tpanna"jñāne'rthapratibimbakaṃ vyatirekīva" bhinnaṃ bāhyamiva "yadābhā" bahirarthasvarūpaṃ kintu "bhrāntiḥ sā vāsanānirmitā" | yathā taimirikadṛṣṭeṣu keśādiṣu bāhyabhramaḥ | evaṃ vikalpākārepi bāhyavyavahāro'vidyāvaśādityarthaḥ | (165)

{2.166}

[2.166,0]

jñānākārastarhi vastubhūto vācyaḥ syādityāha |

[2.166,1]

"tasyābhidhāne śrutibhirarthe koṃśovagamyate | tasyāgatau ca saṃketakriyā vyarthā tadarthikā || 166 ||"

[2.166,2]

"tasya" jñānākārasya "śrutibhirabhidhāne'rthe"'tatkāryavyāvṛtte śabdenācodite koṃśovagamyate na kaścittadakāryavyāvṛ"ttasyā"rthasya śabdā"dagatau ca" satyāṃ "saṃketakriyā vyarthā" yasmā"ttadarthikā" atatkāryavyāvṛttārthapratītiphalā seṣyate | (166)

{2.167}

[2.167,0]

evantarhyanyāpohepi saṃkete kṛte pravṛttirartheṣu na syāt | tasyārthātmatvābhāvādityāha |

[2.167,1]

"śabdorthāṃśaṃkamāheti tatrānyāpoha ucyate | ākāraḥ sa ca nārthesti taṃ vadannarthabhāk katham || 167 ||"

[2.167,2]

"śabdo'rthāṃśaṃkamāheti" praśne "tatrānyāpoho"'tatkāryavyāvṛttiḥ sarvvaviśeṣasaṃbhavinī vācyatayo"cyate" | ato'rthāṃśātmanyanyāpohe gṛhītasaṃketaḥ śabdāduccaritārthaṃ pratītya tatra pravarttita iti yuktaṃ | yastatrā"kṣākāraḥ sa cārthe nāsti taṃ" buddhyākāraṃ "vadan śabdo'rthabhāk" bāhyārthābhidhāyī kathamastu | (167)

{2.168}

[2.168,0]

kiñca |

[2.168,1]

"śabdasyānvayinaḥ kāryamarthenānvayinā sa ca | ananvayī dhiyo'bhedād darśanābhyāsanirmmataḥ || 168 ||"

[2.168,2]

"śabdasyānvayi"'nvayinā"rthena kāryaṃ" vyavahārakāle pratītilakṣaṇaṃ prayojanaṃ | "sa ca" buddhyākāraḥ svalakṣaṇa"darśanābhyāsena" vāsanā"nirmmito'nanvayī dhiyo"'nanvayinyā "abhedāt" | (168)

{2.169}

[2.169,0]

nanu yadyarthaḥ śabdasya na viṣayastadā tadaṃ śarūpopyanyāpohaḥ kathaṃ vācya ityāha |

[2.169,1]

"tadrūpāropagatyānyavyāvṛttādhigateḥ punaḥ | śabdārthārthaḥ sa eveti vacane na virudhyate || 169 ||"

[2.169,2]

buddhyākāre tadrūpasyāparthāṃśāpohasyā"ropagatyā" ekatvādhyavasāyenā"nyavyāvṛ"rthasyā"dhigateḥ śabdārthāṃ"śāpohaḥ śabdārtha ucyate | na tu sāmānyācchabdādarthapratīteḥ | yadi punarbuddhyākārasya vyāvṛttārthatvena pratīteḥ sa buddhyākāra eva śabdārtha ityupacārāducyate buddhyākāraśabdārthavādinā | tadaivaṃ "vacane" kiñcidapi "na " | buddhyākārasyānvayinaḥ śabdārthatvāniṣṭeḥ | (169)

{2.170}

<kha. anyāpohakṛcchabdaḥ>

[2.170,0]

"mithyāvabhāsino vaite pratyayāḥ śabdanirmmitāḥ |"

[2.170,1]

mithyā"vabhāsino vā śabdanirmitā ete pratyayāḥ" | tathā hi na tāvadarthaḥ śabdabuddherviṣayaḥ | tatsvarūpānavabhāsataḥ | tatra śabdasaṃketābhāvācca | nāpi buddhyākārastasya vedanepi viṣayatvenānadhyavasāyāt svalakṣaṇatvāt saṃketābhāvācca | na hi buddhyākārasya bahiṣṭvaṃ bāhyasya vā buddhyākaratvamasti yena tatheti bhāsaḥ satyapratibhāsaḥ syāt | tasmādvastuto'vastupratibhāsinaḥ śābdāḥ pratyayāḥ |

[2.170,2]

kathantarhīdānīmarthāṃśāpohakṛcchrutiruktetyāha |

[2.170,3]

"anuyāntīmamarthāṃśamiti vāpohakṛcchrutiḥ || 170 ||"

[2.170,4]

"imama"nyāpohama"rthāṃśaṃ" śabdā atatpratibhāsitvepi "anuyānti" vṛttiviṣayatvena vyavasthāpayanti | arthadarśanāyātatvena parasparaṃ yā tatpratibandhanāditi cānyā"poha"ruktā | (170)

{2.171}

[2.171,0]

"tasmāt saṃketakālepi;"

[2.171,1]

yasmād vyavahārakāle'nyavyavacchedapratītiḥ śabdāt "tasmātsaṃketakālepya"nyāpohaḥ śrutau vācyatayā sambadhyate nānyat |

[2.171,2]

nanvarthamupadarśya saṃketaḥ kriyate tatkathamapoha ucyata ityāha |

[2.171,3]

"nirdiṣṭārthena saṃyutaḥ | svapratītiphalenānyāpohaḥ saṃbadhyate śrutau || 171 ||"

[2.171,4]

"nirdiṣṭenārthenā"nyavyāvṛttena vyavahārakāle "sva"sya "pratītiḥ phalaṃ" prayojanaṃ yasya tena "saṃyuto"'bhedādhyavasāyādekatvamupanīto"'nyāpoho" buddhyākārasvabhāvaḥ "śrutau samba" na tvartha eva | (171)

{2.172}

[2.172,0]

tathā hi |

[2.172,1]

"anyātrādṛṣṭyapekṣatvāt kvacittaddṛṣṭyapekṣaṇāt | śrutau saṃbadhyatepoho naitad vastuni yujyate || 172 ||"

[2.172,2]

saṃketasyā"nyatra" vyavacchedye"'vṛkṣe'darśanāpekṣatvāt | kvaci"davyavacchedye vṛkṣaikadeśe "dṛṣṭyapekṣaṇāt śrutā"vapohaḥ "sambadhyata" iti niścīyate | "vastuni"sāmānyādau saṃketaviṣaye etat vyavacchedyāvyavacchedyayordarśanādarśanāpekṣaṇaṃ "na yujyate" | vastuni vidhimukhena pratipādye kimanyatrādarśanāpekṣayā | apekṣyate ca tato'nyavyavaccheda eva pratipādyata iti gamyate | anyavyavacchedaḥ sāmānyādikaṃ cāpekṣyate vipakṣaparihāreṇa pratipattyarthamiti cet | alaṃ tadā sāmānyena | anyavyavacchedenaiva vyavahāraparisamāpteḥ | (172)

{2.173}

[2.173,0]

yataśca jātiguṇakriyādīni viśeṣaṇāni vastugrāhiṇi jñāne nābhāsante |

[2.173,1]

"tasmād jātyāditadyogā nārthe teṣu ca na śrutiḥ | saṃyojyatenyavyāvṛttau śabdānāmeva yojanāt || 173 ||"

[2.173,2]

"tasmājjātyādayasteṣāṃ yogāścārthe na" santi | "ata"steṣu "śrutiśca nopa"yujyate | "anyavyāvṛttāveva" pratītisiddhāyāṃ "śabdānāṃ yojanāt" | (173)

{2.174}

<(6) ka. pratyakṣe śabdakalpanānirāsaḥ>

[2.174,0]

tadevaṃ jātyādikalpanā tatsambandhakalpanā ca nāstītyuktaṃ | śabdakalpanāpi na sambhavatītyāha |

[2.174,1]

"saṃketasmaraṇopāyaṃ dṛṣṭasaṃkalanātmakam | pūrvāparaparāmarśaśūnye taccākṣuṣe katham || 174 ||"

[2.174,2]

śabdakalpanaṃ hi pūrvvagṛhītasya "saṃketa"sya "smaraṇamupāyo" yasya saṃketasmaraṇopāyaṃ vācakatvena "dṛṣṭa"sya śabdasya "saṃkalanaṃ" tathāyojana"mātmā" yasya tat dṛṣṭasaṃkalanātmakaṃ prasiddhaṃ | tacca "pūrvva"sya saṃketakāladṛṣṭavācakaśabdasyā"parasya" dṛśyamānārthasya "parāmarśo" vācyavācakatāyojanantena śūnyā śabdāmiśravastusvarūpagrāhiṇi "cākṣuṣe" jñāne "kathaṃ" saṃbhāvyate | cākṣuṣaṃ cākṣajamātropalakṣaṇamindriyajñānamityarthaḥ | (174)

{2.175}

[2.175,0]

kiñca |

[2.175,1]

"anyatra gatacittopi cakṣuṣā rūpamīkṣate | tatsaṃketāgrahastatra spaṣṭastajjā ca kalpanā || 175 ||"

[2.175,2]

dṛśyamānādarthāda"nyatrā"tītādau vikalpanīye "gatacittaḥ" pravṛttavikalpopi draṣṭā "cakṣuṣā" cakṣurvvijñānena "rūpamīkṣate" | tasya dṛśyamānārthasya "saṃketaḥ" saṃketaviṣayo vācakaṃ nāma tasyā"graho"'smaraṇaṃ "tatra" cākṣuṣe jñāne "spaṣṭaḥ" | tata"stajjā" vācakanāmasmaraṇaprabhavā "kalpanā ca" cākṣuṣe jñāne nāstīti śeṣaḥ | (175)

{2.176}

[2.176,0]

kiñca |

[2.176,1]

"jāyante kalpanāstatra yatra śabdo niveśitaḥ | tenecchātaḥ pravartteran nekṣeran bāhyamakṣajāḥ || 176 ||"

[2.176,2]

tatra viṣaye śabdayojanātmikāḥ "kalpanā jāyante | yatra" saṃketakāle "śabdo " | na cendriyaviṣaye śabdasaṃketa iti na tat jñānaṃ śabdayojanātmakaṃ prāk | athendriyaviṣaya eva śabdaniveśastadā "tena" śabdaviṣayatvena kāraṇe"necchātaḥ pravartterannakṣajāḥ" pratyayā vikalpavat | na caitadasti | icchāprabhavatve vā bāhyārthasaṃnidhānānapekṣatvāt | "bāhyamarthaṃ nekṣerannakṣajāḥ" pratyayavikalpavat | (176)

{2.177}

[2.177,0]

api ca |

[2.177,1]

"rūpaṃ rūpamitīkṣeta taddhiyaṃ kimitīkṣate || asti cānubhavastasyāḥsovikalpaḥ kathaṃ bhavet || 177 ||"

[2.177,2]

sarvvavikalpavādino mate "rūpamiti" pravṛttavikalpabuddhī "rūpamīkṣeta | taddhiyaṃ" rūpadhiyamapi kalpyamānāṃ "kimitīkṣate" jñātā rūpabuddhya"nubhavo" nāstīti na yuktaṃ | yasmādasti cānubhavastasyāḥ sarvveṣāṃ pratipattṛṇāṃ | na ca rūpa iva tadbuddhāvapi kalpanā'nubhūyate | tataśca rūpabuddheranubhavo"'vikalpaḥ kathambhavet" | (177)

{2.178}

[2.178,0]

"tayaivānubhave dṛṣṭaṃ na vikalpadvayaṃ sakṛt | etena tulyakālānyavijñānānubhavo gataḥ || 178 ||"

[2.178,1]

"tayai"va rūpabuddhyā rūpasya svātmanaścā'"nubhave"bhyupagamyamāne rūpamiti rūpānubhava iti ca "vikalpadvayaṃ sakṛt" syāt | tacca nāstyanubhavavādhitatvāt | "etena" sakṛtkalpanādvayaniṣedhena "tulyakālenānyena" nirvvikalpajñānenā"nubhavo" rūpabuddhe"rgato" nirṇṇītottaro boddhavyaḥ | (178)

{2.179}

<kha. uttarakālabhāvivikalpajñānenānubhavaḥ>

[2.179,0]

uttarakālabhāvinā vikalpajñānenānubhava iti cedāha |

[2.179,1]

"smṛtirbhavedatīte ca sā'gṛhīte kathaṃ bhavet | syāccānyadhīparicchedābhinnarūpā svabuddhidhīḥ || 179 ||"

[2.179,2]

"atīte ca" rūpānubhave "smṛtiḥ" paścāttanena vikalpena na bhavennānubhavaḥ | "sā" smṛtira"gṛhīte"'nubhave "kathambhavet" | yadi cātītabuddhirvvikalpyate tadā'nyasya puṃso dhiyaḥ "paricchedena" parokṣabuddhivikalpātmakenā"bhinnarūpā" tathātvena "svabuddhidhīḥ" syāt | asti ca parabuddhipratītivilakṣaṇasvabuddhyanubhavaḥ | tasmādavikalpa evāsau | (179)

{2.180}

[2.180,0]

kiñca |

[2.180,1]

[2.180,2]

savikalpakapratyakṣavādinā nirvvikalpasyāpyasvasaṃvedanavādino mate'"tīta" na kevalamadhyakṣato vartamānaviṣayatvānna sidhyati | kintvanumānādapi yasmāda"liṅgaṃ" liṅgarahitaṃ | tathā hi dharmiṇo jñānasyāsiddhatvāt liṅgamāśrayā"siddhaṃ | anumānāt jñānasiddhivādinaḥ kasyacijjñānasyādhyakṣāsiddhatvāt" anumānasiddhāvanavasthānāt "apadṛṣṭāntaṃ" | dṛṣṭāntāsiddhau na"vyāptisiddhiriti" liṅgarahitamevātītaṃ rūpādidarśanaṃ | "tattasmātkena pramāṇena siddhaṃ tasmin hi" rūpādidarśane "na pratyakṣa"mabhimatatvādasti | "na ca laiṅgikamanumānamuktakramāditi" sakalamapratipattikamandhamūkaṃ jagatprāptamiti || (180)

{2.181–2.184}

[2.181–2.184,0]

[2.181–2.184,3]

[2.181–2.184,4]

"na syāt tatpūrvadhīgrahaḥ || 181 ||"

[2.181–2.184,5]

[2.181–2.184,6]

"sāmānyavācinaḥ śabdāstadekārthā ca kalpanā | abhāve nirvikalpasya viśeṣādhigamaḥ katham || 183 ||"

[2.181–2.184,7]

"asti cennirvikalpañca kiñcittattulyahetukam | sarvaṃ tathaiva hetorhi bhedād bhedaḥ phalātmanām || 184 ||"

[2.181–2.184,8]

tasmādantyāt jñānāt yāḥ "pūrvvā" dhiyastāsāṃ "graho na syādi"ti doṣaḥ | antyabuddhijanitayā hi dhiyā saiva gṛhyate na tvanyā iti syāt | asti cānubhavastāsāṃ yadvalena ciramahamadrākṣamiti bhavati draṣṭuḥ | tasmā"tsvaviṣayaḥ" svarūpālambano "vijñānā"nāṃ pūrvvabhāvinā"manubhavo'vikalpaḥ" | sa yathā "tadvadanyadapi" jñānamantyamapratibaddhavṛtti "cāvikalpakaṃ" boddhavyaṃ | yasmātsakalameva svarūpa"maśakya" śabdasaṃketāviṣayaḥ | tataśca na vikalpagrāhyaṃ | kiñca viśeṣasaṃketābhāvāt vyavahārakālānuyāyitvācca "sāmānyavācinaḥ śabdāstaiḥ" śabdai"rekārthā" ekaviṣayā "ca kalpanā" śabdayojanayā śabdārtha eva kalpanā | paramate ca "nirvvikala" jñānasyā"bhāve" viśeṣasya "vikalpā"viṣayasyā"dhigamaḥ kathaṃ" na kathañcidityarthaḥ | viśeṣānubhavadarśanā"dasti kiñci" jñānaṃ yathāhurmī māṃ sa "kādaya iti cet" | evantarhi tena nirvvikalpena "tulyahetukaṃ" cakṣūrūpamanaskārādisamānahetukaṃ viśeṣaviṣayaṃ "sarvvaṃ" jñānaṃ "tathaivā"vikalpakamastu | na tu svalakṣaṇaviṣayamapi kiñcitsavikalpakaṃ | hiryasmā"ddhatorbhedātphalātmanāṃ bhedo" bhavati | hetvabhede tu phalābheda eva yuktaḥ | nānyathā kvacidapyekajātīyatā syāt || (181–84)

{2.185}

kiñca |

{2.186}

{2.187}

[2.187,2]

"tasyāḥ smṛtesta"syārthasya "saṃgamena" sammukhībhāve"notpatteḥ | na tvakṣadhī"rarthā"tsyāt" | sā tu smṛterarthajanitāyāḥ syāt | na vā smṛterapi bhavet smṛtyadhīnatāyāṃ nārthādhīnatā | yacca smaraṇaṃ bhāvi tannāvaśyaṃ bhavatīti kadācinna bhavedapi | "tataḥ" smṛteḥ "kālānta"dhyakṣadhīḥ smṛtyanantaraṃ "kvaci"dviṣayāntare "vyākṣepasyā"śaktilakṣaṇasya "saṃbhavāt" | tannivṛttau satyāṃ krameṇa bhavet | (187)

{ii.vi}

<(6. pratyakṣabhedāḥ)>

<(1) indriyapratyakṣam>

{2.191cada}

[2.191cada,0]

"atha kasmād dvayādhīnajanma tattena nocyate || 191 ||"

[2.191cada,1]

"atha dvayādhīnajanma"viṣayendriyotpatti"tadi"ndriyajñānamindriyeṇo"cyate" vyapadiśyate pratyakṣamiti pratigatamakṣampratyakṣamindriyāśritamityarthaḥ ḥ | kasmātpunarvviṣayeṇa "nocyate" prativiṣayamiti || (191)

{2.192}

[2.192,0]

na khalu vyasanitayā vyapadeśo niyujyate | api tu |

[2.192,1]

"samīkṣya gamakatvaṃ hi vyapadeśo na gṛhyate | taccākṣavyapadeśesti taddharmaśca niyojyatām || 192 ||"

[2.192,2]

"gamakatvaṃ samīkṣya" paribhāvya | "tacca gamakatvamakṣeṇa vyapa" pratyakṣamityatrāsti tasya gamakatvasya vyāpakasya "dharmmo" vyāpyabhūto "niyojyatāṃ |"(192)

{2.193}

[2.193,0]

"tato liṅgasvabhāvotra vyapadeśe niyojyatām | nivarttate vyāpakasya svabhāvasya nivṛttitaḥ || 193 ||"

[2.193,1]

"tato" vyāpakābhāvāt "vyapadeśe" dharmmiṇi "atra" gamakatve sādhye "niyojyatāṃ" liṅgaṃ | prativiṣayamiti vyapadeśāt "vyāpakasya" gamakatvasya "nivṛttito nivartate" niyojyateti vyāpakānupalabdhyā tatra niyojyatvābhāvaḥ siddhaḥ | (193)

{2.194}

<ka. akṣāṇāṃ gamakatvāt pratyakṣam>

[2.194,0]

"sañcitaḥ samudāyaḥ sa sāmānyaṃ tatra cākṣadhīḥ | sāmānyabuddhiścāvaśyaṃ vikalpenānubadhyate || 194 ||"

[2.194,1]

nanu sañcitālambanāḥ pañca vijñānakāyā iti siddhāntaḥ | "tatrānekārtha" miti coktaṃ | tathā ca paramāṇūnāṃ "samudāyaḥ" sañcita ityucyate | "sa" eva ca sāmānye mataḥ "tatra ca" sāmānye'"kṣadhī"rjjāyate | "sāmānyabuddhiścāvaśyaṃ vikalpenānubadhyate" anusīvyate | (194)

{2.195}

[2.195,0]

tatkathamavikalpaṃ pratyakṣamucyate ||

[2.195,1]

atrāha |

[2.195,2]

"arthāntarābhisambandhājjāyante ye'ṇavo'pare | uktāste sañcitāste hi nimittaṃ jñānajanmanaḥ || 195 ||"

[2.195,3]

"arthāntarāṇāṃ paramāṇvantarāṇāmabhisambandhāt" sannidhānaviśeṣeṇopasarpaṇapratyayebhyaḥ pūrvvakebhyaḥparamasannihitebhyo'parenye"ye'ṇavo jāyante" te sañcitā "uktāḥ "tālambanā vijñānakāya ityādau | "jñānajanma"nasta eva hi "nimitta"muktāḥ tatrānekārthajanyatvādityādinā | (195)

{2.196}

[2.196,0]

"aṇūnāṃ sa viśeṣaśca nāntareṇāparānaṇūna | tadekāniyamājjñānamuktaṃ sāmānyagocaram || 196 ||"

[2.196,1]

"aṇūnāṃ" sa ca jñānajananasāmarthyalakṣaṇo "viśeṣo'parānaṇūna"vyavadhānavarttino'ntareṇa vinā na bhavati | na hi pratyekamaṇavo dṛśyāḥ kiṃ tu sahitā eva | "tattasmā"sminnarthe paramāṇau jñānasyā"niyamāt sāmānyagocaraṃ" saṃcitaparamāṇusaṃghātaviṣayaṃ "jñānamuktaṃ" tattvavādinā | na tu paramāṇvatiriktasāmānyaviṣayaṃ | tatkathaṃ sāmānyaviṣayatvāt savikalpatvaprasaṅgaḥ || (196)

{2.197}

[2.197,0]

"athaikāyatanatvepi nānekaṃ dṛśyate sakṛt | sakṛdgrahāvabhāsaḥ kiṃ viyukteṣu tilādiṣu || 197 ||"

[2.197,1]

athaikendriyajñānajanakatvāt nīlapītādīnā"mekāyatanatve" rūpāyatanatvasaṃgrahepi "nānekaṃ" nīlādi "sakṛd dṛśyate" kintu krameṇa tatkathamaṇūnā "bahūnāmekadā""grahaṇaṃ | atrocyate" | yadi nānekamekadā gṛhyate tadā "tilādiṣu viyukteṣu" vibhinna"deśeṣu sakṛdgra"hāva"bhāso" yugapad grahaṇānubhavaḥ kiṃ kasmāddhe toḥ | (197)

{2.198}

[2.198,0]

[2.198,2]

[2.200,2]

[2.201,2]

"citrama"nekarūpaṃ "hi" yasmāttasmānnaikaṃ pataṅgādi | "yathaiva" saṃsthānaviśeṣeṇa sanniviṣṭānāṃ bahūnāṃ "maṇī"nāṃ "rūpaṃ ta"ccitramanekaṃ naikamavayavi dravyaṃ vijātīyānāṃ dravyānārambhāt | citrabuddhirekatvānmukhyā pataṅgemaṇirūpādiṣu punarupacariteti cet | āha | nīlādipratibhāsaścitrapratibhāsaḥ sa "citrapaṭa ādi"ryeṣāṃ maṇirūpādīnāṃ teṣu citrapataṅge "ca tulyaḥ" | na tvagnimāṇavakayordahanabuddhiriva skhaladaskhaladvṛttirlakṣyate | (201)

{2.202}

[2.202,1]

"tatra" citrapaṭādiṣu kevalamava"yavarūpaṃ tathā citratayā dṛśyate" nāvayavī vijātīyānāṃ dravyānārambhāditi cet | citrapataṅgādāvapi "nīlādīni nirasya" pṛthakkṛtya "tebhyo"mavayavirūpaṃ "yadīkṣase" tvaṃ ta"ccitra"māścaryaṃ | svasiddhāntānurāgabheṣajaviśodhitacakṣurīkṣase tvameva yadīdṛśamavayavinaṃ paraṃ nātrānyeṣāmadhikāraḥ | (202)

{2.214}

[2.214,0]

[2.214,1]

{2.215}

[2.215,0]

[2.215,2]

rūpādīnāṃ "grāhyagrāhakākārā"bhyāṃ "bāhyaṃ" bhinnaṃ "lakṣaṇaṃ na cāsti" | tathā hi viṣayatayā kiñcinnirddiśyate | yathā rūpyata iti kṛtvā rūpaṃ | kiñcidviṣayitayā vijānātītyādi vyutpattyā yathā rūpiṇaḥ skandhāḥ | na tvetadvyatiriktaṃ kiñcillakṣaṇamasti | "ato lakṣaṇena" grāhyagrāhakatvena "śūnyatvānniḥsvabhāvāḥ" sarvvadharmmāḥ "prakāśitā" bhagavadbhirbu ddhaiḥ | (215)

{2.216}

[2.216,0]

kiñca | bahirarthavādepi lakṣaṇaśūnyatvāt niḥsvabhāvatāṃ dharmmāṇāmākhyātumāha |

[2.216,1]

"vyāpāropādhikaṃ sarvaṃ skandhādīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ | lakṣaṇaṃ sa ca tattvanna tenāpyete vilakṣaṇāḥ || 216 ||"

[2.216,2]

"skandha" ādiryeṣāṃ dhātvāyatanā"nāṃ" teṣāṃ yallakṣaṇaṃ rāśībhavantīti rāśyarthaḥ skandhānāṃ | kāryotpādakatvenākārārtho dhātūnāṃ | āyantanvantītyāyadvārārtha āyatanānāṃ | "tatsarvaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vyāpāropādhikaṃ" vyāpāraviśeṣaṇaṃ | "sa ca" vyāpāro'pratīterbhedapakṣe na tattvaṃ | abhedepi prāgabhāvī bhāva eva syāt | sa ca tattvaṃ na bhavati | aśaktaṃ sarvamiti cedi(2 | 4) tyatroktakramāt | "tena" vyāpāropādhikalakṣaṇāyogenāpi "vilakṣaṇā" niḥsva"bhāvā ete" skandhādayaḥ | (216)

{2.217}

[2.217,0]

kathaṃ tarhi bāhyaskandhādideśanā bhagavatāmityāha |

{2.219}

[2.219,0]
