[2.219,1]

"tad bhrā"ntadarśanānurodhā"dupekṣitatatvārthai"ravadhāritatadadvayavivekai"rbhagavadbhirbuddhai" gajasyeva pārśvadvayaṃ paśyatopi nayananimīlanakalayā tattvamapaśyantamivātmānaṃ darśayadbhi"rloka"syāvidyopahatasya "buddhyā" dvayagrāhiṇyā "bāhya"sya "cintā"skandhāyatanāditvena "pratanyate" | skandhādideśanayā hi lokabuddhyanurodhapravartitapāṣaṇḍagrāhanivṛttau mukhyayā yeṣu mumukṣavo'vatāryanta iti deśanākramaḥ | (219)

{2.220}

[2.220,0]

athavā citratvepi bāhyamekaṃ na yuktaṃ buddhistu citrāpyekaiveti darśayitumāha |

[2.220,1]

"nīlādiścitravijñāne jñānopādhirananyabhāk || aśakyadarśanaḥ;"

[2.220,2]

"nīlādiścitre jñāne jñānopādhira"nubhavasyātmabhūtaḥ "ananyabhāk" ākārāntarāsahacaraḥ kevala ityarthaḥ | tādṛśo'"śakyadarśanaḥ" sahaivākārāntaravedananiyamāt | na hi citre vijñāne samutpanne nīlaṃ nirasya pītaṃ śakyadarśanaṃ | tasmādaśakyavivecanatvaṃ tulyayogakṣematvaṃ sahapratibhāsaniyatatvaṃ jñānātmanāṃ nīlādīnāmekatvaṃ | bāhyātmanāṃ tu naitatsaṃbhavati | ekaṃ pidhāyāpi draṣṭumanyasya śakyatvāt |

[2.220,3]

nanu jñānākāropi nīlaḥ pītānubhavakāle tadā nānubhūyate tadā śakyavivecana evetyāha |

[2.220,4]

"taṃ hi patatyarthe vivecayan || 220 ||"

[2.220,5]

tamanubhūyamānāt pītāt "vivecayan" bhedena vyavasthāpayan pramātā "artha" eva nīle "patati" vivecakatvena | parokṣaṃ tadā nīlamartha eva | aparokṣataiva tu jñānasvabhāvaḥ | ato yad vivicyate tadajñānaṃ | yajjñānaṃ tanna vivecyata eva | (220)

{2.221}

[2.221,0]

tasmād |

[2.221,1]

"yad yathā bhāsate jñānaṃ tattathaiva prakāśate | iti nāmaikabhāvaḥ syāccitrākārasya cetasi || 221 ||"

[2.221,2]

"yajjñānaṃ yathā" nīlādyātmatayā jātaṃ "sattathā" bhāsate "prakāśate" | bhāsamānasvabhāvatvāt "jñānaṃ" tathā tenaiva svarūpeṇānubhūyate sarveḥ pratipattṛbhiḥ | na cotpannasyāpi jñānasya svaprakāśakasyāviditaḥ kaścidākārosti "itya"śakyavivecanatvāt tulyayogakṣematvāt sahapratibhāsaniyamāt | "citra"sya nīlapītādyā"kārasya "tasi buddhāvekabhāvo nāma bhavettadā ko doṣaḥ | (221)

{2.222}

[2.222,0]

"paṭādirūpasyaikatve tathā syādavivekitā |"

[2.222,1]

jñānavat paṭādirūpasya ekatve'bhyupagamyamāne tathā jñānasyevāvivekitā'śakyavivecanatvaṃ syāt | na cāsti | nīlādīnāṃ grahaṇāgrahaṇabhedasya darśanāt |

[2.222,2]

syādetad | avayavā nīlādyāḥ parasparato'vayavinaśca bhinnāsteṣāṃ bhedādvivekena grahaṇaṃ | yastvabhinno'vayavī na tasya vivekena grahaṇamityāha |

[2.222,3]

"vivekīni nirasyānyadā viveki ca nekṣate || 222 ||"

[2.222,4]

vivekīni nīlādyavayavarūpāṇi nirasya pṛthak kṛtvā "anyadā vivekirūpañca " | dṛśyasammatamanupalabhyamānaṃ kathamabhyupagamārha | (222)

{2.223}

[2.223,0]

yaccocyate paramāṇavaḥ pratyekamatīndriyatvāt sañcitā api na jñānagocara iti tatrāha |

[2.223,1]

"ko vā virodho bahavaḥ saṃjātātiśayāḥ pṛthak | bhaveyuḥ kāraṇaṃ buddheryadi nātmendriyādivat || 223 ||"

[2.223,2]

"yadi bahavaḥ" paramāṇava upasarpaṇapratyayāt "saṃjā tātiśayā" vijñānajananayogyāḥ saṃhatā utpannā svagrāhi kāryañca "buddheḥ kāraṇaṃ bhave"yustadā "ko virodha indriyā" divat | indriyādayaḥ pratyekaṃ na buddherheturmilitāstu bhavanti tadvadaṇavopi syuḥ | na hi pareṣāmivāsmākañca nityaikasvabhāvā aṇavaḥ | te hi yathāpratyayamatīndriyāḥ santa aindriyā api syuḥ || (223)

{2.224}

[2.224,0]

nanu hetutvepi kathamaṇavo grāhyā ityāha |

[2.224,1]

"hetubhāvādṛte nānyā grāhyatā nāma kācana ||"

[2.224,2]

"hetubhāvadṛte vinā grāhyatā nāma" yā prasiddha sā nānyā "kācit" | api tu hetutaina grāhyatā |

[2.224,3]

evantarhīndriyādikamapi hetutvād grāhyaṃ syādityāha |

[2.224,4]

"tatra buddhiryadākārā tasyāstad grāhyamucyate || 224 ||"

[2.224,5]

"tatra" teṣu hetuṣu "buddhiryadākārā" bhavati "tasyā" buddhestad grāhya"mucyate" aṇusañcayaḥ | saiva ca buddhirākāramanukaroti nendriyādeḥ | (224)

{2.225}

[2.225,0]

"kathaṃ vā'vayavī grāhyaḥ sakṛt svāvayavaiḥ saha | na hi gopratyayo dṛṣṭaḥ sāsnādīnāmadarśane || 225 ||"

[2.225,1]

"tatkathaṃ" tadgrāhyaṃ | yopyāha | nānekaṃ "sakṛ"d gṛhyata iti | tanmate"'vayavī " sāsnākakudlāṅgūlādibhiḥ saha kathamvā grāhyo yuktaḥ | na gṛhyata eveti cet | "na hi go"ravayavinaḥ "pratyayaḥ"vayavā"nāmadarśane" kvāpi "dṛṣṭaḥ" | (225)

{2.226}

[2.226,0]

"guṇapradhānādhigamaḥ sahāpyabhimato yadi | sampūrṇāṅgo na gṛhyeta sakṛnnāpi guṇādimān || 226 ||"

[2.226,1]

"yadi sahāpyabhimato guṇa"pradhānayorviśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayora"dhigamo" nopādhīnāmanyonyaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhūtānāṃ dravyānāṃ vā tādṛśānāṃ | evantarhi viṣāṇī sāsnādimāniti vā yadā gṛhyate tadā tenaivāvayavena sambandhavyavasāyāditarāvayavasambandhānavasāyāt "saṃpūrṇāṅgo"'vayavī "na gṛhyeta | sakṛd" gṛhyate ca | "nāpi guṇā" gṛhyeta | viṣāṇī gauriti buddhyā viṣāṇaviśiṣṭo gaurviṣayīkṛto na tvanye guṇakarmasāmānyādayaḥ | tataśca nīlādirūpaṃ guṇaḥ parispandādi ca karmma | vastutvādi ca sāmānyaṃ na gṛhyeta | dṛṣṭaviruddhañcaitat | (226)

{2.227}

[2.227,0]

sarvveṣāṃ guṇakarmmasāmānyāvayavādīnāṃ vastuto viśeṣaṇatvāt "sarvvagrahaṇamiti" cet | āha |

[2.227,1]

"vivakṣā paratantratvāt viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ | yadaṅgabhāvenopāttantattenaiva hi gṛhyate || 227 ||"

[2.227,2]

"viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayorvvivakṣāparatantratvān" puruṣecchānurodhāt na pāramārthikatvaṃ | tathā viṣāṇī gauriti gorviṣāṇamityādau viparyayo viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyayoḥ prayokturicchāvaśena dṛśyate | tasmādyadeva "hyaṅgabhāvena" viśeṣaṇabhāvena svamanīṣikayā pratipādayitropāttaṃ "tenaiva" viśeṣaṇena viśiṣṭaṃ tadvivakṣitaṃ "gṛhyate" na taditaraiḥ | teṣāmavivakṣitatvenāvivakṣitatvāt | tataśca na saṃpūrṇṇāṅgo nāpi guṇādimān gṛhyeta | (227)

{2.228–2.229}

[2.228–2.229,0]

kiñca |

[2.228–2.229,1]

"svato vastvantarābhedād guṇāderbhedakasya ca | agrahādekabuddhiḥ syāt paśyatopi parāparam || 228 ||"

[2.228–2.229,2]

"guṇādibhedagrahaṇānnānātvapratipadyadi | astu nāma tathāpyeṣāṃ bhavet sambandhisaṃkaraḥ || 229 ||"

[2.228–2.229,3]

vastunaḥ "svato vastvantarād bhedābhāvāt" | vadanti hi svato hi na gaurnāgaurggotvayogāt gauḥ | tathā svato hi śuklo nāśuklaḥ śuklatvayogāt śukla ityādi | "bhedakasya ca guṇā"deragrahāt padārthaiḥ saha | tataśca "parāparama"rthajātaṃ "paśya"padārthatva"buddhiḥ syāt" | na hi dravyāṇāmanyonyasya bhedakā guṇajātyādayastaiḥsaha gṛhyante yena bhedabuddhiḥ syāt | dravye gṛhīte paścād guṇādīnāṃ bhedānāṃ viśeṣāṇāṃ nānātvagrahaṇaṃ dravyāṇāṃ yadīṣyate | "astu nāma" paścād guṇādigrahaṇaṃ | "tathāpyeṣāṃ" guṇakarmmasāmānyādīnāṃ "sambandhinaḥ sāṃkaryaṃ" syāt | svato hi dravyaṃ bhedānnopalabhyate | paścādupalabhyamānaistu guṇādibhiḥ saṃbandhitayāvagatairbhedena tad vyavasthāpanīyaṃ | tataścaikatraika dravye guṇādayaḥ sambandhitayā pratīyeran || bhinnadeśānāṃ guṇānāṃ bhinnadeśeṣu yojanānna sambandhisāṃkaryamiti cet | na | deśabhedasyāpi viśeṣaṇatvāt sopyekasyeti syāt | ekasya viruddhadharmāyogāt pratīyamānārthāḥ paścāt pratīyamānairūpādhibhirbhinnā vyavasthāpyanta iti cet | nanvevamapi svato'rthānāṃ bhedābhāvāt | bhedanibandhanaiścopādhibhiḥ saha vedanābhāvānnādhyakṣasiddhā bhedavyavasthitiḥ syāt | kintu viruddhopādhisambandhānyathānupapattyā kalpanīyā | tathā ca pratyakṣavirodhaḥ |

[2.228–2.229,4]

atha dṛṣṭerthe paścāttanamadhyakṣamupādhigrāhakaṃ tān yojayed bhedagrāhakaṃ | kathamadṛśyamāne yojanopādhīnāṃ pratyakṣakṛtā vikalpakṛtaiva tu syāt | tathā ca vyaktaṃ na bhedadarśanaṃ syāt | vikalpaviṣayasyāsphuṭatvāt | ṛṣṭe'rthe paścādupādhiḥ pratīyamānastasyaiva dṛṣṭa iti cet | tasyeti kimucyate | na tāvadanekāsūpādhigrahaṇāt pūrvvamanekatvasyāpratīteḥ | ekaṃ cet kathamupādhibhirbhedanīyaṃ | anavadhṛtaikānekabhāvaṃ vastumātraṃ taditi cet | tatra tarhi deśabhedādayopyupādhayaḥ paścādupalabhyamānā yojyante | tadanantaraṃ dṛṣṭatvāt tataścānivāryaḥ sambandhisaṃkaraprasaṅgaḥ | (228–229)

{2.230}

[2.230,0]

sāṃ khya matepi |

[2.230,1]

"śabdādīnāmanekatvāt siddhonekagrahaḥ sakṛt | sanniveśagrahāyogādagrahe sanniveśinām || 230 ||"

[2.230,2]

"śabdādīnāṃ" sukhaduḥkhamohātmakatayā anekatvāt śabdādigrahe "sakṛdanekagrahaḥ " | na hyaṅgulyagrahaṇe muṣṭigrahaṇaṃ | (230)

{2.231}

<ga. ka kalpanāpoḍhatve dharmadharmyādisaṃgatiḥ>

[2.231,0]

yadi pratyakṣamavikalpaṃ tadā kathaṃ dharmmadharmmyādigrahaṇamityāha |

[2.231,1]

"sarvato vinivṛttasya vinivṛttiryato yataḥ | tad bhedonnītabhedā sā dharmmiṇo'nekarūpatā || 231 ||"

[2.231,2]

"sarvvataḥ" parasmā"dvinivṛttasyā"rthasya "yato yataḥ" parasmā"dvinivṛttastairbhedai"rvyāvṛttibhirunnītā sā'"nekarūpatā" dharmmidharmmātmakatayā "dharmmiṇo"'rthasya | sarvvaṃto vyāvṛtte pratyakṣeṇa gṛhīte vastuni tadvyāvṛttyanukāriṇo vikalpāḥ pratyakṣadṛṣṭatvena dharmmidharmmabhāvaṃ vyavasthāpayantīti pratyakṣakṛtaḥ sa ucyate | na tu pratyakṣapratibhāsamānatvāt | (231)

{2.232}

[2.232,0]

tathā hi |

[2.232,1]

"te kalpitā rūpabhedād nirvvikalpasya cetasaḥ | na vicitrasya citrābhāḥ kādācitkasya gocaraḥ || 232 ||"

[2.232,2]

"te" dharmidharmādayo "rūpabhedād" buddhyākāraviśeṣā vijātīyavyāvṛttyāśrayeṇa "kalpitā" vicitrābhā vastubalabhāvitvāt "kādācitkasya vicitrasya" dharmmidharmmabhedapratibhāsarahitasya "nirvvikalpasya cetasaḥ" pratyakṣasya "na gocaraḥ" | pratyakṣaṃ hi vastusāmarthyotpannaṃ tadākāramanukuryāt na vikalpitaṃ | (232)

{2.233}

<kha śabdavikalpaviṣayaḥ sāmānyam>

[2.233,0]

bhavatu vā vastveva sāmānyaṃ tathāpi nāsau śabdavikalpaviṣaya ityāha |

[2.233,1]

"yadyapyasti sitatvādi yādṛgindriyagocaraḥ | na sobhidhīyate śabdairjñānayo rūpabhedataḥ || 233 ||"

[2.233,2]

"yadyapi sitatvādi" sāmānyamasti paṭādau dharmmiṇi "yādṛk" sitatvādiviśadākāra "indriyasya gocaraḥ | sa" indriyajñānagocaro'rtho'"bhidhīyate na śabdaiḥ | jñānayo"rindriyaśabdajanitayo "rūpa"syākārasya sphuṭāsphuṭatvena "bhedataḥ" (233)

{2.234}

[2.234,0]

"ekārthatvepi buddhīnāṃ nānāśrayatayā sa cet | śrotrādicittānīdānīṃ bhinnārthānīti tatkutaḥ || 234 ||"

[2.234,1]

"buddhīnā"mindriyaśabdajanitānā"mekārtha"tve ekaviṣayatve"pi nānāśrayatayā" kāraṇabhedā"tma"kasya ākārabheda"ścet | i"mevaṃ sthitau "śrotrā"dīndriya"cittāni""bhinnārthāni" śabdarūpagandhādibhinnaviṣayāṇīti vyapadiśyake | "tatkutaḥ" pramāṇādavadhāritaṃ | tānyapi citānyabhinnaviṣayatvepīndriyāṇāmāśrayabhūtānāṃ bhedād bhinnākārāṇīti kinna kalpyate | (234)

{2.235}

[2.235,0]

kiñca |

[2.235,1]

"jāto nāmāśrayonyonyaḥ cetasāṃ tasya vastunaḥ | ekasyaiva kuto rūpaṃ bhinnākārāvabhāsi tat || 235 ||"

[2.235,2]

"sāmānyādicetasāmāśrayaḥ" kāraṇamindriyaṃ śabdaśceti "anyonyo nāma jātaḥ" | tathā pi sāmānyāde"rvvastuna ekasyaiva rūpaṃ tatkuto bhinnākārāvabhāsi" sphuṭāsphuṭāvabhāsi sphuṭāsphuṭapratibhāsaṃ | na hi svarūpeṇa bhāsamānamekaṃ bhinnapratibhāsaṃ yuktam | (235)

{2.236}

[2.236,0]

yadapyucyate paraiḥ | śābdendriyajñānayoryādi naikaviṣayatvaṃ tadā viṣāṇādimantamarthaṃ gauriti śabdātpratītya kālāntare vyaktiviśeṣaṃ dṛṣṭavato'yamasau śabdāt prāṅmayā pratīto gauriti pratyabhijñānamekatādhyavasāyi yadutpadyate tanna syāditi | tatrāha |

[2.236,1]

"vṛtterdṛśyāparāmarśenābhidhānavikalpayoḥ | darśanāt pratyabhijñānaṃ gavādīnāṃ nivāritam || 236 ||"

[2.236,2]

"abhidhānavikalpa"yordṛ śyasyādhyakṣaviṣayasyā"parāmarśena" viṣayīkaraṇena "vṛtteḥ"paścād "darśanāt" sa evāyaṃ śabdanirdiṣṭo gauriti "pratya bhijñānaṃ gavādīnāṃ" yadiṣyate "tannivāritaṃ" boddhavyaṃ | indriyaśabdajñānayorbhinnākāratvenaiva viṣayattvābhāvāt kathaṃ tadekatāvyavasāyi vastuviṣayaṃ syāt | (236)

{2.237}

[2.237,0]

"anvayāccānumānaṃ yadabhidhānavikalpayoḥ | dṛśye gavādau jātyādestadapyetena dūṣitam || 237 ||"

[2.237,1]

yacca "dṛśye gavādā"vanekatrābhinnākārayora"bhidhānavikalpayoranvayādanuvṛtte"nābhidhānavikalpayordṛśyatvāparāmarśena hetunā "dūṣitaṃ" boddhavyaṃ | na hyanvayināvapi śabdavikalpau vastu spṛśataḥ | tatkathaṃ tābhyāṃ vastunaḥ sāmānyasya siddhiḥ | (237)

{2.238}

[2.238,0]

yadi nāsti sāmānyaṃ tathā kathamastu pratyabhijñānamityāha |

[2.238,1]

"darśanānyeva bhinnānyapyekāṃ kurvanti kalpanām | pratyabhijñānasaṃkhyātāṃ svabhāveneti varṇitam || 238 ||"

[2.238,2]

"darśanānī"ndriyajñā"nānyeva bhinnāni" nānākṣaṇaviṣayāṇyanekā"nyapi svabhāvena" pratyabhijñānakāraṇasvarūpeṇa svakāraṇaprasūtena kalpanātmekatvādhyavasāyinīṃ "pratya" pratyabhijñānanāmnā prasiddhāṃ "kurvantīti varṇṇitaṃ" prāk |

[2.238,3]

tasmātsthitametat pratyakṣamanirdeśyatvādavikalpamiti | uktamindriyapratyakṣaṃ || ḹḹ || (238)

{2.239}

<(2) mānasapratyakṣam>

[2.239,0]

mānasamākhyātumāha | taccendriyajñānānantaramiṣṭaṃ | tena sahaikaviṣayaṃ bhinnaviṣayaṃ vā syāt | ubhayathāpi tu doṣa ityāha |

[2.239,1]

"pūrvvānubhūtagrahaṇe mānasasyāpramāṇatā | adṛṣṭagrahaṇendhāderapi syādarthadarśanam || 239 ||"

[2.239,2]

"pūrvvānubhūta"syendriyajñānagṛhītasya "grahaṇe mānasasya" svīkriyamāṇe"'pramāṇatā" syāt | ajñātārthaprakāśasya pramāṇatvāt | indriyajñānā"dṛṣṭasya grahaṇe" punariṣyamāṇe"'ndhāderapi syādartha"sya rūpāde"rdarśanaṃ" | (239)

{2.240}

[2.240,0]

indriyajñānānubhūtaviṣayatvepi dvau vikalpau so'rthaḥ kṣaṇiko na vā |

[2.240,1]

"kṣaṇikatvādatītasya darśane ca na sambhavaḥ | vācyamakṣaṇikatve syāllakṣaṇaṃ saviśeṣaṇam || 240 ||"

[2.240,2]

prathamapakṣa indriyajñānaviṣayasyārthasya pūrvvakālasya sahabhuvo vā "kṣaṇika" naṣṭasya mānasena "darśane" darśanasya "ca na sambhavo"sti | "akṣaṇikatve" vā adhigatārthādhigantṛtvādapramāṇaṃ syāt | atha mānasamadhigatārthādhigantṛpramāṇamiṣyate tadāpi mānasasya "saviśeṣaṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vācyaṃ syāt" | yathādhigataviṣayatvepi "kalpanāpoḍhamabhrānta"(tasa.1214) mānasaṃ pratyakṣamiti | (240)

{2.241}

[2.241,0]

kiñca |

[2.241,1]

"niṣpāditakriye kiñcid viśeṣamasamādadhat | karmmaṇyaindriyamanyad vā sādhanaṃ kimitīṣyate || 241 ||"

[2.241,2]

"niṣpāditā kriyā" yasmin tatra "karmaṇi viśeṣaṃ kañcidasamādadhat aindriyami"ndriyajñāna"manyadvā" paraśvādi "sādhanaṃ kimitīṣyate" | kriyānirvvartanaṃ hi sādhanavyāpāraḥ | taccenniṣpannaṃ kimanyat kurvvattat sādhanaṃ syāt | (241)

{2.242}

[2.242,0]

api ca |

[2.242,1]

"sakṛd bhāvaśca sarvvāsāṃ dhiyāṃ tadbhāvajanmanām | anyairakāryabhedasya tadapekṣāvirodhataḥ || 242 ||"

[2.242,2]

tasmāt sthirād "bhāvājjanma" yāsāntāsāṃ "sarvvāsāṃ dhiyāṃ sakṛd bhāvaśca " | na kramabhāvaḥ | kramisahakāryapekṣayā krameṇa sthiropyarthaḥ karoti buddhīriti cet | ato"'nyaiḥ" sahakāribhira"kāryo bhedo" viśeṣo yasya sthiraikarūpasya tasya "tada" || (242)

{2.243}

[2.243,0]

yata evaṃ |

[2.243,1]

"tasmādindriyavijñānāntarapratyayodbhavaḥ | manonyameva gṛhṇāti viṣayaṃ nāndhadṛk tataḥ || 243 ||"

[2.243,2]

"tasmādindriyavijñāna"mevānantara"pratyaya"stasmā"dudbhavo" yasya ta"nmano" mānasaṃ pratyakṣaṃ | indriyapratyakṣagrāhya (ā) dviṣayā"danyameva viṣayaṃ gṛhṇāti | tata" indriyajñānajanyatvāt mānasasyāndhānāṃ cakṣurvvijñānavikalānāṃ dṛg darśanaṃ rūpasya na bhavati | gṛhītagrāhitvaṃ ca viṣayāntaragrahaṇādapāstaṃ | (243)

{2.244}

[2.244,0]

yadyanyaviṣayagrāhakaṃ mānasaṃ tadā bhūtabhaviṣyadgrāhakamapi syādityāha |

[2.244,1]

"svārthānvayārthāpekṣaiva heturindriyajā matiḥ | tatonyagrahaṇepyasya niyatagrāhyatā matā || 244 ||"

[2.244,2]

svārthaḥ svakīyo viṣayastasmāda"nvaya" utpādo yasyārthasya tada"pekṣaiva indriya"rmanovijñānasya "hetu"riṣyate | "tato'nya"sya viṣayasya "grahaṇepi" manovijñānasyeṣyamāṇe niyata indriyajñānagrāhyopādeyakṣaṇa eva grāhyo yasya tadbhāvo "niyatagrāhyatā " | (244)

{2.245}

[2.245,0]

nanu svajñānena svālambanajñānena ekakālikastulyakālikorthaḥ |

[2.245,1]

"tadatulyakriyākālaḥ kathaṃ svajñānakālikaḥ | sahakārī bhavedartha iti cedakṣacetasaḥ || 245 ||"

[2.245,2]

tena sahakārisammatendriyajñāne"nātulyaḥ kriyākālo" yasya bhinnakālatvātso'rthaḥ "sahakārī" katha"makṣacetaso bhavediti cet" | (245)

{2.246}

[2.246,0]

atrāha |

[2.246,1]

"asataḥ prāgasāmarthyāt paścāccānupayogataḥ | prāgbhāvaḥ sarvvahetūnāṃ nātorthaḥ svadhiyā saha || 246 ||"

[2.246,2]

kāryotpatteḥ prāgasatastatrāsā"marthyāt" | sadadhiṣṭhānaṃ hi "sāmarthyamasataḥ kathaṃ" syāt | kāryotpatteḥ "paścāt" sataḥ kāraṇavyāpārādvā paścāt kāryasamakālasya sato vā tatrā"nupayogato" vyāpārābhāvāt | kāryā"tprāgbhāvaḥ sarvvahetūnāmi"ti sthitaṃ | viṣayaśca jñānānāṃ nākāraṇamatiprasaṅgāt | "ato" viṣayaḥ kāraṇātmakaḥ "svadhiyā" svālambanadhiyā "saha na" bhavati | pūrvvabhāvitve ca viṣayasya tatkālendriyajñānasahakāritā yuktimatī | (246)

{2.247}

[2.247,0]

nanu |

[2.247,1]

"bhinnakālaṃ kathaṃ grāhyamiti ced grāhyatāṃ viduḥ | hetutvameva yuktijñā jñānākārārpaṇakṣamam || 247 ||"

[2.247,2]

prāgbhāvabhāvitvād "bhinnakālaṃ" vastu "kathaṃ grāhya"miti "cet | hetutvameva "sya svānurūpasyā"rpaṇakṣaṇaṃ grāhyatāṃ yuktijñā viduḥ" | na hi saṃdaṃśāyogolayoriva jñānapadārthayorgrāhyagrāhakabhāvaḥ | kathantarhi yadākāramanukaroti tat grāhyasya grāhakamityucyate | (247)

{2.248}

[2.248,0]

nanu yadi kāraṇaṃ grāhyaṃtadā samanantarapratyayādikaṃ ca tathā syāt | ityāhaṃ |

[2.248,1]

"kāryaṃ hyanekahetutve'pyanukurvvadudeti yat | tattenāpyatra tadrūpaṃ gṛhītamiti cocyate || 248 ||"

[2.248,2]

"kāryaṃ" hi jñānama"nekahetutve'pi" yatkāraṇamākāradvāreṇā"nukurvvadudeti" tatkāraṇamarpi tadrūpamuparopitasvākāraṃ "tena" kāraṇākāreṇa "gṛhītamiti cocyate" | yathā pitṛrūpaṃ putreṇa gṛhītamiti kathyate | uktaṃ "mānasaṃ" || ḹ ḹ || (248)

{2.249}

<(3) ka. svasaṃvedanapratyakṣam>

[2.249,0]

svasamvedanamākhyātumāha |

[2.249,1]

"aśakyasamayo hyātmā rāgādīnāmananyabhāk | teṣāmataḥ svasaṃvittirnnābhijalpānuṣaṅgiṇī || 249 ||"

[2.249,2]

rāgadveṣasukhaduḥkhādīnāṃ sarvvacittacaittānāmātmasaṃvedanaṃ pratyakṣamavikalpatvāt |

[2.249,3]

tathā hi | "rāgādīnāmātmā svarūpamananyabhāk" nānyaṃ bhajate | svarūpamātrāvasthiteḥ | tasmā"daśakyaḥ samayaḥ" saṃketo'smin "ataḥ" saṃketāviṣayatvāt "teṣāṃ" rāgādīnāṃ "sva"syātmanaḥ "samvittiḥ" prakāśo'"bhijalpo" vācakaśabdollekhasta"danu"ṣaṅgo yasyāsti sā tathā na bhavati | vācyaṃ hi vācakena saṃyojyeta | na ca rāgādyātmā vācyastatastatprakāśo na śabdasaṃgataḥ | (249)

{2.250}

[2.250,0]

"avedakāḥ parasyāpi te svarūpaṃ kathaṃ viduḥ |"

[2.250,1]

nanu rāgasukhādaya ātmaguṇāḥ"parasya" bāhyasyā"pyavedanā"ṅgajñātatvāt "te " | vedakasya kadācit svavedanaṃ saṃbhāvyeta | avedakaṃ ca na kvacidupayogi ||

[2.250,2]

yadi na svavedanā rāgādayastadā kathaṃ vedayanta ityāha |

[2.250,3]

"ekārthāśrayiṇā vedyā vijñāneneti kecana || 250 ||"

[2.250,4]

"ekortha" ātmā "āśrayo" rāgādibhiḥ saha yasyāsti "tenai"kārthāśrayiṇā "jñānena vedyā" rāgādaya "iti kecana nai" yā yi kā dayaḥ | (250)

{2.251}

[2.251,0]

atrāha |

[2.251,1]

"tadatadrūpiṇo bhāvastadatadrūpahetujāḥ | tatsukhādi kimajñānaṃ vijñānābhinnahetujam || 251 ||"

[2.251,2]

"tadrūpiṇo" vivakṣitaikarūpavanto'"tadrū"piṇa itararūpavanto bhāvā yathākramaṃ tadrūpād dṛṣṭaikarūpāddhetoḥ sāmagrīlakṣaṇājjātā "atadrūpahetujātā" vilakṣaṇasāmagrījātā bhavantīti tāvat sthitaṃ | tat tasmādimaṃ nyāyamullaṅdhya "vijñānena sahābhinna" eko "hetu"rindriyaviṣayamanaskārādisāmagrīlakṣaṇastasmā (t) jātaṃ "sukhādikaṃ" kasmādajñānaṃ samānasāmagrīprasūtatvāt dvayamapi jñānaṃ syānna vā kiñcit | (251)

{2.252}

[2.252,0]

abhinnahetukatāmeva samarthayitumāha |

[2.252,1]

"sārthe satīndriye yogye yathāsvamapi cetasi | dṛṣṭaṃ janma sukhādīnāṃ tattulyaṃ manasāmapi || 252 ||"

[2.252,2]

yasya yadātmīyaṃ janakaṃ tasmi"nnindriye sārthe" saviṣaye yogye kāryotpādanaṃ prati "cetasi" samanantarapratyaye sati "sukhādīnā"mapi "janma dṛṣṭaṃ" | tadyathāsvamindriyādiṣu yogyeṣu satsu janma darśanaṃ "mana"sāṃ jñānānā"mapi tulyaṃ" | atastulyahetukatvāt tulyajātīyataiva yuktā nānyathā kvacidekatā syāt | (252)

{2.253}

[2.253,0]

tulyahetukatvepi saṃskārāderniyāmakatvāt sukhādikamajñānaṃ syādityāha |

[2.253,1]

"asatsu satsu caiteṣu na janmājanma vā kvacit | dṛṣṭaṃ sukhāderbuddhervā tattato nānyataśca te || 253 ||"

[2.253,2]

"asa"tsvindriyādiṣu duḥkhāderbuddhervvā janma na kvacidiṣṭaṃ | "satsu" ca eteṣvi"ndriyā"diṣu ajanma vā "sukhāderbbuddhervvā na kvacid dṛṣṭaṃ" | tat tasmāt tata indriyāderdṛṣṭasāmarthyāt kāraṇāt te sukhabuddhī jāyete | "anyataḥ" saṃskārāde"rna te" tasya sāmarthyādarśanāt | (253)

{2.254}

<kha. sukhādiparavedyatānirasa>

[2.254,0]

nanvabhinnahetukatve sukhaduḥkhādibhedaśca na syādityāha |

[2.254,1]

[2.254,2]

"sukhaduḥkhādibhedaścā"vāntara"steṣāmi"ndriyādīnā"meva" hetūnāṃ "viśeṣato"'vāntarāt | "yathā tasyā buddhe"revāntarahetuviśeṣāt "māndyapāṭavasaṃśrayāḥ" parasparasaṃbhavino bhavanti | tasmāt sukhādayo vijñānenābhinnahetukatvādvijñānasvabhāvā evetisthitaṃ | (254)

{2.255}

[2.255,0]

[2.255,2]

"yasyārthasya" stryāde"rnipātena" sannidhānena "te dhīsukhādayo jātā"staṃ kāraṇabhūtamākārārpaṇakṣamaṃ "muktvā" sukhādīneva sahabhāvino viṣayalakṣaṇarahitān sā buddhiḥ "kathaṃ pratipadyeta" | akāraṇasya viṣayatvetiprasaṅgāt | (255)

{2.256}

[2.256,0]

"athe"ndriyajñānena viṣayagrahastadanantaraṃ mānasādhyakṣeṇa sukhādigraha iti "kramagrahe" svīkriyamāṇe tayorvviṣayasukhayoḥ "saṃvittiravicchinnā" yaugapadyena na "bhāseta" | asti ca yugapatpratibhāsaḥ parisphuṭaḥ | tayorbbāhyasukhagrāhimanasorlāghavāt yaugapadyapratibhāsa"ścet | ta"llāghavaṃ pratikṣaṇamekaikatvasaṃvedanābhāvasyāpi "tulyami" sāhityasya "kiṃ na bhavati" | (256)

[2.260,1]

tataśca kathamarthasukhayoḥ sahavedanaṃ | "arthena vinaiva cakṣurādi"bhiścakṣurādijñānaiḥ "sukhādīnāṃ" vedane cābhyupagamyamāne "stryāderbhedo" viśeṣo "rūpādiḥ" sukhaheturakṣṇā cakṣurjñānena na "kadācana gṛhyeta" | (260)

kasmādevamityāha |

[2.261,2]

"anta"raṅge sannihite "arthe" kṣetrajñasamavete sukhādau "śakte" svagrāhijñānotpādanakṣame sati na hi "bāhyadarśanī dhī"rarthagrāhiṇī yuktā | bahiraṅgo bāhyortha indriyālokādisahakāryapekṣaṇāt | sukhādistu na tatsāpekṣa iti tasmājjātā dhīstameva gṛhṇīyāt | indriyadhiyā"'rthagrahe" svīkriyamāṇe "sukhādīnāṃ" tajjānāmarthadarśanaprasūtānāma"rthamavedanaṃ syāt" | indriyabuddhirarthagraha evopayuktā tatkālamanyā ca dhīrnāsti paścāt jñānāntarakāle viṣayabalabhāvinaḥ sukhāderabhāva iti kathaṃ vedanaṃ | (261)

{2.262}

"tadvijñānamajñānasya" sukhaduḥkhāderu"pādānakāraṇaṃ" kena hetunā sammataṃ | samānajātīyaṃ kāraṇamupādānaṃ nānyat | na ca sukhādijñānāmiṣṭaṃ | jñānamajñānakārye ādhipatyaṃ sahakāritvaṃ kurvvīta | "tadā"dhipatyaṃ "viruddhepi" kārye dṛśyate | (264)

[2.266,1]

yasmādanyena sukhādīnāṃ vedanaṃ na ghaṭate | "tasmātsukhādayo" jñānātmānaḥ svasmin svarūpe pratibandhadvāreṇa "saṃkrāntāvabhāsana"śīlāśca ye"'rthānāṃ" teṣāṃ "vedakāḥ" | "ātmanaścā"parokṣatvādvedakāḥ | arthasarūpasyātmano'parokṣataiva arthavedanaṃ svavedanañca | na tvanyaḥ kaścid grahaṇaprakāraḥ | tata"ścaiṣāṃ" sukhādīnāmarthasarūpāṇā"marthebhyo janmaiva " grahītṛtvaṃ nāparaḥ kaścid vyāpāraḥ | (266)

{2.267}

[2.267,0]

[2.267,1]

ata evā"rthānubhavaḥ" kathaṃ svavedanamarthajñānayorbhedāt | tadvedanayośca bhedasya nyāyaprāptatvāditi bruvāṇaḥ pratikṣiptaḥ | tathā hi teṣāṃ sukhādīnā"marthātmā" arthākāraḥ pratibimbasaṃkrāntyā "svātmabhūtaḥ" svabhāvabhūta"staiḥ" sukhādibhi"ranubhūyate"'parokṣatvāt | tenopacāreṇārthasya parabhūtasya pratibimbahetoranubhavasya khyātiḥ prasiddhiḥ | tataśca jñānasyālambo'rthālambanaṃ tadābhatā arthākāratvaṃ vicāryamāṇamavaśiṣyate na tu pāramārthikamālamvyālambakatvaṃ nāma | (267)

{2.268}

<ga. svasaṃvedane sāṃkhyamatanirāsaḥ>

[2.268,0]

[2.268,2]

"kaścid bahiḥsthitāneva" na tvātmasamavāyinaḥ | pradhānapariṇāmajatvena sukhaduḥkhamohasvabhāvatvāt arthāna"pracetanāt" ātmana eva cetanatvād | buddhidarpaṇe jaḍātmani svacche'rthacetanayoḥ pratibimbasaṃkrāntidvāreṇa cchāyāpattyā cetanasya "grāhyā" mate "dvayasya" sukhasya nīlādeśca "sakṛd graho" niyamena "na yuktaḥ" | kadācidrūpanirapekṣamapi rūpasukhamanubhūyeta | (268)

kiñca |

yadi nīlādyeva sukhādyātmakaṃ tadā "tasya bāhyasya" sukhaduḥkhādyātmatayā'"viśeṣe" viśeṣābhāve rucyaruciviṣayatayā "bhāvanā"yāstā"ratamyataḥ | tāratamyañca buddhau " syāt | na hi grāhyāviśeṣe tajjñānaṃ viśiṣyate | (270)

{2.271}

"sukhādyātmatayā buddherapi yadyavirodhitā | sa idānīṃ kathaṃ bāhyaḥ sukhādyātmeti gamyate || 271 ||"

[2.271,1]

buddherapi pradhānapariṇāmarūpāyā bhāvanātāratamyāt sukhādyātmatāviśeṣād bāhyāviśeṣepi prītiparitāpatāratamyasyāvirodhiteṣyate | "yadi idānī"manyābhyupagame "bāhyo'rthaḥ" sa sukhādyātmeti kathaṃ gamyate | anubhūyamānaṃ sukhamanyatrāsaṃbhavad bāhye vyavasthāpanīyaṃ | (271)

{2.272}

[2.272,0]

"agrāhyagrāhakatvācced bhinnajātīyayoḥ pumān | agrāhakaḥ syāt sarvvasya tato hīyeta bhoktṛtā || 272 ||"

[2.272,1]

yadā tu buddhirapi sukhātmikā tadā kiṃ bāhyasukhakalpanayā | bāhyamahatorasukharūpatvācca "bhinnajātīyayorgrāhyagrāhakatvā"bhāvāt sukhādyātmatā bāhyasya gamyata iti cet | "pumān" cetano nirguṇatvādasukhādirūpo grāhyasyācetanasya sukhādyātmakasya sarvvasya bhinnajātīyatvāt "agrāhakaḥ" syāt | "tato"'grāhakatvāt "bhoktṛ" | anubhavitā hi bhoktocyate'nubhavābhāve kathaṃ bhoktā | (272)

{2.273}

[2.273,0]

"kāryakāraṇatānena pratyuktā'kāryakāraṇe | grāhyagrāhakatābhāvād bhāvenyatrāpi sā bhavet || 273 ||"

[2.273,1]

buddhisukhayorgrāhyagrāhakābhāvāt | nākāraṇaṃ viṣaya iti kāryakāraṇatā | tato grāhyasya sukhādyātmakatvāt tatkāryayā buddhyāpi sukhādyātmikayābhavitavyamiti parairuktā "kāryakāraṇatā" sānenātiprasaṅgena "pratyuktā" | tathā hi bhoktāpi "grāhaka" iti sa ca kāryasukhādyātmakaḥ kathaṃ "syāt" | api cākāryakāraṇe buddhisukhe | grāhyagrāhakatāyāḥ kāryakāraṇatānibandhanāyā abhāvāt | "grāhyagrāhaka"bhāvāt kāryakāraṇabhāvasya ca "bhāve"'bhyupagamyamāne"'nya"trātmaviṣayayorapi "sā" kāryakāraṇatā syāt | grāhyagrāhakatāyā bhāvāt | (273)

{2.274}

[2.274,0]

yasmātsukhāderbbāhyasya bhāvanātastāratamyānuyogayogaḥ |

[2.274,1]

"tasmātta āntarā eva,"

[2.274,2]

"tasmāda"sukhādaya "āntarā" jñānasvabhāvā abāhyā abhyupagantavyāḥ |

[2.274,3]

kiñca |

[2.274,4]

"samvedyatvācca cetanāḥ | saṃvedanaṃ na yad rūpaṃ na hi tattasya vedanam || 274 ||"

[2.274,5]

"samvedyatvācca hetoste cetanāḥ" | tathā hi samvedanaṃ tadrūpaṃ yadviṣayasvarūpaṃ na bhavati "tatsaṃvedanaṃ tasya" viṣayasya "vedanaṃ" yasmā"nna" bhavati | na hyaviṣayasvarūpaṃ prativiṣayaṃ bhedavyavasthāṃ karttumarhatīti sākāraṃ grāhakaṃ | tathā ca sākāraṃ jñānameva sukhamastu tadupadhāyakaṃ tu bāhyamayuktaṃ | bhāvanāviśeṣeṇa sukhādivedanasyāviśeṣadarśanāt | bāhyādhīnatve ca tadayogāt | (274)

{2.275}

[2.275,0]

syādetad |

[2.275,1]

"atatsvabhāvo'nubhavo bauddhāṃstān sannavaiti cet | muktvādhyakṣasmṛtākārāṃ saṃvittiṃ buddhiratra kā || 275 ||"

[2.275,2]

bhāvanātastāratamyayoginastān buddhyātmakasukhādīn "atatsvabhāvo"'sukhyādyākāro'"nubhavaḥ sannavaiti" pratyetīti"cet | saṃvittimadhyakṣā"kārāṃ harṣaviṣādākārāṃ "smṛtākārāma"tītasukhādikalpanārūpāṃ saumanasyalakṣaṇāṃ muktvā atra saṃvedanāvasare "kā" parā buddhiranubhūyate | yasyāḥ sukhādyātmakatvamadhyavasāyātmakatvañceṣyate | (275)

{2.276}

[2.276,0]

"tāṃstānarthānupādāya sukhaduḥkhādivedanam | ekamāvirbhavad dṛṣṭaṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ tvanyadantarā || 276 ||"

[2.276,1]

"tāṃstānarthāni"ṣṭānaniṣṭā"nupādāyā"śrityaikaṃ "sukhaduḥkhādivedanamāvirbhavad dṛṣṭaṃ" anyad buddhirūpa"mantarā" viṣayasaṃvedanayorantarāle "na dṛṣṭaṃ" | (276)

{2.277}

[2.277,0]

"saṃsargādavibhāgaścedayogolakavahnivat | bhedābhedavyavasthaivamucchinnā sarvavastuṣu || 277 ||"

[2.277,1]

buddhicetanayoḥ "saṃsarggādayogolakavahnyo"rivāvibhāgo bhedānupalabdhiriti "cet" | evaṃ bhinnākārānubhavepyabhedakalpanāyāṃ"sarvvavastuṣu bhedābhedavyavasthocchinnā" syāt | (277)

{2.278}

[2.278,0]

tathā hi |

[2.278,1]

"abhinnavedanasyaikyaṃ yannaivaṃ tad vibhedavat | sidhyedasādhanatvesya na siddhaṃ bhedasādhanam || 278 ||"

[2.278,2]

"abhinna"mekākāraṃ "vedanaṃ" yasya tasyaikyaṃ | "yannaivaṃ" bhinnavedanaṃ "tadvibheda vat " asyaikākārajñānasyābhedampra"tyasādhanatve" tadviparītabhinnākāravedanaṃ "bheda" || (278)

{2.279}

[2.279,0]

"bhinnābhaḥ sitaduḥkhādirabhinno buddhivedane | abhinnābhe vibhinne cet bhedābhedau kimāśrayau || 279 ||"

[2.279,1]

sāṃ khya sya tu sitaduḥkhādirbhinnākāro'bhinna iṣṭaḥ | "buddhivedane tvabhinnā" kiṃ nimittau te vyavasthāpanīyau | (279)

{2.280}

[2.280,0]

nanu vedanācetanāsaṃjñādīnāṃ caittānāṃ mahābhūmikādīnāṃ sakṛdutpannānāṃ bhedaḥ parasparaṃ pratīyate | atha cāsti | tadvadbuddhisukhayorapi syādityāha |

[2.280,1]

"tiraskṛtānāṃ paṭunāpyekadā'bhedadarśanāt | pravāhe vittibhedānāṃ siddhā bhedavyavasthitiḥ || 280 ||"

[2.280,2]

"paṭunā" sukhaduḥkhādīnāṃ vedanāskandhasaṃgṛhītena caittena "tiraskṛtānāma"bhibhūtānāṃ saṃjñādī"nāme"kadā'"bhedadarśanāt | pravāhe" citta santāne sukhādyabhāvakāle svarūpeṇopalakṣitānāṃ "bhedavyavasthitiḥ siddhā" | raverudaye tārakā anupalakṣitā api niśāyāmupalakṣyamāṇā bhedena vyavasthāpyanta eva | tasmājjñānātmānaḥ svavedanāśca sukhādaya ityākhyātaṃ svavedanaṃ || ḹ ḹ || (280)

{2.281}

<(4) yogijñānapratyakṣam>

[2.281,0]

yogijñānamākhyātumāha |

[2.281,1]

"prāguktaṃ yogināṃ jñānaṃ teṣāṃ tad bhāvanāmayam | vidhūtakalpanājālaṃ spaṣṭamevāvabhāsate || 281 ||"

[2.281,2]

"prāk" prathamaparicchede"yogināṃ jñānaṃ" sattyaviṣayamuktaṃ | "teṣāṃ" yogināṃ "bhāvanā" bhāvanāhetuniṣpattikaṃ "tat" jñānaṃ sattyasvarūpaviṣayatvena "vidhūtakalpanājālama"vikalpatvācca "spaṣṭaṃ" viśadajñeyākāra"mevāvabhāsate" | (281)

{2.282}

[2.282,0]

bhāvanābhavaṃ kathaṃ spaṣṭamityāha |

[2.282,1]

"kāmaśokabhayonmādacaurasvaprādyupaplutāḥ | abhūtānapi paśyanti puratovasthitāniva || 282 ||"

[2.282,2]

"kāmaśca" śokaśca bhayañca tairunmādāścaurasvapnādayaśceti "kāmaśokabhayonmāda" bhrāntāste"'bhūtānapya"rthān bhāvanāvaśāt "purato'vasthitā"| yasmāttadanurūpāṃ pravṛttiṃ ceṣṭante || (282)

{2.283}

[2.283,0]

bhavatu bhāvanājaṃ spaṣṭamavikalpaṃ tu kathamityāha |

[2.283,1]

"na vikalpānubaddhasyāsti sphuṭārthāvabhāsitā ||"

[2.283,2]

"na vikalpenānubaddhasya" saṃstutasya jñānasya "sphuṭārthāvabhāsitāsti" ||

[2.283,3]

nanu viplavavaśāt vikalpakamapi svapne spaṣṭābhaṃ jñānaṃ bhavatītyāha |

[2.283,4]

"svapnepi smaryate smārttaṃ na ca tattādṛgarthavat || 283 ||"

[2.283,5]

"svapnepi smārttaṃ" smaraṇaṃ kiñcidutpadyate | "na ca" tatprabodhāvasthāyāṃ "tādṛgartha"dṛśo nirvvikalpenānubhūto'rthastādṛśārthena yuktaṃ smaryate | kintarhi aspaṣṭārthameva svapnasmaraṇaṃ smaryate | (283)

{2.284}

[2.284,0]

nanvabhūtārthabhāvanābalajaṃ bhavatāpi spaṣṭābhamavikalpañca siddhānte neṣyate iti tena saha virodha ityā ha |

[2.284,1]

"aśubhā pṛthivīkṛtsnādyabhūtamapi varṇyate | spaṣṭābhaṃ nirvikalpañca bhāvanābalanirmitam || 284 ||"

[2.284,2]

"aśubhā" vinīlakavipūyakāsthisaṃkalādikā "pṛthvīkṛtsnādi" bhūmayatvādi "abhūta"masatyamapi "bhāvanābalena nirmitaṃ spaṣṭābhaṃ nirvvikalpakañcā"smā"bhirvvarṇṇyata" iti nāsti siddhāntavirodhaḥ | (284)

{2.285}

[2.285,0]

"tasmād bhūtamabhūtaṃ vā yad yadevābhibhāvyate | bhāvanāpariniṣpattau tat sphuṭākalpadhīphalaṃ || 285 ||"

[2.285,1]

yato bhāvanāyā bhāvyaspaṣṭatāyāmādhipatyaṃ | "tasmād bhūta"māryasatyādi "abhū"śubhādi "yadyadevā"tyantaṃ "bhāvyate" | tad bhāvyamānaṃ "bhāvanāyāḥ" sādaranirantaradīrghakālapravarttitāyāḥ "pariniṣpattau" sā phalaṃ yasya tattathā | (285)

{2.286}

[2.286,0]

"tatra pramāṇāṃ samvādi yat; prāṅ nirṇītavastuvat | tad bhāvanājaṃ pratyakṣamiṣṭaṃ śeṣā upaplavāḥ || 286 ||"

[2.286,1]

"tatra" bhāvanābalabhāviṣu spaṣṭānirvvikalpeṣu "yatsaṃvādi" upadarśitārthaprāpakaṃ tad bhāvanājaṃ pratyakṣaṃ "pramāṇamiṣṭaṃ" |

[2.286,2]

kimivetyāha |

[2.286,3]

"prāk" prathamaparicchede "nirṇṇītaṃ vastu" satyacatuṣṭayaṃ tasminniva | yathā āryasattyaviṣayaṃ bhāvanābalajaṃ saṃvāditvātpratyakṣaṃ pramāṇamevamanyadapīdṛśaṃ | "śeṣā" bhramā yathā aśubhā pṛthvīkṛtsnādipratyayāḥ | (286)

{2.287}

[2.287,0]

kalpanāpi svasaṃvittāviṣṭā nārthe vikalpanāditi vyākhyātumāha |

[2.287,1]

"śabdārthagrāhi yad yatra tajjñānaṃ tatra kalpanā | svarūpañca na śabdārthastatrādhyakṣamato'khilam || 287 ||"

[2.287,2]

"śabdārthagrāhi" anyavyavacchedasya grāhakaṃ "yajjñānaṃ yatra" viṣaye "tajjñānaṃ tatra kalpa" | jñānānāṃ "svarūpañca" svalakṣaṇātmakaṃ "na śabda"syā"rtho" viṣayo"'to" vācyatvā"ttatra svarūpe'khilaṃ" jñānamavikalpatvā"dadhyakṣaṃ" | uktaṃ caturvvidhaṃ pratyakṣaṃ || ḹ ḹ || (287)

{ii.vii}

<7. pratyakṣābhāsacintā>

{2.288}

[2.288,0]

pratyakṣābhāsamidānīṃ vaktavyaṃ |

[2.288,1]

"trividhaṃ kalpanājñānamāśrayopaplavodbhavam | avikalpakamekañca pratyajñābhaṃ caturvidham || 288 ||"

[2.288,2]

"trividhaṃ kalpanājñānaṃ" pratyakṣābhaṃ marīcikāyāṃ jalādhyavasāyi bhrāntijñānaṃ saṃvṛtau vi saṃvādivyavasāyasāṃvṛtajñānaṃ | pūrvvadṛṣṭaikatvakalpanāpravṛttaṃ liṅgānumeyādijñānaṃ | "avikalpakañca ekaṃ pratyakṣābhaṃ" | kīdṛśamā"śrayasye"ndriyasyo"paplavasti"mirā dyupaghātastasmā"d bhavo" yasya tattathā | evañca "caturvidhañca" pratyakṣābhāsaṃ || (288)

{2.289}

[2.289,0]

nanvavikalpakaṃ pratyakṣaṃ | tatastrayamapīdaṃ savikalpakatvādekaḥ pratyakṣābhāsaḥ | tat kiṃ bhrāntijñānaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇikāyāṃ jalāvasāyi | saṃvṛtisato dravyāderjñānaṃ | anumānaṃ liṅgajñānaṃ ānumānikaṃ liṅgijñānaṃ smārtta smṛtiḥ ābhilāpikaṃ ceti vikalpaprabheda ācārya di gnā ge nokta ityāha |

[2.289,1]

"anakṣajatvasiddhyarthamukte dve bhrāntidaśanāt || siddhānumādivacanaṃ sādhanāyaiva pūrvvayoḥ || 289 ||"

[2.289,2]

dve sāṃvṛtāropitayoḥ kalpanājñāne'"nakṣajatva"syānindriyatvasya "siddhyarthaṃ" bhede"nokte" | pareṣāṃ tayorakṣajatvabhrāntidarśanād | ghaṭoyaṃ dvau kampata ityādi | jalamidamiti ca vyavasāyātmaka"mindriyapratyakṣameva" pratipadyata iti paro manyate | tannirā sārthaṃ dvayorupādānaṃ | anindriyatvena smṛtibalabhāvitvena siddhaṃ ca tada"numādi" ca tasya "vacanaṃ pūrvvayoḥ" saṃvṛtāropitakalpanayorevā"nakṣajatvasādhanāya" | tathā hi yatpūrvvānubhūtasamayasmṛtibhāvi na tatpratyakṣaṃ | yathā'numānādi | anubhūtasamayasmṛtisāpekṣā cāvayavijalādikalpanā iti viruddhopalabdhiruktā | (289)

{2.290}

[2.290,0]

nanu sāṃvṛtāropitakalpanāyāḥ kathaṃ pratyakṣatāśaṅketyāha |

[2.290,1]

"saṃketasaṃśrayānyārthasamāropavikalpane | na pratyakṣānuvṛttitvāt kadācid bhrāntikāraṇam || 290 ||"

[2.290,2]

bahūnāṃ rūpādīnāmekārthakāritvakhyāpanārthaṃ ghaṭa ityādiśabdaniveśaḥ sa saṃśrayo heturyasyāḥ sā "saṃketasaṃśrayā"kalpanā dṛśyamānānmarīcinicayāderanyasya jalāderāropitasya kalpanā | "anyārtha"kalpanā | te ete kalpane pratyakṣānantarabhāvitvena "pratyakṣānuvṛttitvādā"tmanyapi "kadācida"vimarśakānāṃ pratyakṣatā — "bhrāntikāraṇaṃ" bhavataḥ | (290)

{2.291}

[2.291,0]

"yathaiveyaṃ parokṣārthakalpanā smaraṇātmikā | samayāpekṣiṇī nārthaṃ pratyakṣamadhyavasyati || 291 ||"

[2.291,1]

ato "yathaiveyama"numānānumānikādi"paro" pūrvvaṃ gṛhīta"samayāpekṣiṇī" satī "smaraṇā"dirūpā "pratyakṣaṃ" pratyakṣaviṣaya"marthaṃ nā""dhya""vasyati" | kintu kalpitameva gṛhṇāti | (291)

{2.292}

[2.292,0]

"tathānubhūtasmaraṇamantareṇa ghaṭādiṣu | na pratyayonuyaṃstacca pratyakṣāt parihīyate || 292 ||"

[2.292,1]

"tathā" saṃketakāle vyavahāralaghavārthaṃ kalpitasya dravyāderanu"mānabhūta"sya paścā"tsmaraṇamantareṇa ghaṭādiṣu" ghaṭo'yamityādyekavastvavasāyī "pratyayo" na bhavati | "tacca" saṃketitamāropitaṃ cārthamanuyan ghaṭo'yaṃ jalamiti ca pratyayaḥ "pratyakṣāt" pratyakṣa"tvāt " | tasya vastuviṣayatvāt saṃketāpekṣasya ca viparyayāt | (292)

{2.293}

[2.293,0]

"apavādaścaturthotra tenoktamupaghātajam | kevalantatra timiramupaghātopalakṣaṇam || 293 ||"

[2.293,1]

sataimiramiti "caturtho" hetvābhāsaḥ kalpanārahitatvenātiprasaktāyāḥ pratyakṣatāyā "apavādaḥ" | abhrāntatvasya lakṣaṇaikadeśatvopalakṣaṇatvaṃ ca na tu kalpanāpoḍhatvanirākṛtasyodāharaṇamidaṃ | "kevalaṃ sataimirami"tyatra timiraṃ sabāhyo"paghātasya" jñānavikṛtiheto"rupalakṣaṇaṃ" | tenānyendriyavikārajamindriyajañca nirvvikalpaṃ pratyakṣābhāsaṃ sidhyati || (293)

{2.294}

[2.294,0]

"mānasaṃ tadapītyeke teṣāṃ grantho virudhyate | nīladvicandrādidhiyāṃ heturakṣāṇyapītyayam || 294 ||"

[2.294,1]

"tad" dvicandrādijñāna"mapi mānasaṃ" manobhrama "ityeke" ā cā ryāḥ | "teṣā"mevaṃ vādināṃ "nīladvicandrādidhiyāmakṣāṇyapi hetu"rityetadarthavācako "grantho virudhyate | " punarayaṃ yāvaccakṣurādīnāmapyā"lambanatvaprasaṅgaḥ" | tepi hi paramārthato'nyathā vidyamānā nīlādyābhāsasya dvicandrādyābhāsasya ca jñānasya kāraṇībhavantīti | (294)

{2.295}

[2.295,0]

syādetat |

[2.295,1]

"pāramparyeṇa hetuścedindriyajñānagocare | vicāryamāṇe prastāvo mānasasyeha kīdṛśaḥ || 295 ||"

[2.295,2]

mānasasya pratyakṣasyendriyaṃ "pāramparyeṇa hetuḥ" | tena virodhābhāva"ścet" vā da vi dhi pra karaṇe "indriyajñāna"sya pratyakṣasya "gocare" vikalpasya ihāvasare kīdṛśaḥ "prastāvaḥ" | yena paramparayā taddheturindriyamucyate | (295)

{2.296}

[2.296,0]

"kimvaindriyaṃ yadakṣāṇāṃ bhāvābhāvānurodhi cet | tattulyaṃ vikriyāvaccet saiveyaṃ kiṃ niṣidhyate || 296 ||"

[2.296,1]

timirajñānaṃ bhramamanicchatopi "kiṃ" kīdṛśa"maindriya"jñānamiṣyate | "yadakṣāṇāṃ bhāvā" svabhāvābhyāmanuvartakaṃ tadaindriyamiti "cet" | tat indriya"bhāvābhā"vānurodhitvaṃ taimirikajñānasyāpi "tulyaṃ" | na hīndriyavyāpāramantareṇa taimirikajñānamutpadyate | indriyavikāreṇa vikriyāvat jñānamaindriyaṃ cet dvicandrādijñānānāṃ timirādīndriyavikāreṇa "vikriyā" | "saiveya"mabhūtārthopadarśanānmikā bhrāntatvanimittamuktā'smābhiḥ "kiṃ niṣidhyate" | (296)

{2.297}

[2.297,0]

"sarppādibhrāntivaccāsyāḥ syādakṣavikṛtāvapi | nivṛttirna nivartteta nivṛttepyakṣaviplave || 297 ||"

[2.297,1]

yadi ca dvicandrādidhīrmānasī bhrāntistadā sarpocitadeśe mandamandāloke rajvādau saṃsthānasāmyagrahāt utpannāyāḥ sarpādibhrānteriva marīciṣu jalabhrānteriva yathā pratyakṣaṃ vicārāt | asya(ā) dvicandrādibhrānterakṣa"vikṛtāvapi" sā nivṛttiḥ syāt | akṣaviplavo hi na tasyā hetuḥ | tataśca satyapi tasmin vimarśānnivartate sarpabuddhiriva | tathā hyakṣa"viplavepi" timirādau "nivṛttepi" tattvamavicārayato "na " taddvicandrabuddhiḥ | akṣaviplavasya tatkāraṇatvābhāvāt | akāraṇanivṛttau ca nivṛttyayogāt | (297)

{2.298}

[2.298,0]

kiñca |

[2.298,1]

"kadācidanyasantāne tathaivārpyeta vācakaiḥ | dṛṣṭasmṛtimapekṣeta na bhāseta parisphuṭam || 298 ||"

[2.298,2]

yathānubhavaṃ samadeśakālasyānyasya cittasantāne yathā ahirahirityupadarśanena sarpabhrāntirarpyate | "tathā" dvicandrādibhrāntirapi tasyā vācakaiḥ śabdaira"rpyeta" sāmagrītulyatvāt | timirasya cāhetukatvāt | api ca | yathā marīciṣu taraṅgajalasamāsu pūrvvadṛṣṭajalasmaraṇasāpekṣā jalabhrāntiḥ | tatra dvicandrādibhrāntirapi mānasītvāt "dṛṣṭa"candradvaya"smṛtimapekṣeta" | na ceyaṃ smaraṇasāpekṣā cakṣurvvisphāraṇamātreṇa spharaṇāt | tathā mānasītvāt "parisphuṭaṃ" suvyaktagrāhyākārā "na bhāseta" | jalādibhrāntiriva | (298)

{2.299}

[2.299,0]

"suptasya jāgrato vāpi yaiva dhīḥ sphuṭabhāsinī | sā nirvvikalpobhayathāpyanyathaiva vikalpikā || 299 ||"

[2.299,1]

tasmā"tsuptasya jāgratopi vā yaiva dhīḥ sphuṭāvabhāsinī" vyaktagrāhyākārā sā "nirvvikalpā"'bhyupagantavyā"anyathaiva" hyasphuṭāvabhāsinī dhīrubhayathā suptasya jāgrato pi vā "kalpikā" yuktā | (299)

{2.300}

[2.300,0]

yata evaṃ |

[2.300,1]

"tasmāttasyāvikalpepi prāmāṇyaṃ pratiṣidhyate | visaṃvādāttadarthaṃ ca pratyakṣābhaṃ dvidhoditam || 300 ||"

[2.300,2]

"tasmāt" kalpanāpoḍhamityukte timirajñānasyā"vikalpe" nirvvikalpatvepi sati "prāmāṇyaṃ" pratyakṣātmakaṃ prāptaṃ sataimiramityapavādena "visamvādāt pratiṣidhyate" | saṃvādalakṣaṇatvātprāmāṇyasya | "tadarthamu"paplutajñānanivṛttyartha cācārya diṅ nā ge na pratya "kṣābhaṃ" saṃkṣepato "dvidhoktaṃ" savikalpamavikalpañca | uktaṃ pratyakṣābhaṃ || ḹḹ || (300)

{ii.viii}

<8. pramāṇaphalacintā>

{2.301}

[2.301,0]

pramāṇaphalavyavasthāṃ kartumāha |

[2.301,1]

"kriyāsādhanamityeva sarvvaṃ sarvvasya karmmaṇaḥ | sādhanaṃ na hi tattasya sādhanaṃ yā kriyā yataḥ || 301 ||"

[2.301,2]

"kriyāyāḥ sādhanaṃ" heturi"tyeva na" hi "sarvvaṃ" kāraṇaṃ "sarvvasya karmmaṇaḥ" kriyāyāḥ "sādhanaṃ" karaṇaṃ | kintarhi tadvastu "tasya" karmaṇaḥ "sādhanaṃ" karaṇaṃ "yā kriyā yataḥ" padārthādavyavadhānena bhavati sa tasyāḥ kāraṇamucyate | tataścendriyādeḥ pramitiṃ pratyavyavahitasādhakatvābhāvāt na pramāṇaṃ | (301)

{2.302}

[2.302,0]

kintarhi pramāṇamastītyāha |

[2.302,1]

"tatrānubhavamātreṇa jñānasya sadṛśātmanaḥ | bhāvyantenātmanā yena pratikarmma vibhajyate || 302 ||"

[2.302,2]

"tatra" rūpādau karmaṇi "jñānasyānubhavamātreṇā"nubhavātmano "sadṛśātma"nastulyarūpasya"tenātmanā" svarūpeṇa prativiṣayaṃ vyatirekiṇā "bhāvyaṃ yena pratikarmma" prativiṣayajñānaṃ "vibhajyate" | nīlasyedaṃ pītasyedamiti | anyathānubhavamātratayā sarvvatra viṣaye sadṛśaṃ jñānaṃ prativiṣayaṃ kathaṃ bhedena vyavasthāpayituṃ śakyeta | (302)

{2.303}

[2.303,0]

syādetadindriyāderhetoḥ savyāpā ratādilakṣaṇo viśeṣo jñānānāṃ bhedena niyāmakamityāha |

[2.303,1]

"anātmabhūto bhedosya vidyamānopi hetuṣu | bhinne karmaṇyabhinnasya na bhedena niyāmakaḥ || 303 ||"

[2.303,2]

"hetu"ṣvindriyādiṣu "bhedo" viśeṣaḥ savyāpāratādilakṣaṇo "vidya" jñānasyānubhavamātrātmatayā bhinnasya "bhinne karmmaṇi" nīlādau grāhye "bhedena niyāmako" na yuktaḥ | kasmādityāha | "anātmabhūtaḥ" | jñānāsvarūpatvādindriyasya viśeṣaḥ pratikarmma na bhettumarhati | (303)

{2.304}

[2.304,0]

"tasmād yatosyātmabhedādasyādhigatirityayam | kriyāyāḥ karmaniyamaḥ siddhā sā tatprasādhanā || 304 ||"

[2.304,1]

"tasmādasya" jñānasyā"tmabhedāt yato'syā"rthasyeyama"dhigatiriti" kriyāyā adhigateḥ "karmaṇi" vedye "niyamaḥ sā kriyā tatprasādhanā" tatkaraṇā'bhyupagantavyā | (304)

{2.305}

[2.305,0]

syādetad | indriyādireva svabhedād bhedako jñānasya prativiṣayamadhigaterniyāmakaḥ | tataścānubhavātmatvādaviṣaya evāsiddha ityāha |

[2.305,1]

"arthena ghaṭayatyenāṃ na hi muktvārtharūpatām | anyaḥ svabhedājjñānasya bhedakopi kathañcana || 305 ||"

[2.305,2]

"enāma"dhigatima"rtharūpatā"marthasarū patāṃ "muktvā na" hyanyaḥ kaścindriyādiḥ "svabhedāt " kenāpi prakāreṇa "jñānasya bhedakopyartheva" jñeyena "ghaṭayati" yojayati nīlasyeyamadhigatiḥ pītasya ceyamityādi | tathā hi yadyapi pratyarthaṃ pratīndriyañca jñānānāmasti bhedaḥ tathāpi viṣayasārūpyābhāve sa eva viśeṣo'śakyanirdeśaḥ | atha viśeṣopyadhigatereva vyavasthāpyata iti cet | nanu tasyā eva vyavasthāpakamiṣyate | na cāvyasthite vyavasthāpake vyavasthāpyasiddhiḥ | nanu na sarvatra paraśuvyāpāradṛṣṭipūrvvikācchidāsiddhiḥ | chidādarśanādapi paraśuvyāpāravyavasthiteḥ | evamihāpyadhigatipūrvvikāyāṃ pramāṇasthitau na doṣaḥ | asamānametat | tathā hi paraśucchidayoḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvaviśeṣaḥ kriyākaraṇabhāvaḥ | adhigatijñānātmabhūtaviśeṣayostu vyavasthāpyavyavasthākabhāva eṣitavyaḥ | ubhayorapi jñānasvarūpātmatvāt | tatra kāraṇamajñātamapi svakāryaṃ nirvartayatīti kāryadarśa"nācca tadvyavasthā" yuktaiva | vyavasthāpakastu nānupalakṣito vyavasthāpya vyavasthāyāṃ kṣamate | na hyapratītaṃ kalpyamānaṃ āśvastyaṃvyavasthāpayati | (305)

{2.306}

[2.306,0]

"tasmātprameyādhigateḥ sādhanaṃ meyarūpatā | sādhane'nyatra tatkarmasambandho na prasidhyati || 306 ||"

[2.306,1]

"tasmātprameyādhigateḥ" phalabhūtāyāḥ vyavasthāpyāyāḥ "sādhanaṃ" pramāṇaṃ "meyarūpatā" | atha na sārūpyaṃ tasya prativiṣayaṃ bhinnasya sūpalakṣaṇatvāt sārūpyātpunara"nyatra sādhane " kriyāyāḥ "karmmasambandho" nīlasyeyamadhigatiḥ pītasya cetyādi "na sidhyati" | indriyādhigativiśeṣasya sambhavepyanubhavamātrātmakajñānasyāviśeṣakatvāyogāt | jñānagatasyāparaviśeṣasya lakṣaṇabhedenānupalakṣaṇāt | (306)

{2.307}

[2.307,0]

"sā ca tasyātmabhūtaiva tena nārthāntaraṃ phalam |"

[2.307,1]

"sā cā"dhigatiranubhavasvabhāvā jñānasyā"tmabhūtaiva | tena" pramāṇānnā"rthāntaraṃ phalaṃ" | prameyameva phalamityarthaḥ |

[2.307,2]

grāhyagrāhakabhāvopi bhākta eveti darśayitumāha |

[2.307,3]

"dadhānaṃ tacca tāmātmanyarthādhigamanātmanā || 307 ||"

[2.307,4]

"tacca" jñānamā"tmani" tāmartha"sarūpatāṃ dadhānaṃ" bibhrad arthasyā"dhiga manātmanā"'dhigamalakṣaṇena (307)

{2.308}

[2.308,0]

"savyāpāramivābhāti vyāpāreṇa svakarmaṇi | tadvaśāttadvyavasthānādakārakamapi svayam || 308 ||"

[2.308,1]

vyāpāreṇa savyāpāra"miva" svakarmmaṇi grāhye "ābhāti" | vyāpāramapi vastuto'kārakamapi svayaṃ tadvaśānmeyasārūpyavaśāttasyādhigamasya "vyavasthānāt" | (308)

{2.309}

[2.309,0]

"yathā phalasya hetūnāṃ sadṛśātmatayodbhavād | heturūpagraho loke'kriyāvatvepi kathyate || 309 ||"

[2.309,1]

"yathā lokepi hetūnāṃ sadṛśātmatayā" sadṛśarūpatayo"dbhavāt | phalasyākriyāvattvepi" heturūpagrahaṇavyāpārābhāvepi "heturūpagrahaḥ kathyate" pitū rūpaṃ gṛhītaṃ sutenetyādi | ato'rtharūpatāṃ muktvā'dhigatisādhanamanyadayuktaṃ | (309)

{2.310}

[2.310,0]

"ālocanākṣasambandhaviśeṣaṇadhiyāmataḥ | neṣṭamprāmāṇyameteṣāṃ vyavadhānāt kriyāmprati || 310 ||"

[2.310,1]

ata ā"locana"syārthālocanamātrasya jātyādiviśiṣṭaniścayaphalaṃ prati | "akṣasambandhasya" indriyārthasannikarṣasyālocanaphalaṃ prati "viśeṣaṇa"sya vedyaviśeṣyabuddhiphalaṃ prati "prāmāṇyaṃ" sādhanatvaṃ "neṣṭaṃ | eteṣā"mālocanārthasambandhaviśeṣaṇajñānānāṃ "kriyā"yāmadhigativiṣayasārūpyeṇa "vyavadhānāt" | (310)

{2.311}

[2.311,0]

vyavasthānepi sādhakatamatvaṃ syāditi cet | āha |

[2.311,1]

"sarveṣāmupayogepi kārakāṇāṃ kriyāmprati | yadantyaṃ bhedakaṃ tasyāstat sādhakatamaṃ matam || 311 ||"

[2.311,2]

"sarvveṣāṃ" sākṣātpāramparyeṇa "kriyāṃ pratyupayogepi" teṣu madhye "yatkāraka" kārakāntareṇāvyavahitavyāpyāraṃ sat kriyā"bhedakaṃ tattasyāḥ sādhakatamaṃ mataṃ" nānyat | (311)

{2.312}

[2.312,0]

tathā hi |

[2.312,1]

"sarvasāmānyahetutvādakṣāṇāmasti nedṛśam | tadbhedepi hyatadrūpasyāsyedamiti tatkutaḥ || 312 ||"

[2.312,2]

"akṣāṇāṃ" tāvadī"dṛśaṃ" sādhakatamatvaṃ "nāsti sarvvaṃ — sāmānyahetutvāt" | sarvvajñānasādhāraṇahetutvāt | avāntarādhigatibhedakatvānupapatteḥ | teṣāmindriyāṇāṃ pramādāvilatvādi"bhedepi" jñānasyātadrūpasya viṣayasārūpyarahitasya idamasya grāhakamiti grāhakatvaṃ yadiṣyate "tatkutaḥ" | (312)

{2.313}

[2.313,0]

"etena śeṣaṃ vyākhyātaṃ viśeṣaṇadhiyāṃ punaḥ | atādrupye na bhedopi tadvadanyadhiyopi vā || 313 ||"

[2.313,1]

"ete"nākṣāṇāmasādhanatvadarśanena "śeṣa"mālocanārthasambandhādi "vyākhyātaṃ" | tadapyarthasārūpyarahitamasādhanaṃ | sārūpye ca svīkartavye tadevāvyavahitatvāt sādhanamastu | "viśeṣaṇadhiyāṃ punara"yamadhiko doṣaḥ | "atādrūpye" viśeṣaṇasārūpyābhāve viśeṣyadhiyaḥ sakāśā"dbhedopi" na syāt | dvayorapyākārarahitatvena bhedasthityanupapatteḥ | tataścaikā pramāṇamanyā ca phalamiti kutaḥ | atha sārūpyaṃ viśeṣaṇadhiyo bhedakamiṣyate | evaṃ ca sati tadeva pramāṇaṃ phalaṃ ca syāt | arthasarūpatvādadhigatirūpatvācca | "tadvad" viśeṣaṇabuddheriva "anya" buddherviṣayasārūpyaṃ phalātmakañceṣyatāṃ | (313)

{2.314}

[2.314,0]

kiñca |

[2.314,1]

"neṣṭo viṣayabhedopi kriyāsādhanayordvayoḥ | ekārthatve dvayaṃ vyarthaṃ na ca syāt kramabhāvitā || 314 ||"

[2.314,2]

"kriyāsādhanayorviṣayabhedopi neṣṭaḥ" sarvvasya | na hyanyatra paraśuvyāpāraśchidā cānyatra | iha tu viśeṣaṇe pramāṇavyāpāraḥ kriyā ca viśeṣya iti bhinnaviṣayatā kathamiṣṭā |

[2.314,3]

athaitaddoṣatayā "dvayoḥ" kriyāsādhanayoḥ kramabhāvino"rekārthatve" ekaviṣayatve ca svīkriyamāṇe "dvayaṃ" bhinnaṃ pramāṇaṃ phalaṃ ca "vyarthaṃ" viśeṣaṇajñānaṃ pramāṇaṃ phalaṃ cāstu viṣayasvarūpatvādadhigamasvabhāvācca | tataḥ paraṃ tu viśeṣyajñānamadhigatādhigantṛtvādanupayuktaṃ | "na cai"kaviṣayayorjñānayoḥ "kramabhāvitā"sti viṣayasya tajjananaśaktasya krameṇa svakāryajananavirodhāt | (314)

{2.315}

[2.315,0]

sakṛdutpattāveva viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyadhiyoḥ pramāṇaphalatā bhaviṣyatīti cet | āha |

[2.315,1]

"sādhyasādhanatābhāvaḥ sakṛdbhāve;"

[2.315,2]

"sakṛd bhāve sādhyasādhanatāyāḥ abhāvaḥ" | kāryakāraṇabhāvaviśeṣatvena tasyā iṣṭatvāt |

[2.315,3]

nanvevamākārādhigamayorekajñānātmatvepi pramāṇaphalatā'nupapannetyāha |

[2.315,4]

"dhiyoṃśayoḥ | tadvyavasthāśrayatvena sādhyasādhanasaṃsthitiḥ || 315 ||"

[2.315,5]

"dhiyo'śaṃyo"rākārādhigamalakṣaṇayoḥ "sādhyasādhanasaṃsthitiḥ" kriyākaraṇavyavasthā | "tadvyavasthāśrayatve"nākāravaśenādhigativiśeṣavyavasthānāt | nāstyatra kāryakāraṇātmakaḥ kriyākaraṇabhāvaḥ kiṃ tu vyavasthāpyavyavasthāpakabhāvaḥ | sa ca tādātmyepyaviruddhaḥ | (315)

{2.316}

[2.316,0]

arthasannikarṣopi na pramāṇamityāha |

[2.316,1]

"sarvātmanāpi sambaddhaṃ kaiścidevāvagamyate | dharmaiḥ sa niyamo na syāt sambandhasyāviśeṣataḥ || 316 ||"

[2.316,2]

bāhyaṃ "sarvvātmanā" sarvvairākārairindriyādibhiḥ "sambaddhamapi kaiścideya dharmmai"rnīlatvādibhi"rggamyate" na tpaṇupuñjatvādibhiḥ | "sa eṣa" grahaṇasya "niya mo na syāt | ""ndha"syāpi gatisthitihetora"viśeṣataḥ" | (316)

{2.317}

[2.317,0]

"tadabhedepi bhedoyaṃ yasmāttasya pramāṇatā | saṃskārāccedatādrūpye na tasyāpyavyavasthiteḥ || 317 ||"

[2.317,1]

"yasmā"dindriyasannikarṣādeḥ prāmāṇyamayuktaṃ "tatta"smāda"bhedepi" sannikarṣādyaviśeṣepi yasmānniyāmakāt tajjñānasyā"yaṃ bhedo" nīlasyedaṃ jñānaṃ pītasya cedamityādi "tasya "tā yuktā | sa ca ākāra eveti sa eva pramāṇaṃ jñānajātajñānahetoḥ "saṃskārā"jjñānasya kaiścideva dharmairgrahaṇaniyama iti cet "na" | "tasya" saṃskārasyāpya"tādrūpye" viṣayāsarūpatve"'vyavasthiteḥ" | (317)

{2.318–2.319}

[2.318–2.319,0]

yadākāraṃ jñānaṃ syāttasyānubhavaḥ saṃskāraśca bhavet | tasmācca grahaṇapratiniyamaḥ | anubhavasthityabhāve tu sarvvamavyavasthitaṃ |

[2.318–2.319,1]

"kriyākaraṇayoraikyavirodha iti cedasat | dharmabhedābhyupagamād;"

[2.318–2.319,2]

"kriyākaraṇayo"radhigamākārayoraikātmye virodha "iti cet | asade"tat | "dharma"sya vyāvṛttyupakalpitasyā"bhyupagamāt" | anākāravyāvṛttiḥ pramāṇaṃ | anadhigativyāvṛttiśca phalamiti nānayoraikyaṃ |

[2.318–2.319,3]

kathantarhyuktaṃ | sā ca tasyātmabhūtaiva tena nārthāntaraṃ phalami(2 | 307)tyāha |

[2.318–2.319,4]

"vastvabhinnamitīṣyate || 318 ||"

[2.318–2.319,5]

paramārthato jñānātmakaṃ "vastvabhinnamitīṣyate" | (318) na tu kalpitadharmadvāreṇapi | kiṃ punastattvata eva sādhanād bhinnā'dhigatiśchi dādivanneṣyata ityāha |

[2.318–2.319,6]

"evaṃ prakārā sarvvaiva kriyākārakasaṃsthitiḥ | bhāvasya bhinnābhimateṣvapyāropeṇa vṛttitaḥ || 319 ||"

[2.318–2.319,7]

"sarvaiva kriyākāraka"yoḥ "saṃsthiti"rvyavasthā "evaṃprakārā" kalpitaiva "bhinnābhi" dāruparaśvādiṣu kriyākaraṇabhāvasyā"ropeṇa vṛttitaḥ" | na hi tatrāpi kāryakāraṇavastudvayavyatiriktā kriyāsti | dvidhābhūtaṃ kāṣṭhamevātadvyāvṛttyā bhedāntarapratikṣepeṇa chidetyucyate | tatkāraṇeṣu ca puruṣakaraparaśvādiṣu sāmagryantaravarttinaḥ karācchidāyāḥ anutpatteḥ paraśorasādhāraṇaṃ sahakāritvamupadarśayitumatadvyāvṛttyā karaṇavyapadeśaḥ | na tu kriyākaraṇatvamanyadeva kāryakaraṇābhyāṃ | adhigamākārayostu vyavasthāpyavyavasthāpakabhāvaḥ kriyākaraṇabhāvaḥ | yathā yaḥ kampate so'śva iti | uktā pramāṇaphalavyavasthā || ḹ ḹ || (319)

{ii.ix}

<9. vikṣaptimātratācintā>

<(1) arthasaṃvedanacintā>

<ka. arthasaṃvid>

{2.320}

[2.320,0]

idānīṃ yo gā cā ro vedyavedakabhāvamapaśyan sau trā nti kaṃ pṛ cchati |

[2.320,1]

"kārthasaṃvid;"

[2.320,2]

"kā'rthasya saṃvit" jñānamucyate |

[2.320,3]

ata āha |

[2.320,4]

"yadevedaṃ pratyakṣaṃ prativedanam |"

[2.320,5]

"yadevedaṃ pratyakṣa"manubhavasiddhaṃ "prativedanaṃ" nīlādyākāreṇa pratiniyataṃ vedanaṃ pratisantānaniyataṃ vā saivārthasaṃviducyate |

[2.320,6]

"tadarthavedanaṃ kena tādrūpyād vyabhicāri tat || 320 ||"

[2.320,7]

nanu "tat" pratiniyataṃ "vedana"manubhūyamānamarthaṃsya vedanaṃ "kena" hetunocyate svaprakāśātmakatvāt svavedanameva tadyuktaṃ nārthavedanaṃ | tasya sarvvadā parokṣatvāt | "tādrū"darthasarūpatvāt jñānamarthavedanamiti cet | tadarthasārūpyaṃ"vyabhi cāri", dvicandrakeśoṇḍūkajñānādyākārasyārthamantareṇāpi bhāvāt | (320)

{2.321}

[2.321,0]

"atha sonubhavaḥ kvāsya"

[2.321,1]

athānubhāvyābhāve "so'nubhavaḥ" pratyātmavedyo"'sya" jñānasya na karmmaṇi vyavasthāpanīyaḥ | na hi karmarahitā kriyā "kva"cidasti |

[2.321,2]

atrāha |

[2.321,3]

"tadevedaṃ vicāryate |"

[2.321,4]

yaducyate vyavahartṛ bhiridamanenānubhūyate iti "tadeveda"masmābhi"rvvicāryate" | jñānaṃ svaprakāśamupalabhyate prakāśaścocyata ityayuktaṃ |

[2.321,5]

yaccārthasārūpyamanubhavanibandhanamuktaṃ tadapyasambhavīti darśayannāha |

[2.321,6]

"sarūpayanti tat kena sthūlābhāsañca te'ṇavaḥ || 321 ||"

[2.321,7]

"te" parasparaṃ bhinnā "aṇavaḥ" tajjñānaṃ "sthūlābhāsaṃ" sthūlākāraṃ kena rūpeṇa sa"rūpa" | yadaṇusvarūpamasthūlamasti na tat jñānārūḍhaṃ | yacca jñānārūḍhaṃ sthaulyaṃ nāṇuṣu tadasti | (321)

{2.322}

[2.322,0]

"tannārtharūpatā tasya satyāṃrthāvyabhicāriṇī | tatsamvedanabhāvasya na samarthā prasādhane || 322 ||"

[2.322,1]

tasmāttulyajñānasya "nārtharūpatā"'sti | satyāṃ vārtharūpatāyāṃ vyabhicāriṇī sā dvicandrajñānādiṣu | tataśca "tatsaṃvedanabhāvasyā"rthasaṃvedanatvasya "pra"ṣu sā'rtharūpatā na "samarthā | na" kevalādarthasārūpyādarthasaṃvedanatvaṃ yena vyabhicāraḥ syāt | kintarhi sārūpyatadutpattibhyāṃ | te ca dvicandrajñānādīnāṃ na staḥ | candradvayasyābhāvāt tadutpatterayogāt | (322)

{2.323}

[2.323,0]

etadevāha |

[2.323,1]

"tatsārūpyatadutpattī yadi samvedyalakṣaṇam | samvedyaṃ syāt samānārthaṃ vijñānaṃ samanantaram || 323 ||"

[2.323,2]

"tena" grāhyeṇa "sārūpyaṃ tasmādutpattiḥ" sva"samvedya"sya "lakṣaṇaṃ" yadi saṃmataṃ tadāpi "samanantaraṃ jñāna"muttarajñānena "samānārthaṃ" samānagrāhyaṃ "saṃvedyaṃ syāt" | tatsarūpatadutpattyoḥ saṃbhavāt | (323)

{2.324}

<kha. dṛśyadarśane pratyāsattivicāraḥ>

[2.324,0]

syādetat |

[2.324,1]

"idaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śrutamvedamiti yatrāvasāyadhīḥ | sa tasyānubhavaḥ;"

[2.324,2]

sārūpyatadutpattimattvepīdaṃ "dṛṣṭaṃ śrutamvedamiti yatrāvasāyadhī"rutpadyate "tasya " nānyasya | na ca samanantarapratyaye dṛṣṭaśrutādyavasāyo bhavati tanna grāhyo'sau |

[2.324,3]

atrāha |

[2.324,4]

"saiva pratyāsattirvvicāryate || 324 ||"

[2.324,5]

dṛśyadarśanayoḥ "saiva" pratyāsatti"rvvicāryate"'smābhiḥ | (324)

{2.325}

[2.325,0]

"dṛśyadarśanayoryena tasya tad darśanammatam | tayoḥ sambandhamāśritya draṣṭureṣa viniścayaḥ || 325 ||"

[2.325,1]

"yena" pratyāsattisambhavena "tasya" bāhyasya tajjñānaṃ "darśanaṃ mataṃ | tayordṛ śyadarśanayoḥ " pratyāsattimā"śritya draṣṭuḥ" puruṣa"syedaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ vedamityarthaniścayaḥ" | tatsārūpyatadutpattilakṣaṇā ca pratyāsattiḥ samanantarapratyayepi samāneti tannibandhano dṛṣṭaśrutādhyavasāya(o) pi tatra syādityarthaḥ | (325)

{2.326}

[2.326,0]

"ātmā sa tasyānubhavaḥ sa ca nānyasya kasyacit | pratyakṣaprativedyatvamapi tasya tadātmatā || 326 ||"

[2.326,1]

tasmādvedyarahitastasya jñānasya sa nīlādirūpa ātmā"nubhavaḥ | sa cānubhavo " bāhyasya | "tasya" jñānasya "pratyakṣaprativedyatvamapi" yaducyate | sā tadātmatā'parokṣānubhavātmatā | (326)

{2.327}

[2.327,0]

"nānyonubhāvyastenāsti tasya nānubhavoparaḥ | tasyāpi tulyacodyatvāt svayaṃ saiva prakāśate || 327 ||"

[2.327,1]

yathā ca svarūpāda"nyo" buddhyā "anubhāvyo nāsti" | tathā "tasya" jñānasya cāparo'"nubhavo nāsti" | tasyajñānagrahaṇa syāpi "tulyārthacodyatvāt" | sa hyanyatvanibandhano grāhyagrāhakabhāvaḥ | taccānupapannamityuktaṃ | tattasmāttat jñānamaparokṣatayotpannaṃ "svayaṃ prakāśate" | nānyena prakāśyate | (327)

{2.328}

<ga. nīlādyanubhavaprasiddhiḥ>

[2.328,0]

kathaṃ tarhi nīlādyanubhavaprasiddhirityāha |

[2.328,1]

"nīlādirūpastasyāsau svabhāvonubhavaśca saḥ || nīlādyanubhavāt khyātaḥ svarūpānubhavopi san || 328 ||"

[2.328,2]

tasya jñānasya nīlādirūpo'sau svabhāvo'nubhavaḥ prakāśātmakaśca saḥ | tena svarūpānubhavopi sannīlādyanubhavot tathā saṃprasiddhiḥ | (328)

{2.329}

[2.329,0]

"prakāśamānastādātmyāt svarūpasya prakāśakaḥ | yathā prakāśobhimatastathā dhīrātmavedinī || 329 ||"

[2.329,1]

"yathā prakāśastādātmyāt" prakāśātmakatvāt paranirapekṣaḥ "prakāśamānaḥ " paranirapekṣā prakāśātmanotpannā prakāśamānā'"tmavedinīti" upacārāducyate | (329)

{2.330}

[2.330,0]

"tasyāścārthāntare vedye durghaṭau vedyavedakau | avedyavedakākārā; yathā bhrāntairnirīkṣyate || 330 ||"

[2.330,1]

"vibhaktalakṣaṇagrāhyagrāhakākāraviplavā |"

[2.330,2]

cakāro hetau | yasmā"ttasyā" dhiyo'"rthāntare vedye vedyavedakākārau durghaṭau" | tasmād vastuto'"vedyavedakākārā" sā buddhirnīlaprakāśātmanotpannā tathā prakāśate | na tu tatra kaścid grāhyasya grāhakasya cākāraḥ samasti | kathaṃ tarhi grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsavyavasāyāvityāha | "bhrāntai"raprahīṇadvayavāsanāviplavai"ryathā vibhakta" yasyāḥ sā tādṛśī "nirīkṣyate " | (330)

{2.331}

<gha. grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsavyavasāyaḥ>

[2.331,0]

"tathā kṛtavyavastheyaṃ keśādijñānabhedavat || 331 ||"

[2.331,1]

"tathā" grāhyagrāhakabhedena "kṛtavyavasthā" sa nīlādibahirdeśaṃ grāhyamāntarañca saṃvedanaṃ grāhakamiti viplava eṣa "keśādijñānabhedavat" | na hi keśoṇḍūkajñānaviśeṣasya grāhakavad grāhyaḥ keśāvayavosti | kiṃ tarhi keśābhāsaḥ prakāśa eva kevalaḥ | (331)

{2.332}

[2.332,0]

"yadā tadā na saṃcodyagrāhyagrāhakalakṣaṇī | tadānyasamvidobhāvāt svasamvit phalamiṣyate || 332 ||"

[2.332,1]

viplavavaśācca grāhyagrāhakabhedena buddhi"ryadā" vyavasthāpyate "tadā na saṃ codya""grāhyagrāhakalakṣaṇā sā" | na hi vastuto grāhyagrāhakabhāvaḥ sambhavati | na ca viplavavaśādvastuvyavasthā keśadvicandrāderapi tattvaprasaṅgāt | yadā ca na grāhyagrāhakatā vijñaptimātratāyāṃ "tadānya"sya grāhyasya "saṃvido" jñānasyā"bhāvāt svasaṃvit phalami" | (332)

{2.333}

<ṅa. bāhyārthanirāsaḥ>

[2.333,0]

"yadi bāhyonubhūyeta ko doṣo naiva kaścana | idameva kimuktaṃ syāt sa bāhyorthonubhūyate || 333 ||"

[2.333,1]

nanu "yadi bāhyo'rtho" jñānenā"nubhūyate" tadā "ko doṣaḥ" | yena svasaṃvit phalamiṣyate |

[2.333,2]

āha | yadyanubhūyate tadā "naiva kaścana" doṣaḥ | anubhava eva tu bāhyasya nāstītyucyate | tathā "idameva kimuktaṃ syāt " iti(333 | )

{2.334}

[2.334,0]

"yadi buddhistadākārā sāstyākāraviśeṣiṇī | sā bāhyādanyato veti vicāramidamarhati || 334 ||"

[2.334,1]

"yadi buddhistadākārā" vā bāhyasarūpetyucyate | satyamasti "sā buddhirākāra" nīlānīlādyākāraviśeṣayuktā | kiṃtu sā buddhi"rbbāhyāda"rthājjāyetā"nyato" vāsanāpratiniyamā"dvā iti vicāramidamarhati" | na tāvad buddhivyatirekiṇā'rthaḥ kaściddhetutayopalabhyate | buddhisvarūpamātravedanāt | kādācitkatayā tu kāraṇaṃ tasyāḥ kiñcid vyavasthāpanīyaṃ tacca bāhyaṃ vāsanā vā syāt ubhayathāpyupapatteḥ | (334)

{2.335}

[2.335,0]

"darśanopādhirahitasyāgrahāttadgrahe grahād | darśanaṃ nīlanirbhāsaṃ;"

[2.335,1]

tatra "darśanena" jñāneno"pādhi"nā viśeṣaṇena "rahitasya" nīlādera"grahāt" tasya grahe ca nīlasya "grahāt" sahaiva nīladhiyorvvedanāt "darśanaṃ nīlādinirbhāsaṃ" nīlākāraṃ "vyavasthitaṃ" | yattāvat nīlādikaṃ bāhyamityucyate | tajjñānena sahopalambhaniyamāt tadabhinnasvabhāvaṃ dvica ndrādivat |

[2.335,2]

kastarhi nāstītyāha |

[2.335,3]

"nārtho bāhyosti kevalam || 335 ||"

[2.335,4]

"bāhyo" nīlādi"rarthaḥ kevalaṃ nāsti" | tatsādhakatvenābhimatasyādhyakṣasyāsāmarthyāt | (335)

{2.336}

[2.336,0]

evantarhi jñānasya gajādyākārasyālokādinimittāntarasadbhāvepi deśakālādipratiniyamadarśanāt artho vyavasyatītyāha |

[2.336,1]

"kasyacit kiñcidevāntarvvāsanāyāḥ prabodhakam | tato dhiyāmviniyamo na bāhyārthavyapekṣayā || 336 ||"

[2.336,2]

"kasyacijjñā"nasya gajādyākārasya "kiñcideva" jñānama"ntarvvāsanāyāḥ" samanantarapratyayāntara"varttinyā" niyatajñānajananayogyatālakṣaṇāyāḥ "prabodhakaṃ" kāryotpādanābhimukhyakārakaṃ | "tataḥ" prabodhakavaśāt "dhiyāṃ" niyatākāratayā "viniyamaḥ | na bāhyārtha" | ko hi viśeṣo bāhyo vā niyāmakaḥ pratibhāsasya prabuddhavāsanāviśeṣaḥ samanantarapratyayo vā | tatra vāsanāyāḥ sāmarthyaṃ svapnādāvupalabdhaṃ | na tu bāhyasya nityaparokṣatvāt | na tathāpi parokṣasya bāhyasya sādhakasyābhāvepi nābhāvasthitiriti cet | pratibhāsamānaṃ jñānaṃ bāhyaṃ tu na pratibhāsata eveti tāvataivābhimatasiddheḥ | sādhakapramāṇarahitapiśācāyamānabahirarthaniṣedhenāsmākamādaraḥ | yadi tu tanniṣedhanirbbandho garīyān sāṃśatvānaṃśatvakalpanayā paramāṇupratiṣedhe ā cā ryī yaḥ paryeśitavyaḥ | (336)

{2.337}

<ca. vijñānadvairūpyam>

[2.337,0]

yasmād bāhyo'rtho "nānubhūyate tasmā"dekaṃ vijñānaṃ avidyopaplutatvāt "dvirūpaṃ" bodharūpaṃ nīlādirūpañcā"sti" | yat yasmājjñānamevaṃ dvyākāratayā'nubhūyate svavedanena yathānubhavaṃ kālāntare "smaryate ca" | yathā cānyasya saṃvedanābhāvāt | "ubhayādyākārasya" nīlādyanubhavarūpasya "saṃvedanaṃ phalaṃ" | tadevaṃ prameyo grāhyākāraḥ pramāṇaṃ grāhakākāraḥphalaṃ svasaṃviditi darśitaṃ bhavati | (337)

{2.338}

<cha. arthasaṃvitphalam>

[2.338,0]

{2.339}

[2.339,0]

[2.339,2]

{2.340}

[2.340,0]

[2.340,1]

bahirarthanayepi buddhivedanasyaivārthavedanatvāt tathā "yadīṣṭākā"ro'syā buddherā"tmā"niṣṭākāro vā | tadā "tena" jñānene"ṣṭo'niṣṭo vārthaḥ pravedito bhava"ti nānyathā | (340)

{2.341}

[2.341,0]

[2.341,1]

yasmā"dvidyamānepi bāhye'rthe yathānubhava"manubhavākārānatikrameṇa sa bāhyo'rtho "niścitātmā" vyavasthāpyate nārtha"svarūpeṇa" | yathā sambhavinā niścitātmā vyavatiṣṭhate | iṣṭāniṣṭatvena puruṣābhyāmekasyārthasya grahaṇāda"nekātmatvadoṣaḥ" prasajyate | (341)

{2.342–2.343}

[2.342–2.343,0]

"yadi bāhyaṃ na vidyeta kasya saṃvedanaṃ bhavet | yadyagatyā svarūpasya bāhyasyaiva na kiṃ matam ||"

[2.342–2.343,1]

anekātmakatvasyā"bhyupāye" svīkārepi"dvayoḥ" puruṣayo"rbhedene"ṣṭatvenaikasyānyasya cāniṣṭatve"nānubhavo na syāt" | dvyākāratvādvastunastathaiva pratītiprasaktiḥ | adṛṣṭena sukhaduḥkhavedanīyena karmaṇāvaraṇāt | dvitīyasyākārasya ekātmatvena pratibhāsaḥ syāditi cet | evaṃ satyartha"vaśā gati"rjñānamiti nāma prasiddhaṃ na syāt | adṛṣṭavaśeneṣṭāniṣṭākārayoḥ pratīterupadarśanāt | (342–343)

{2.344}

[2.344,0]

kiñca |

[2.344,1]

[2.344,2]

bhāvama"nekātmakamekātmakatve"naikākāratayā darśa"yadadṛṣṭaṃ tatkathamarthasya darśakaṃ nāma " | tadeva hi darśakamasya yat tatsvarūpaṃ pratibhāsayati | na caikākāro'rthaḥ | tatastatpratītirnārthapratītiḥ | (344)

{2.345}

{2.347}

{2.348}

<ja. ātmasaṃvidevārthasaṃcid>

[2.348,0]

[2.348,1]

"yasmā"tkāraṇa"dyathā" iṣṭatvenāniṣṭatvena vārthasyātmākāraḥ "pratyaye niviṣṭa"stathā'rthoṃ niścīyate tasmādarthākāraḥ pramāṇaṃ | "asā"varthākāra evamiṣṭāniṣṭatvena buddhau "niviṣṭa" ityātmasaṃvidaḥ svasaṃvedanā"nniścīyate" | (348)

{2.349}

[2.349,0]

"ityarthasaṃvit saiveṣṭā yatorthātmā na dṛśyate | tasmād buddhiniveśyārthaḥ sādhanaṃ tasya sā kriyā || 349 ||"

[2.349,1]

iti tasmāt saivātmasaṃvida"rthasaṃvidiṣṭā | yataḥ" svarūpād bahirbhūto"'rthātmā na " buddhyākāra eva tu vedyate | atastadvedanadarśanamevārthavedanaṃ | yasmāccārthasārūpyavaśenārthādhigativyavasthā "tasmā"d "buddhi"nive"śyārtho"'rthapratibimbaṃ "sādhanaṃ" pramāṇaṃ "tasya" pramāṇasya "sā"dhigatiḥ "kriyā" phalamiṣyate | (349)

{2.350}

[2.350,0]

"yathā niviśate sortho yataḥ sā prathate tathā | arthasthitestadātmatvāt svavidapyarthavinmatā || 350 ||"

[2.350,1]

yataḥ kāraṇāt "yathārtho" jñānātmani "niviśate" tathā sā svasaṃvittiḥ prathate khyāti | tasmādarthasya sthiteradhigatestadātmatvāt paramārthataḥ"svavi" satī "arthavid matā" | svasaṃvedanamevārthavedanamupacārāducyata iti tādātmyamanayoḥ | (350)

{2.351}

[2.351,0]

"tasmād viṣayabhedopi na;"

[2.351,1]

yasmādarthākāra eva pramāṇaṃ pratītisādhanatvāt phalañca pratīyamānaṃ "tasmā"tpramāṇaphalayo"rvviṣayabhedopi" nāsti | yathā paramate ālocanaviśeṣaṇajñānādīnāmekārthāpekṣiṇyāveva hi sārūpyapratipattī pramāṇaphalatvaṃ pratilabhete |

[2.351,2]

yadyarthasaṃvedanaṃ phalaṃ tadā svavitphalaṃ kathamuktamityāha |

[2.351,3]

[2.351,4]

arthasaṃvedaṃnasya vastutaḥ "svabhāvacintāyāṃ" svasaṃvedanaṃ phala"muktaṃ | arthasaṃvidastā""dātmyāt"svasaṃvedanātmatvāt | na svākārapratīteranyāstyarthapratītiḥ svarūpeṇa tasyāḥ pratīteḥ | (351)

{2.352}

[2.352,0]

nanu yadi yathārthaṃ nānubhavastadā svavāsanāprabodhakamanuvartamānasya jñānasyārthoṃbāhyostītyetadeva kuta ityāha |

[2.352,1]

"tathāvabhāsamānasya tādṛśo'nyādṛśopi vā | jñānasya heturarthopītyarthasyeṣṭā prameyatā || 352 ||"

[2.352,2]

"tathā" iṣṭāniṣṭākāreṇā"vabhāsamānasya jñānasyā"rtho"pi tādṛśo"nyādṛśo vā heturityarthasya "prameyateṣṭā" sau trā nti ka mate | sārūpyasya paramārthataḥ sarūpa(2 | 321) iti pratiṣedhāt | (352)

{2.353}

[2.353,0]

"yathā kathañcittasyārtharūpaṃ muktvāvabhāsinaḥ | arthagrahaḥ kathaṃ;"

[2.353,1]

yadi sārūpyābhāvastadā tasya jñānasyāvabhāsino "yathā kathañci"diṣṭāniṣṭādinā bhāsamānamartharūpamarthākāraṃ muktvā "kathaṃ" kena prakāreṇārthasya "grahaḥ" syāt | na hyarthaḥ svarūpeṇa dṛśyate | tat svarūpabuddhivedanādarthagrahavyavasthā | sārūpyameva cenna saṃbhavati kathamarthagraha iti manyate sau trā nti kaḥ

[2.353,2]

yo gā cā ra stu tasya sāhāyyakaṃ manyamāna āha |

[2.353,3]

"satyaṃ na jānehamapodṛśam || 353 ||"

[2.353,4]

"satyaṃ na jāne'hamapīdṛśamarthagrahaḥ" kathamiti | (353)

{2.354}

[2.354,0]

kathaṃ tarhyasatyarthe grāhyagrāhakaphalabheda ityāha |

[2.354,1]

"avibhāgopi buddhyātmaviparyāsitadarśanaiḥ | grāhyagrāhakasaṃvittibhedavāniva lakṣyate || 354 ||"

[2.354,2]

paramārthato"'vibhā"go bhedarahito"pi buddhyātmadva"yavāsanayā "viparyāsitaṃ" vibhāgenopa"darśitaṃ" darśanaṃ yeṣāṃ tairatattvadarśipuruṣai"rgrāhyagrāhakasaṃvittī"nāṃ parasparaṃ bhedastadvāniva lakṣyate | (354)

{2.355}

[2.355,0]

atra dṛṣṭāntamāha |

[2.355,1]

"mantrādyupaplutākṣāṇāṃ yathā mṛcchakalādayaḥ | anyathaivāvabhāsante tadrūparahitā api || 355 ||"

[2.355,2]

"yathā mūcchakalādayo mantrādibhirupapluta"yathārthajñānahetukṛta"makṣaṃ" yeṣāṃ teṣāmanyathā suvarṇṇāditve"naivāvabhāsante" | tena suvarṇṇādinā rūpeṇa "rahitā api" vastutaḥ | (355)

{2.356}

[2.356,0]

kasmātpunarmmantrādisāmarthyāt suvarṇṇāditāmeva yātaṃ mṛtkhaṇḍamiti nābhyupagamyate ityāha |

[2.356,1]

"tathaivādarśanātteṣāmanupaplutacakṣuṣām | dūre yathā vā maruṣu mahānalpopi dṛśyate || 356 ||"

[2.356,2]

"mantrādi"nā'nupaplutacakṣuṣānyena puṃsā teṣāṃ mṛcchakalādīnāṃ yathopahatākṣeṇa te dṛśyante "tathaiva darśanāt" mṛdātmatvenaiva darśanāt suvarṇṇāditvena niṣpattikalpanamayuktaṃ | "yathā maruṣu dūre'lpopi mahān dṛśyate" taddeśasthairalpatvenaiva bhātasya darśanāt | (356)

{2.357}

[2.357,0]

"yathānudarśanañceyaṃ meyamānaphalasthitiḥ | kriyate'vidyamānāpi grāhyagrāhakasaṃvidām || 357 ||"

[2.357,1]

tasmād "grāhyagrāhakasaṃvidāṃ" paramārthato"'vidyamānāpi meyamānaphalasthitiryathā"te | grāhyākāro meyaḥ grāhakākāro mānaṃ saṃvittiḥ phalamiti vyavasthāpyate | (357)

{2.358}

[2.358,0]

"anyathaikasya bhāvasya nānārūpāvabhāsinaḥ | satyaṃ kathaṃ syurākārāstadekatvasya hānitaḥ || 358 ||"

[2.358,1]

"anyathā" yadi vastuto grāhakādivibhāga iṣyate ta"daikasya bhāvasya" jñānātmano "nānārūpāvabhāsino"'nekākārapratibhāsavanta ākārā grāhyādikāḥ "kathaṃ satyaṃ " | tasyaikajñānātmana "ekatvasya hānitaḥ" | na hyekaṃ pratibhāsamānānekākārātmakaṃ bhavitumarhati | pratibhāsena sarvveṣāṃ bhedena vyavasthāpanāt | (358)

{2.359}

[2.359,0]

anekameva tarhi jñānaṃ paricchedāditvena syādityāha |

[2.359,1]

"anyasyānyatvahāneśca ;"

[2.359,2]

na cānekaṃ jñānaṃ ekameveṣṭavyaṃ | vastuto bhinnasyābhede iṣyamāṇe grāhyādeḥ parasparato"'nyasyānyatvahāneḥ" | yadā hi bhedapratibhāsepyekatvamiṣṭaṃ tadā bheda eva na vyavasthitaḥ | tataśca sukhaduḥkhādayo nīlapītādayaśca parasparaṃ na bhidyeran | pratibhāsabhedasya tatsādhanatvāt | anyasya ca tatsādhanasyābhāvāt |

[2.359,3]

evantarhyekaṃ tāvat jñānaṃ nānākāraṃ syāditi śaṅkāyāṃ nakāraṃ kākākṣivat saṃbandhayannāha |

[2.359,4]

"nābhedo rūpadarśanāt | rūpābhedepi paśyantī dhīrabhedaṃ vyavasyati || 359 ||"

[2.359,5]

"nābhedo" jñānasyābhibuddhasya "rūpa"syāda"rśanāt" | rūpābhedañcādrayādau "paśya" dhīrabhedaṃ "vyavasyati" | na ca grāhyagrāhakādiṣu bhinnābhāseṣvabhedapratibhāsaḥ | (359)

{2.360}

[2.360,0]

tasyād |

[2.360,1]

"bhāvā yena nirūpyante tadrūpaṃ nāsti tattvataḥ | yasmādekamanekaṃ ca rūpaṃ teṣāṃ na vidyate || 360 ||"

[2.360,2]

"bhāvā" grāhyādayo "yena" rūpeṇa grāhyatvādinā "nirūpyante" anubhūyante "tadrūpaṃ tattvata"steṣāṃ "nāsti | yasmādekaṃ" rūpa"manekañca rūpaṃ teṣāṃ na vidyate" | vastubhavadekamanekaṃ vā syāt | na ca grāhyādyābhā eko'neko vā yuktaḥ | tasmāduppalava evāyaṃ | (360)

{2.361–2.363}

[2.361–2.363,0]

nanu |

[2.361–2.363,1]

"sādharmyadarśanālloke bhrāntirnāmopajāyate | atadātmani tādātmyavyavasāyenā neha tat || 361 ||"

[2.361–2.363,2]

"adarśanājjagatyasminnekasyāpi tadātmanaḥ ||"

[2.361–2.363,3]

"loke sādharmyadarśanādatadātmani tādātmyavyavasāyena bhrāntirvvi"tathākārā buddhi"rjāyate" iti nāma prasiddhaṃ | "iha" vijñaptinaye tat sādharmyadarśanaṃ "nā"sti | (361) "ekasyāpi tadātmano"'bhūtākārasya "jagatyadarśanāt" |

[2.361–2.363,4]

atrāha |

[2.361–2.363,5]

"astīyamapi yā tvantarupaplavasamudbhavā || 362 ||"

[2.361–2.363,6]

"doṣodbhavā prakṛtyā sā vitathapratibhāsinī | anapekṣitasādharmyadṛgādistaimirādivat || 363 ||"

[2.361–2.363,7]

sādharmyadarśanādyā mānasī bhrānti"riyamapyasti | yā punarantarupaplavasamudbhavā" avidyāprabhavā sā prakṛtyā doṣodbhavā | avidyā timirādihetukā vitathapratibhāsinyabhūtākārā anapekṣitasādharmyadṛgādistaimirādivat | yathā timirajñānamindriyadoṣādanapekṣitasādharmyameva jāyate tathā grāhyādibhrāntirapītyarthaḥ, jāyamānameva hi jñānaṃ vāsanāsāmarthyādanubhavānanubhavatvenāntarbbahirdeśatvena sukhādi nīlādi darśayati | evaṃ tarhi bahirarthopadarśanaśaktameva svadarśanahetubalāt kasmānneṣyata jñānamiti cet | na | svapnādāvavidyāyā asadgrāhyākāropadarśanasāmarthyopalabdheḥ | ākārātiriktabahirarthasyādarśanānna jñānasya tadupadarśanasāmarthyakalpanā nyāyyetyāstāṃ tāvadidaṃ || (362–363)

{2.364}

<bha. vijñaptimātratāyāṃ pramāṇaphalavyavasthā>

[2.364,0]

vijñaptimātratāyāṃ pramāṇaphalavyavasthāpanārthamāha |

[2.364,1]

"tatra buddheḥ paricchedo grāhakākārasammataḥ | tadātmyādātmavittasya sa tasya sādhanaṃ tataḥ || 364 ||"

[2.364,2]

"tatra" vijñaptimātratāyāṃ "buddheḥ" sagrāhakākāraḥ "saṃmataḥ pariccheda" ākāra "ātma" tasya grāhakākārasya phalaṃ | "tādātmyāt" paricchedasvabhāvatvāt "svasaṃvittiḥ " paricchedātmaka eva hi grāhakākāraḥ sa eva cātmavedanaṃ | "tataḥ" paricchedavaśenātmavedanavyavasthānāt | sa pariccheda"stasyā"tmavidaḥ phalabhūtāyāḥ "sādhanaṃ" pramāṇaṃ | (364)

{2.365}

[2.365,0]

"tatrātmaviṣaye māne yathā rāgādivedanam | iyaṃ sarvvatra saṃyojyā mānameyaphalasthitiḥ || 365 ||"

[2.365,1]

"tatra" evaṃ satyā"tmaviṣaye māne" svasaṃvedane pramāṇe "yathā rāgādivedanaṃ" mānameyaphalātmakaṃ | "iyaṃ mānameyaphalasthitiḥ" sarvvatra vijñaptinayepi saṃyojyā | (365)

{2.366}

[2.366,0]

tathā hi |

[2.366,1]

"tatrāpyanubhavātmatvātte yogyā svātmasaṃvidi | iti sā yogyatā mānamātmā meyaḥ phalaṃ svavit || 366 ||"

[2.366,2]

"tatrāpi" rāgādivedanepi "te" rāgādayo'"nubhavātmatvāt svā"tmanaḥ "saṃvidi " tasmāt "sā" svavedana"yogyatā" rāgādīnāṃ "mānamātmā meyaḥ phalaṃ svavit" | (366)

{2.367}

[2.367,0]

nanu rāgādiṣṭātmasaṃvedanaṃ phalabhūtaṃ mānayuktamiha tu grāhakākāro yogyatālakṣaṇaṃ pramāṇamucyata iti vyāhatamiti śaṅkāyāmuttaraṃ |

[2.367,1]

"grāhakākārasaṃkhyātā paricchedātmatātmani | sā yogyateti ca proktaṃ pramāṇaṃ svātmavedanam || 367 ||"

[2.367,2]

yā "grāhakākārasaṃkhyātā paricchedātmatā sā'tmani" saṃvedane "yogyatā ceti" tasmādrāgādiṣu "svā" phalabhūtamiha vivakṣitaṃ kintu yogyatā | tasmādabhinnārthataiva | (367)

{2.368}

[2.368,0]

nanu svābhāsaṃ tāvadastu jñānaṃ paricchedasvabhāvatvāt | viṣayābhāsaṃ tu kathaṃ | yathā viṣayaṃ kāraṇaṃ tathā cakṣurādirapīti tadākāratāpi syādityāha |

[2.368,1]

"sarvvameva hi vijñānaṃ viṣayebhyaḥ samudbhavad | tadanyasyāpi hetutve kathañcid viṣayākṛti || 368 ||"

[2.368,2]

"sarvameva hi jñānaṃ viṣayebhyaḥ samudbhavadu"tpadyamānaṃ tebhyo viṣayebhyo'nyasyendriyāderapi hetutve kathañcit svakāraṇāyātaviṣayagataśaktibhedā"dviṣayākṛti" bhavati nendriyādyākāraṃ | (368)

{2.369}

[2.369,0]

"yathaivāhārakālāderhetutve'patyajanmani | pitrostadekasyākāraṃ dhatte nānyasya kasyacit || 369 ||"

[2.369,1]

"yathaivāpatyajanmani" pitrormātā"pitrorāhārakālāde"śca hetutvepi tadekasya pitrormmadhye ekasya piturmmāturvvā"kāra"mapatyaṃ "dhatte'nyasyā"hārakālādeśca "kasya" na | (369)

{2.370}

[2.370,0]

"taddhetutvena tulyepi tadanyairviṣaye matam | viṣayatvaṃ tadaṃśena tadabhāve na tad bhavet || 370 ||"

[2.370,1]

yata evaṃ "tat" tasmāt tato viṣayādanyairindriyādibhi"rhetutvena tulye" sadṛśepi viṣaye rūpādau "viṣayatvaṃ" grāhyatvaṃ tena svākārārpakatvenāṃ"śena" viśeṣaṇaṃ "mataṃ" | yasmādākārārpakatvaṃ viṣayalakṣaṇamavasthitaṃ | tasmāttasyākārārpakatvasyābhāve tadviṣayatvamindriyādiṣu "na bhavet" | (370)

{2.371}

[2.371,0]

kiñca |

[2.371,1]

"anarthākāraśaṅkā syādapyarthavati cetasi | atītārthagrahe siddhe dvirūpatvātmavedane || 371 ||"

[2.371,2]

"arthavati cetasyanarthākāra"tā arthākārarahitatā śaṅkā "syādapi" dṛśyamānasyākārasyārthatvenaiva sambhāvyamānatvāt | "atīta"syā"rthasya grahe" vikalpātmake tvarthasyābhā vāt | arthābhāsatayā ca "dvirūpatvaṃ" tathā cāparokṣatvādā"tmasaṃvedanaṃ" ceti dve apyastu siddhe | na hyasannevārtho dṛśyate | tato'rthākāratā sā jñānasyaiva tathārthena ca parokṣatvābhāvāt svābhāsañca tat | na cānyena jñānena tad vedyate | vedyavedakabhāvasya niṣiddhatvāt | ataḥ svavedanameva tat | (371)

{2.372}

<ba. sāmānyasya nityānityatvapratiṣedhaḥ>

[2.372,0]

syādetad | atītā vyaktirasattvānna vikalpaviṣayo jātisyu sattvāt syādityāha |

[2.372,1]

"nīlādyābhāsabheditvānnārtho jātiratadvatī | sā vānityā na jātiḥ syānnityā vā janikā katham || 372 ||"

[2.372,2]

atītavikalpasya "nīlādyābhāsabheditvāt" varṇṇasaṃsthānādyākāraviśeṣavattvāt "na jātiratadvatī" varṇṇādyākārarahitārtherviṣayaḥ | kiñca | jātirvviṣayībhavantī anityā vā bhavet nityā vā | "sā cānityā jātirna syāt" nityalakṣaṇatvāttasyāḥ "nityā" vā buddhe"rjanikā kathaṃ" syāt | (372)

{2.373}

[2.373,0]

nityasya kramayaugapadyābhyāṃ virahāt || nāmanimitte viprayuktaḥ saṃskāro viṣayaścedityāha |

[2.373,1]

"nāmādikaṃ niṣiddhaṃ prāṅ nāyamarthavatāṃ kramaḥ | icchāmātrānurodhitvādarthaśaktirna sidhyati || 373 ||"

[2.373,2]

"nāmādikaṃ" viṣayatvena "niṣiddhaṃ prāk"(2 | 11)nāmādivacane vaktṛśrotṛvācyānu(2 | 11) tyādinā | kiñcā"rthavatāṃ" saviṣayāṇāṃ cakṣurvvijñānādīnā"mayaṃ "'rthasāmarthyena vinotpāda iti nāsti | manovijñānānāṃ tvarthasannidhānānapekṣāṇā"micchāmātrānurodhitvāt" janikā"rtha" | na cāheturarthī grāhyo'tiprasaṅgāt | (373)

{2.374}

<(2) stṛticintā>

[2.374,0]

bhavatvatītārthalambanaṃ vijñānaṃ viṣayākāramanubhavastu mā bhūdityāha |

[2.374,1]

"smṛtiścedṛgvidhaṃ jñānaṃ tasyāścānubhavādbhavaḥ | sa cārthākārarahitaḥ sedānīṃ tadvatī katham || 374 ||"

[2.374,2]

"īdṛgvidhama"tītavikalpanātmakaṃ "jñānañca" smṛtiḥ | "tasyāścānubhavād bhava" utpādaḥ | na hyanubhavamantareṇa smṛtiḥ | "sa cā"nubhavo bhavanmate"'rthākārarahitaḥ | "masminnabhyupagame sā smṛti"stadvatya"rthākāravatī "kathama"stu | yadyanubhavārūḍho nārthākāraḥ kathamasau viditaḥ | aviditasya kā smṛtiḥ | (374)

{2.375}

<ka. nārthāt smṛtiḥ>

[2.375,0]

arthātsmṛtirutpadyata iti cet | āha |

[2.375,1]

"nārthād bhāvastadābhāvāt syāttathānubhavepi saḥ | ākāraḥ sa ca nārthasya spaṣṭākāravivekataḥ || 375 ||"

[2.375,2]

"nārthād bhāva"stasyā"stadā" smṛtikāle"'bhāvā"datītārthasya | yathā cārthādutpadyamānāyāḥ smṛterarthākāro bhavati | "tathānubhavepya"rthādutpadyamāne "so'rthākāraḥ" syāt | api ca smṛtyārūḍhaḥ "so'"spaṣṭa"ścā"kāro "nārtha"syānubhavārūḍhāt "spaṣṭādarthākārād " bhedāt | (375)

{2.376}

[2.376,0]

"vyatiriktaṃ tadākāraṃ pratīyādaparastathā | nityamātmani sambandhe pratīyāt kathitañca na || 376 ||"

[2.376,1]

yadi ca buddhivyatirikto'rtha eva manovijñānagrāhyastadā buddhe"rvyatiriktame"kena vikalpyamāna"ntadākāramaparo"pi yogyadeśasthaḥ pramā na pratīyāt | paropalabhyatāṃ niṣeddhuṃ "nityamātmanyasya" vikalpyasyārthasya "sambandhe" vā svīkriyamāṇe yadā svayamanucintayituṃ parasmai kathyate tadā kathañcit paro na "pratīyāt" | pratyeti ca "kathitaṃ" (376)

{2.377}

[2.377,0]

"ekaikenābhisambandhe pratisandhirna yujyate | ekārthābhiniveśātmā pravaktṛśrotṛcetasoḥ || 377 ||"

[2.377,1]

pratītyartha"mekenaikena" vaktrā śrotrā ca bhinnasya bhinnasya arthasyā"bhisambandhe"'trāpi svīkrimāṇe "pravaktṛśrotṛcetasoḥ pratisandhirekārthābhiniveśāt" yadevānena kathitaṃ tadeva mayā pratītaṃ yadeva mayā kathitaṃ tadevānena jñātamityabhinnārthādhyavasāyarūpo "na yujyate" | (377)

{2.378}

[2.378,0]

"tadekavyavahāraścet sādṛśyādatadābhayoḥ | bhinnātmārthaḥ kathaṃ grāhyastadā syāddhīranarthikā || 378 ||"

[2.378,1]

vaktṛśrotṛsambandhinostayorarthayore"kavyavahāra" ekatvāvasāyaḥ "sādṛśyāccet" | tadubhayadarśane sādṛśyaṃ na cātra darśanaṃ | bhavatu vā tathāpi atadābhayo"rbhinnātma"sambandhārthāpratibhāsinorvvaktṛśrotṛ cetaso"rbhinnātmā'rthaḥ kathaṃ grāhyaḥ" | yadā cārthābhedo nāsti "tadā"'bhinnārthādhyavasāyinī "dhī"rvvaktṛśrotro"ranarthikā syāt" | yathārthaṃ buddherabhāvāt | yathābuddhi cārthābhāvāt | (378)

{2.379}

[2.379,0]

bhavatu tāvadevaṃ smṛtirvviṣayākārā'nubhavajñānaṃ tvanākṛti syādityāha |

[2.379,1]

"taccānubhavavijñānenuobhayāṃśāvalaṃbinā | ekākāraviśeṣeṇa tajjñānenānubudhyate || 379 ||"

[2.379,2]

"taccānubha"viṣayeṇa smaraṇenānuba dhyate'nugamyate smaryate iti yāvat |

[2.379,3]

kīdṛśeno"bhayāṃśāvalambinā" jñeyaprācīnajñānagataviṣayākārānubhavarūpadharmadvayaviṣayeṇa | katha"manubadhyata" ityāha |

[2.379,4]

"eka"smādavivādasiddhādanubhavā"kārādviśeṃṣo" viṣayākārastena smaraṇajñānena hi vijñānamaryākārānubhavākāraviśiṣṭameva smaryate | tatastādṛśameva tat | (379)

{2.380}

[2.380,0]

"anyathā hyatathārūpaṃ kathaṃ jñānedhirohati | ekākārottaraṃ jñānaṃ tathā hyuttaramuttaram || 380 ||"

[2.380,1]

anyathā'tathārūpamākāradvayarahitamanubhavajñānaṃ svagrāhiṇi smaraṇajñāne "kathaṃ" dvyākāramadhirohati | adhirūḍhaṃ ca | tato dvyākāraṃ tat | tathā "jñānamuttaramuttaraṃ" buddhipūrvvajñānālambana"mekākārottara"mekenaikenākāreṇādhikaṃ pratīyate | arthejñānena tadālambaka eko'rthākāraḥ pratīyate | tadālambanenatu viṣayabhūtajñānākārastadālambakaśca svākāraḥ | (380)

{2.381}

[2.381,0]

"tasyārtharūpeṇākārāvātmākāraśca kaścana | dvitīyasya tṛtīyena jñānena hi vivicyate || 381 ||"

[2.381,1]

yasmā"ttasya" dvitīyasya jñānasya tau dvāvākārāva"rtharūpeṇa" viṣayabhāvena tadālambaka "ātmākāraśca kaścana" tṛtīyena dvitīyajñānālambakena hi yasmād vivecyate avadhāryate | tasmādarthākāraṃ svavedanañca jñānamabhyupagantavyaṃ | (381)

{2.382}

[2.382,0]

"arthakāryatayā jñānasmṛtāvarthasmṛteryadi | bhrāntyā saṅkalanaṃ;"

[2.382,1]

atha nirākārameva "jñānama"rthasya kāryamanubhavarūpa"marthakāryatayā" jñāta"smṛtau" viśeṣaṇatvenā"rthasya smṛteḥ" smaryamāṇasyārthasya "bhrāntyā" jñānātmani "saṃka" sambandhanaṃ yadi syāttadā ko doṣaḥ |

[2.382,2]

āha |

[2.382,3]

"jyotirmanaskāre ca sā bhavet || 382 ||"

[2.382,4]

arthavat jyotiṣa ālokasya manaskārasya ca jñānahetutvāt | tatkāryajñāne smaryamāṇe sā smṛti"rjyotirmanaskāre" ālokasamanantarapratyayorapi syāt | tatra bhrāntyā arthākāramivālokamanaskārākāramapi saṃkalanīyaṃ | na tvarthākārameva niyamena saṃkalayituṃ yuktaṃ | (382)

{2.383}

[2.383,0]

"sarvveṣāmapi kāryyāṇāṃ kāraṇaiḥ syāttathā grahaḥ | kulālādivivekena na smaryeta ghaṭastataḥ || 383 ||"

[2.383,1]

yadi cārthakāryaṃ bhrāntyā smaryate tadā "sarvveṣāmapi kāryyāṇāṃ kāraṇaiḥ" saha "tathā grahaḥ" kāraṇātmatvena grahaṇaṃ "syāt" | tataśca dhaṭakulālādikāryaṃ "kulālā" bhedena "na smaryeta" | (383)

{2.384}

[2.384,0]

athāstyeva kaścidālokādibhyo viṣayasya jñānātmanyāropaṇīyo viśeṣastatastadākārāvagraheṇa smaryate | nānyathetyāha |

[2.384,1]

"yasmādatiśayājjñānamarthasaṃsargabhājanam | sārūpyāttat kimanyat syād dṛṣṭeśca yamalādiṣu || 384 ||"

[2.384,2]

"yasmāda"rthāropitāda"tiśayāt jñānamarthasaṃsarga"syārthasaṃśleṣasya "bhājanaṃ" pātraṃ bhavati | arthena sārūpyā"danyat kintat syāt" | sārūpyādanyasyātiśayasyopalakṣaṇatvāyogāt | "yamalādiṣu" sārūpyād bhrāntyā tathārthaniścayasya "dṛṣṭeśca" | (384)

{2.385}

[2.385,0]

kiñca |

[2.385,1]

"ādyānubhayarūpatve hyekarūpaṃ vyavasthitam | dvitīyaṃ vyatiricyeta na parāmarśacetasā || 385 ||"

[2.385,2]

"ādya"syārthajñānasyā"nubhayarūpatve"'rthākārarahitatvāt anubhavaikarūpatve tadālambakaṃ "dvitīyaṃ" jñāna"meka"smin "rūpe"'nubhavātmani "vyavasthitaṃ parāmarśacetasā" jñānajñānālambakena tṛtīyajñānena na vyatiricyeta | na viṣayajñānagrāhakatayā bhedena gṛhyeta | svābhāsamātratvena sarvvasyāviśeṣāt | (385)

{2.386}

[2.386,1]

yato buddheranākāratve doṣo'yaṃ "tataḥ" pu"ro'rthasya" dhiyaṃ "nīlādirūpeṇa bhāsamānāṃ "nasyārthākārāvagrahasyā"śleṣaḥ" saṃsarggo yasyāḥ sā tāma"valamba"te | (386)

{2.387}

[2.387,0]

"anyathā hyādyamevaikaṃ saṃyojyetārthasambhavāt | jñānaṃ nādṛṣṭasambandhaṃ pūrvvārthenottarottaram || 387 ||"

[2.387,1]

"anyathā" yadyanākāraṃ jñānamarthakāryatayā bhrāntyā'rthākāraṃ smaryata ityāśrīyate ta"dādyamevaika"marthajñānaṃ smṛtyā'rthena "saṃyojyeta | arthātsaṃbhavāt" tasya | na "uttaro" jñānasyā"rthenā"kāraṇabhūtenā"dṛṣṭasambandhaṃ" saṃyojyeta |

[2.387,2]

tasmātsthitametat jñānānāṃ viṣayasārūpyānubhavarūpatvābhyāṃ dvyākāratvaṃ | tataśca sahopalambhaniyamo'rthavijñānayoḥ | arthākāratāyā arthopalambhāt | anubhavarūpatāyāḥ sva"bhe"danatvāt | (387)

{2.388}

[2.388,0]

tathā ca |

[2.388,1]

"sakṛt samvedyamānasya niyamena dhiyā saha | viṣayasya tato'nyatvaṃ kenākāreṇa sidhyati || 388 ||"

[2.388,2]

"dhiyā saha niyamena sakṛtsaṃvedyamānasya viṣayasya tato" dhiyo"'nyatvaṃ" bhedaḥ "kenā"ṇa prakāreṇa "sidhyati" | bhinnayoḥ sahopalambhaniyamāyogāt | (388)

{2.389}

[2.389,0]

yadi viṣayajñānayorabhedastadā grāhyagrāhakatayā bhedaḥ kathaṃ pratibhātītyāha |

[2.389,1]

"bhedaśca bhrāntavijñānairdṛśyetendāvivādvaye |"

[2.389,2]

[2.389,3]

bhedepi kasbhānna sahopalambhaniyama ityāha |

[2.389,5]
