"agnisvabhāvaḥ śakrasya mūrddhā" valmīko "yadyagnireva sa" tadā na hi vahnisvarūpatāṃ vihāyānyad vahne rūpaṃ | "athā"nyathā pratīyamānatvāda"nagnisvabhāvosau" tadā "dhūmo" vahnerjanyasvabhāva"statra śakramūrdhni kathaṃ bhavet" | na hi vahnijanyonyasmād bhavitumarhati tadadhīnatvāt | tataḥ śakramūrdhno dhūmotpattiriti bhrāntireṣā | vahnereva taddeśavartino'nupalakṣitādutpattiḥ || (35)

{3.36}

[3.36,0]

kiñca |

[3.36,1]

"dhūmahetusvabhāvo hi vahnistacchaktibhedavān | adhūmahetordhūmasya bhāve sa syādahetukaḥ || 36 ||"

[3.36,2]

"dhūmahetusvabhāvastacchaktibhedavān" dhūmajananaśaktiviśeṣayukto "vahniḥ" pratītaḥ | "adhūmaheto"radahanāt "dhūmasya bhāve sa" dhūmo"'hetukaḥ syāt" | hetuṃ pramāṇaniścitamantareṇaivotpādāt | ahetutve ca nityaṃ sattvamasattvamvāṃ syādityuktaṃ || (36)

{3.37}

[3.37,0]

syādetat | śālūkādi svabījād vijātī"yācca" gomayāderdṛśyate | tatkathamavahnerddhūmotpāde'hetutvaprasaṅga ityāha |

[3.37,1]

"anvayavyatirekādyaḥ yasya dṛṣṭonuvartakaḥ | svabhāvastasya taddheturato bhinnānna sambhavaḥ || 37 ||"

[3.37,2]

"anvayavyatirekād yaḥ svabhāvo yasyānuvarttako"'pekṣako dṛṣṭastaṃsya svabhāvasya tadanuvarttyamānaṃ heturato bhinnād vijātīyānna saṃbhavaḥ kasyacid | yaddhi śālūkādi svabījaprabhavaṃ yacca vijātīyaprabhavaṃ tayoḥ sadṛśatvapratītāvapi na tādṛśatvaṃ rasavīryavipākabhedāt | yadi tu hetubhedepyabhedo viśvātmakaṃ dravyaṃ syādityādyuktaṃprasajyeta || (37)

{3.38}

<(4) sāmānyacintā>

[3.38,0]

"svabhāvepyavinābhāvo bhāvamātrānurodhini | tadabhāve svayambhāvasyābhāvaḥ syādabhedataḥ || 38 ||"

[3.38,1]

svabhāvepi hetāvavinābhāvaḥ | kva | sādhye "bhāvamātrānurodhini" sādhanasvarūpamātrānuvarttini vyāpake yathā kṛtakatvasyānityatve | yata"sta"sya vyāpakasyā"bhāve bhāvasya" vyāpyasya kṛtakatvādeḥ "svayamabhāvaḥ syāt | abhedata" aikātmyād vastutaḥ || (38)

{3.39}

[3.39,0]

yadi ya eva kṛtakaḥ sa evānityo bhedābhāvāt tadā pratijñārthaikadeśo hetuḥ syādityāha |

[3.39,1]

"sarve bhāvāḥ svabhāvena svasvabhāvavyavasthiteḥ | svabhāvaparabhāvābhyāṃ vyāvṛttibhāgino yataḥ || 39 ||"

[3.39,2]

"sarvve bhāvāḥ svabhāvena svasvabhāvavyavasthiteḥ" | ātmātmīyarūpavasthitatvāt | svabhāvaparabhāvābhyāṃ sajātīyād vijātīyācca vyāvṛttibhāgino yasmānna kenacinmiśrāḥ | (39)

{3.40}

[3.40,0]

"tasmād vyāvṛttirarthānāṃ yataśca tannibandhanāḥ | jātibhedāḥ prakalpyante tadviśeṣāvagāhinaḥ || 40 ||"

[3.40,1]

tasmāt "yato" yato'svarūpādarthād "vyāvṛttirarthānāṃ tannibandhanāḥ" tattadvyāvṛttinimittā "jātibhedāstadviśeṣāvagāhinaḥ" tatsvalakṣaṇāśrayāḥ "kalpyante" śabdaiḥ svavācyatayā || (40)

{3.41}

[3.41,0]

yataḥ śabdaḥ kāścid arthakriyāḥ kurvannatatkāriṇo'śabdādakṛtakānnityādeśca vyāvṛtta iti tattadvayavacchedapratipādanārthaṃ śabdakṛtakānityatvādyā jātayo'nanyaśabdavācyatayā kalpyante |

[3.41,1]

"tasmād viśeṣo yo yena dharmeṇa saṃpratīyate | na sa śakyastatonyena tena bhinnā vyavasthitiḥ || 41 ||"

[3.41,2]

"tasmāt" svabhāvābhedepi kṛtakatvānityatvādīnāṃ "yena" dharmeṇa nāmnā'nitya ityanena "yo viśeṣo" nityād vyāvṛttiḥ "saṃpra" sa viśeṣaḥ "śakyaḥ tato"'nityaśabdā"danyena" kṛtakaśabdena pratyetuṃ | | "tena" kāraṇena sādhyasādhanayo"rbhinnā vyavasthitiḥ" | yadyapi śabda eva kṛtako'nityaśca tathāpyaśabdavyāvṛttatayā niścito dharmī kṛtakatayā ca hetuḥ | anityatayā cāsiddhaḥ sādhyaḥ | tato dharmisādhyasādhanānāṃ bhedaḥ kalpito na tu tānyeva kalpitāni teṣāṃ sattvāt | tataḥ kalpitadharmiṇi kalpitāt sādhanāt kalpitasya sādhyasya siddhimācakṣāṇaḥ pratyākhyātaḥ | "tasmānna" pratijñārthaikadeśo hetuḥ | sādhyasādhanayorbhinnavyavacchedarūpatvāt || (41)

{3.42}

[3.42,0]

kasmāt punarvyavacchedaḥ śabdaliṅgābhyāṃ pratipādyata itīṣyate na tu "vastveva" vidhirūpeṇetyāha |

[3.42,1]

"ekasyārthasvabhāvasya pratyakṣasya sataḥ svayam | konyo bhāgo na dṛṣṭaḥ syāt yaḥ pramāṇaiḥ parīkṣyate || 42 ||"

[3.42,2]

"ekasthārthasvabhāvasya svayamātmanā pratyakṣasya sataḥ konyo bhāgo na dṛ" nirṇṇīyate | yadi pramāṇāntaraiḥ śabdāntaraiśca vastveva viṣayīkarttavyaṃtadā tat pratyakṣeṇa śabdāntareṇa ca dṛṣṭameveti vyarthāni pramāṇāni syuḥ | (42)

{3.43}

[3.43,0]

tvanmatepi pratyakṣeṇa dṛṣṭe dharmiṇi pramāṇāntaravaiphalyaṃ syāt | netyāha |

[3.43,1]

"no ced bhrāntinimittena saṃyojyeta guṇāntaram | śuktau vā rajatākāro rūpasādharmyadarśanāt || 43 ||"

[3.43,2]

dṛṣṭe sarvathā vastuni "no ced bhrāntinimittena" sādṛśyādinā "saṃyojye"tāropyeta "guṇāntaraṃ" dharmmāntaramasadeva śuktau vā śuktāviva "rūpasādharmyadarśanāt" bhrāntinimittād rajatākārastadā sarvvathā vastuniścayāt pramāṇāntaraśabdāntaravaiphalyaṃ syāt | (43)

{3.44}

[3.44,0]

etadevāha |

[3.44,1]

"tasmād dṛṣṭasya bhāvasya dṛṣṭa evākhilo guṇaḥ | bhrānterna niścaya iti sādhanaṃ saṃpravarttate || 44 ||"

[3.44,2]

"tasmād dṛṣṭasya bhāvasya dṛṣṭa evākhilo guṇaḥ" dharmaḥ | tathāpi bhrāntervviparītākārāropikāyā na niścīyata ityāropitavyavacchedārthaṃ "sādhanaṃ" śabdāntarañca "saṃpravarttate ||" (44)

{3.45}

[3.45,0]

na kevalaṃ pratyakṣād vastugrahe sādhanāntaraśabdāntaravaiphalyaṃ kintvanumānādapītyāha |

[3.45,1]

"vastugrahenumānācca dharmasyaikasya niścaye | sarvagraho hyapohe tu nāyaṃ doṣaḥ prasajyate || 45 ||"

[3.45,2]

"vastugrahenumānācca dharmasyaikasya" kṛtakatvādeḥ pratyayabhedābheditvādikṛte "niścaye "syānityatvāde"rgrahaḥ" syāt | ekarūpatvāt | kṛtakatvādisādhanāntaravaiyarthyaṃ | "apohe tva"nyavyavacchede śabdaliṅgaviṣaye svīkriyamāṇe "nāyaṃ" pramāṇāntarādivaiphalya"ṣaḥ prasajyate" | na khalu "pratyagradṛṣṭaṃ vastvantaraṃ śabdaliṅgā" kintvanyavyavacchedaḥ | ekasmiṃśca vyavacchede siddhepyasiddhaṃ vyavacchedāntaraṃ liṅgāntarataḥ śabdāntarataśca sādhyata iti na kaścid doṣaḥ || (45)

{3.46}

[3.46,0]

"tasmādapohaviṣayaṃ liṅgamiti prakīrtitam | anyathā dharmiṇaḥ siddhau kimataḥ sādhakaṃ param || 46 ||"

[3.46,1]

"tasmā"dācāryeṇā"pohaviṣayaṃ liṅgamiti prakīrtitaṃ" | liṅgamupalakṣaṇaṃ śabdaśca | "anyathā" yadi vastuviṣayaṃ liṅgaṃ tadā "dharmmiṇaḥ" sarvātmanā pratyakṣataḥ "siddhau kimato" dharmiṇaḥ "parama"siddhamasti yatpra"sādhakaṃ" liṅgampramāṇaṃ syāt || (46)

{3.47}

[3.47,0]

"kvacit sāmānyaviṣayaṃ dṛṣṭe jñānamaliṅgajam | kathamanyāpohaviṣayaṃ tanmātrāpohagocaraḥ || 47 ||"

[3.47,1]

nanu "kvaci"nnīlādāvasamāropito'nyo viparītāṃśo yasmin | tasmin pratyakṣeṇa "dṛṣṭe yajjñānamaliṅgajaṃ" vikalpakaṃ "sāmānyaviṣayaṃ" bhavati | tadāropābhāvāt | kathamanyāpohaviṣayaṃ | āha"tanmātra"syānīlamātrasyā"poho" vijātīyād vyāvṛttirvyavacchedaḥ sa "gocaro" yasya tattathā | nīlavikalpasyānīlavyavaccheda eva viṣaya ityarthaḥ || (47)

{3.48}

[3.48,0]

kasmādevamityāha |

[3.48,1]

"niścayāropamanasorbādhyabādhakabhāvataḥ | samāropaviveke'sya pravṛttiriti gamyate || 48 ||"

[3.48,2]

"niścayāropamanasorbāṣyabādhakabhāvataḥ |" samāropasya "viveke" vyavacchede'sya niścayasya "pravṛttiriti gamyate" || (48)

{3.49}

[3.49,0]

tasmād |

[3.49,1]

"yāvantoṃ'śasamāropā niścayāstannirāsataḥ | tāvanta eva śabdā bhinnavyavacchedagocarāḥ || 49 ||"

[3.49,2]

"yāvanto'"śasya dharmasya "samāropāstasya nirāsa"nimittaṃ vi"niścayāḥ" śabdāśca "tāvanta" eva | tena te niścayāḥ śabdāśca "bhinnavyavacchedagocarāḥ" || (49)

{3.50}

[3.50,0]

"anyathā vastu viṣayīkuruta ekena vā dhiyā | ekatra nānyo viṣayostīti syāt paryāyatā || 50 ||"

[3.50,1]

"anyathā" yadi śabdaniścayau sarvātmanā vastu viṣayīkurutaḥ tadekena śabdena "buddhyā vā" vikalpikayā vyāpte sarvātmanā viṣayīkṛte vastu"nyekatra nānyo"'pratipanno "viṣa"yo"stī"ti "paryāyatā" śabdānāṃ "syāt" vikalpānāñcaikaviṣayatā bhavet || (50)

{3.51}

[3.51,0]

nanu dravyādupādhayaḥ parasparañca bhinnāstannimittā vikalpāḥ śabdāśca teṣu tadādhāre vā dravye varttanta ityāha |

[3.51,1]

"nānopādhiviśiṣṭasya bhedinorthasya grāhikā | upakārāṅgaśaktibhyo'bhinnātmaniścayagrahe || 51 ||"

[3.51,2]

"yasyāpi nai yā yi kā de"rmate "nānopādhe"rdravyatvādyanekadharma"viśiṣṭha" syāta evopāghi bhedād "bhedinorthasya" vidhirūpeṇa dhīḥ | tasyāpi matena nānāprakārāṇāmupādhī"nāmupakārasyāṅgaṃ" yāḥ "śakta"yastābhyo"'bhinnātmana" upādhimato dravyasya "niścaya"jñānena "grahe" || (51)

{3.52}

[3.52,0]

"sarvātmanā kṛte grāhe ko bhedaḥ syādaniścitaḥ | tayorātmani sambandhādekajñāne dvayagrahaḥ || 52 ||"

[3.52,1]

"sarvvātmanā" kṛte satyupakāryasyopādhikalāpasya madhye ko "bheda" upādhiviśeṣaḥ "syādaniścitaḥ |" yathā dravyamekamupādhimupakaroti | tathā parānapi | tata ekopādhyupakārakatve vidhirūpeṇa gṛhyamāṇe sarvvopādhyupakārakatvaṃ gṛhyeta | tathā ca sarvvopādhigrahaṇaprasaṅgaḥ | na hi yatsāpekṣaṃ yadrūpaṃ tadagrahaṇe tad gṛhītuṃ śakyaṃ ||

[3.52,2]

nanu dhūmāpekṣaṃ vahneḥ kāraṇatvaṃ na ca tadgrahe dhūmagrahaḥ | naitad yuktaṃ | tathāhi |

[3.52,3]

kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇatvamiṣṭaṃ vahneryadyavidyamānatvād dhūmāt pūrvvakālabhāvitā | dhūmāsāhityaṃ varttamānakālasattā | na tad dhūmāpekṣaṃ svakāraṇāt tathotpatteḥ | dhūmamantareṇaiva ca bhāvāt | na ca tadgrahe dhūmagraho viruddhatvāt | na hi dhūmagrahaṇe tasmāt prāgbhāvitvasya tadasāhityasya ca grahaṇaṃ | atha dhūmasyāyaṃ heturiti niścayaviṣayatvaṃ kāraṇatvamiṣṭantadā'styevedṛśakāraṇatvasya grahe dhūmapratītirubhayapratītyākāratvādasya niścayasya dvayānvayavyatirekagrahaṇasāpekṣatvācca ||

[3.52,4]

nanu ca gṛhītatadutpatteragnimātradarśanāt kāraṇatvapratītirna ca tadā "dhūma" ||

[3.52,5]

siddhāntī | na ca tatra pratyakṣāt kāraṇatvasya pratītiḥ kintvagnirūpamātrasya | anyathā sarvvasya taddarśinaḥ kāraṇatvapratītiprasaṅgaḥ | kintu vyāptigrahasāpekṣā ānumānikī tatpratītiḥ | tathā hi gṛhītatadutpattereveyaṃ bhavati nānyasya | tadutpattigrahe ca yadevaṃ rūpaṃ tadetatkāraṇamiti gṛhītā vyāptiranumānapratītau ca dhūmakāraṇaṃ vahniriti vyavacchedadvayamanyonyasāpekṣaṃ pratīyata eva ityalaṃ tatprasaṅgena | na hyanutkhātitakāryaḥ kāraṇatvaniścayaḥ | atyantamabhyāsācca vyāptigrahasaṃskārasya prabuddhatvādapekṣā nāstītyatatvavivekināṃ nānumānatvaprabodhaḥ | na hyanumānamahamityutpannamanumānamucyate | kintu trirūpaliṅgajamanumeyaviṣayaṃ kāraṇatvajñānañca tādṛśameva | dravyantu yenaiva rūpeṇa ekamupādhimupakaroti tenaivāparānapītyekopodhyupakārakatve gṛhyamāṇe nānekopādhyupakārakatvasya grahaṇāt sarvvopādhigrahaṇaprasaṅgaḥ parasparasāpekṣatvāt | tataśca "tayo"rupādhikalāpatadupakārakatvayo"rātmani sambandhāt" | dravyasya sambandhā"deka"syopādhyupakārakatvasya "jñāne dvayasya grahaḥ" syāt | ekaniyatā pratītirna bhavedityarthaḥ || (52)

{3.53}

[3.53,0]

atha dravyādupādhyupakārikāḥ śaktayo bhinnā eva dravyagrahaṇe tāsāmagrahaṇāt na sarvvopādhigrahaṇaprasaṅga ityāha |

[3.53,1]

"dharmopakāraśaktīnāṃ bhede tāḥ tasya kiṃ yadi | nopakārastataḥ tāsāṃ tathā syādanavasthitiḥ || 53 ||"

[3.53,2]

"dharmā"ṇāmupādhīnā"upakāra"sya nimittabhūtānāṃ "śaktī"nāṃ dravyād "bhede" svīkriyamāṇe "tāḥ" śaktaya"stasya" dravyasya "kiṃ" kasmāt | yadi "nopakārastato" dravyāt "tāsāṃ" śaktīnāmupakāramantareṇa sambandhe'tiprasaṅgāt | atha tāsāṃ śaktīnāṃ dravyeṇopakāraḥ kriyate svarūpeṇa tadā śaktyupakāratvasya grahaṇācchaktīnāṃ grahaḥ | tadgrahācca sarvvopādhigrahaprasaṅgaḥ tadavasthaḥ |

[3.53,3]

syādetat | śaktīrapi bhinnābhiḥśaktibhirupakaroti "tathā syādanavasthitiḥ" | tathā hi yāstāḥ śaktyupakārikāḥ śaktyapastā dravyasyopakāradvārād (?) yadīṣṭāstadāsvarūpeṇopakārakatve sarvvopādhigrahaprasaṅgabhayādanyāḥ śaktaya eṣṭavyāḥ | tathā cānavasthā vyaktā | (53)

{3.54}

[3.54,0]

uktamarthaṃ saṃgṛhṇannāha |

[3.54,1]

"ekopakārake grāhye'dṛṣṭāḥ tasminna santi te | sarvopakārakaṃ hyekaṃ tadgrahe sakalagrahaḥ || 54 ||"

[3.54,2]

"eka"syopādhe"rupakārake" dravye "grāhye"'bhimate tata ekopādhyupakārakadravyasvabhāvādapare upādhyantarāṇāmupakārakā upakāraśaktibhedā dṛṣṭe "tasminne"kopādhyupakārake dravye'dṛṣṭā ye "te na santi" | ekameva hi rūpaṃ sarvvopādhyupakārakamatasta"syaiko"pādhimato "grahe sakalopādhigrahaḥ" syāt || (54)

{3.55}

<ka. nyāyamīmāṃsāmatanirāsaḥ>

<ka vyāvṛttasvabhāvā bhāvāḥ>

[3.55,0]

"yadi bhrāntinivṛttyarthaṃ gṛhītepyanyadiṣyate | tadvyavacchedaviṣayaṃ siddhantadvat tato'param || 55 ||"

[3.55,1]

sarvvātmanā vikalpena "gṛhītepi" vastuni bhrāntyā tathā na niścaya iti "yadi " pramāṇāntara"miṣyate" | tadbhrāntinivarttakaṃ pramāṇāntaraṃ "vyavacchedaviṣayaṃ siddhaṃ" bhramāropitatvāpohaviṣayatvād | "tato" bhrāntinivarttakāda"paraṃ" yat pūrvvamutpannamvastuviṣayamiṣṭaṃ "tadva"dapohaviṣayaṃ siddhaṃ || (55)

{3.56}

[3.56,0]

kasmādityāha |

[3.56,1]

"tadvipakṣasamāropaviṣaye yadi niścayaiḥ | niścīyate na yad rūpaṃ tatteṣāṃ viṣayaḥ katham || 56 ||"

[3.56,2]

avidyamānānyasamārope "viṣaye vṛtteḥ" | vikalpo hi vyavacchedaviṣayaṃ niścinvan tadvipakṣasamāropaviṣaye na bhavati | kintu tadvyavacchedaniścayāropamanasorbbādhyabādhakabhāvata ityuktaṃ |

[3.56,3]

api ca niścayairekākārapravṛttai"ryad rūpaṃ na niścīyate tatteṣāmviṣayaḥ ka"thamucyate | niścitañcāpratipannaṃ ceti viprati"si"ddhaṃ | yadi kṛtakatvaniścaye'nityatvādyapi niścitaṃ kathaṃ tasyāpratipattiḥ | kṛtakatvasyāpi vā mābhūt || (56)

{3.57}

[3.57,0]

evantarhi pratyakṣagṛhīte vastuni niścayāniścayau na syātāmityāha |

[3.57,1]

"pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītepi viśeṣeṃśavivarjite | yadviśeṣāvasāyesti pratyayaḥ sa pratīyate || 57 ||"

[3.57,2]

"pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītepi viśeṣe" svalakṣaṇe sarvvato vyāvṛtteṃ"'śai"rbhāgai"rvvivarjite" yasya "viśeṣa"sya vyavacchedasyā"vasāye"sti "pratyayaḥ" sahakārī prakaraṇābhyāsapāṭavādiḥ "sa""pratīyate" netaraḥ | na khalvasmanmate pratyakṣaṃ niścayātmakaṃ nāpyanubhavamātrādhīno niścayo yena sarvvathā niścayaprasaṅgaḥ | kintu yatra vyavacchede'bhyāsādayaḥsahakāriṇaḥ pratyakṣasya santi sa niścīyate nānya iti yukto vibhāgaḥ | (57)

{3.58}

[3.58,0]

"tatrāpi cānyavyāvṛttiranyavyāvṛtta ityapi | śabdāśca niścayāścaiva nimittamanurundhate || 58 ||"

[3.58,1]

"tatrāpi" cānyāpohepi śabdavikalpaviṣaye"'nyavyāvṛttiranyavyāvṛtta ityapi | " bhinnaviṣayā iva pravartante na te vyāvṛttivyāvṛttayorvvāstavabhedanibandhanāḥ kintarhi saṃketameva bhedavyavahāravyasthāpakaṃ vakṣyamāṇa"nimittamanurundhate"'nuvarttante | yadi goranyā'govyāvṛttistadā yathā gauragoraśvādervyāvṛttastathā'govyāvṛtterapi vyāvṛttaḥ | tataścāśvādivad goragaureva syāt | yo hyagovyāvṛttervyāvṛttaḥ so'gauryathāśvādirgauśca tatheti syāt | tathā'govyāvṛttirapi na prāpnoti | sarvvasyaivāgotvāt | goragoranyatve hi tasmād vyāvṛttiḥ syāt | yadā tu gaureva nāsti tadā kasya kasmād vyāvṛttiḥ | tasmānna vyāvṛttivyāvṛttayorvvastuto bhedaḥ | (58)

{3.59}

[3.59,0]

tataśca ||

[3.59,1]

"dvayorekābhidhānepi vibhaktirvyatirekiṇī | bhinnamarthamivānveti vācyate sa viśeṣataḥ || 59 ||"

[3.59,2]

"dvayo"rvyāvṛttivyāvṛttayorekasyārthasyā"bhidhānepi" vastuto "vibhaktiḥ" ṣaṣṭhyādi"rvyatireko" vācyabhedaḥ tadvatī | vyāvṛttasya vyāvṛttiriti "bhinnamivārthamanve"tyanugacchati vācakatvena | vācyasya leśaviśeṣato'lpabhedāt sāṅketikādabhinnepyarthe || (59)

{3.60}

[3.60,0]

kimarthaṃ saṃketabhedaḥ kaśca vācyaviśeṣa ityāha |

[3.60,1]

"bhedāntarapratikṣepāpratikṣepau tayordvayoḥ | padaṃ saṅketabhedasya jñātṛvāñchānurodhinaḥ || 60 ||"

[3.60,2]

"bhedānta"rasya pratipādyamānād vyavacchedādanyasya vyavacchedasya "pratikṣepaḥ" | sāmānādhikaraṇyasya svabhāvo'"pratikṣepa"statsambhavaḥ | "tau tayordvayo"rvyāvṛttivyāvṛttaśabdayoḥ"saṃketabhedasya jñātṛvāñchānurodhinaḥ" padaṃ kāraṇaṃ | jñātā hi kadācit gauranaśvatvaṃ niṣkṛṣṭadharmāntara sambandhayogyatvaṃ jijñāsate | tadā gotvamasyetyucyate na tu gotvamasya śuklamiti | yadā tu vyāvṛttirevāniṣkṛṣṭadharmāntarasambandhayogyā jijñāsitā bhavati | tadā vyāvṛttaśabdasaṃketo yathā gaurayamiti dharmmāntarasāmānādhikaraṇyañca gauḥśukla ityādi || (60)

{3.61}

[3.61,0]

"bhedoyameva sarvatra dravyabhāvābhidhāyinoḥ | śabdayorna tayorvācye viśeṣastena kaścana || 61 ||"

[3.61,1]

"bhedoyameva" saṃketakṛto dharmāntarapratikṣepāpratikṣepapratipattiphalo "dravyabhāvā"rddharmidharmavācinoḥ "śabdayorna" vāstavaḥ | "tena tayorvvācye" niścayaviṣaye "na ka"ścid "viśe" | bhedāntarapratikṣepāpratikṣepābhyāmekasyaiva pratyāyanāt || (61)

{3.62}

[3.62,0]

"jijñāpayiṣurarthaṃ taṃ taddhitena kṛtāpi vā | anyena vā yadi brūyāt bhedo nāsti tataḥ paraḥ || 62 ||"

[3.62,1]

tathā vyavaharttā "jijñāpayiṣurarthaṃ taṃ" sāṅketikaṃ bhedaṃ "taddhitena kṛtāpi vā" pācakatvamasya pācakoyampākaḥ pākyo vetyādi | "anyena vā" svayaṃkṛtena samayena "yadi brūyāt" | tathāpi "tato" bhedapratipādakāt taddhitāde"rbhedaḥ" paro vāstavo "nāsti" || (62)

{3.63}

[3.63,0]

"tenānyāpohaviṣaye taddoṣopavarṇṇanam | pratyākhyātaṃ pṛthaktve hi syād doṣo jātitadvatoḥ || ||"

[3.63,1]

"tena" vyāvṛttivyāvṛttayorabhede"nānyāpohaviṣaye" jātimān śabdavācya itipakṣaḥ tadvat pakṣabhūrdoṣo'nyāpohepi syāditi | "taddoṣopavarṇṇanaṃ pratyākhyātaṃ" | tadvat pakṣo hi jātimabhidhāya śabdastadvati varttata iti tadvacane svātantryamasya na syāt sāmānādhikaraṇyañca na bhavet | gauḥ śukla iti jāteraśuklatvāt | na copacārāśrayeṇa svātantryaṃ sāmānyādhikaraṇyañcāskhaladgatiyuktamityādi "jātitadvatoḥ pṛthaktve hi syād doṣa eṣaḥ" | na tu vyāvṛttivyāvṛttimatorbheda iti nātra tatpakṣoktadoṣaḥ || (63)

{3.64}

[3.64,0]

yadi vyāvṛttitadvatorna bhavestadā gorgotvaṃ śuklatvasāsnādimatvādayaśceti ṣaṣṭhīvacanabhedādi na prāpnotītyāha |

[3.64,1]

"yeṣāṃ vastuvaśā vāco na vivakṣāparāśrayāḥ | ṣaṣṭhīvacanabhedādi codyaṃ tān prati yuktimat || 64 ||"

[3.64,2]

"yeṣāṃ" bāhyānāṃ mate "vastuvaśā" vastvāyattā "vāco na vivakṣāpara āśrayaḥ" kāraṇaṃ yāsāṃ tāstathā | "ṣaṣṭhīvacanabhedādi codyaṃ tān prati yuktimat" || (64)

{3.65}

[3.65,0]

"yad yathā vācakatvena vaktṛbhirviniyamyate | anapekṣitabāhyārthaṃ tat tathā vācakaṃ vacaḥ || 65 ||"

[3.65,1]

asmākaṃ yadvaco "yathā" dharmāntarasya pratikṣepeṇāprati"vācakatvena vaktṛbhirniyamyate" viśeṣeṇa vyavasthāpyate"'napekṣitavāhyā" saṃketamātrānurodhitvāt "tadvacastathā vāca"ṣṭamiti na codyāvakāśaḥ || (65)

{3.66}

[3.66,0]

"dārāḥ ṣaṇṇagarītyādau bhedābhedavyavasthiteḥ | khasya svabhāvaḥ khatvaṃ vetyatra vā kiṃ nibandhanam || 66 ||"

[3.66,1]

yasya tu vāstava eva śābdo vyavahārastasya "dārāḥ ṣaṇṇagarītyādā"vādiśabdāt gṛhā viṃśatirityādau ca yathākramamabhinne bhinne ca vastuto "bhedābhedayo"rbahuvacanaikavacananimittayo"rvyavasthiteḥ | khasya svabhāvaḥ khatvaṃ vetyatra" dharmidharmabhedasya "kimvā" nimittaṃ na kiñcana | na hyekasyāḥ striyā bahutvaṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ nagarāṇāṃ vā ekatvamākāśasya svabhāvo bhinnaḥ sāmānyaṃ vāsti | atha cāsti śabdavṛttistataḥ kalpita eva tadviṣayo vaktavyaḥ || (66)

{3.67}

[3.67,0]

yadi sarvato vyāvṛttasvabhāvā bhāvā na teṣu sāmānyamasti kathaṃ gotvamityādisāmānyapratītirityāha |

[3.67,1]

"ekārthapratibhāsinyā bhāvānāśritya bhedinaḥ | rūpaṃ pareṣāṃ vyāvṛttaṃ sā dhīḥ saṃvṛtirucyate || 67 ||"

[3.67,2]

"bhedinaḥ" sarvvato vyāvṛttān "bhāvānāśritya" paramparāpātebhya utpadya "yayā" dhiyā "ekārthapratibhāsinyā" ekārthādhyavasāyasvākārayā svarūpeṇa svapratibhāsena "pareṣāṃ" svalakṣaṇānāṃ "rūpaṃ" sarvvato vyāvṛttaṃ saṃvriyate pracchādyate "sā buddhiḥ""saṃvṛtirucyate" || (67)

{3.68}

[3.68,0]

"tayā saṃvṛtanānātvāḥ saṃvṛtyā bhedinaḥ svayam | abhedina ivābhānti bhedārūpeṇa kenacit || 68 ||"

[3.68,1]

"tayā" saṃvṛttyā "svaya"mātmanā "bhedinaḥ" svasvabhāvavyavasthitā bhāvāḥ "saṃvṛtanānātvāḥ" sthagitabhedāḥ "kenacid rūpeṇa" vijātīyavyāvṛttyupakalpitena gotvādinā'"bhedina " || (68)

{3.69}

[3.69,0]

"tasyā abhiprāyavaśāt sāmānyaṃ satprakīrtitam | yathā tayopakalpitaṃ tadasata paramārthataḥ || 69 ||"

[3.69,1]

"tasyā" buddheḥ sāmānyarūpatayā'dhyavasitākārāyā'"bhiprāyavaśāt" sāmānyaṃ "sat prakīrttitaṃ" | vijātīyavyāvṛttervvastuṣvabhāvāt | tadupakalpitaṃ gotvādi sāmānya rūpeṇa buddhyākāramadhyava"śya"nti vyavaharttāraḥ | adhyavasāyānurodhena ca sāmānyaṃ sadityucyate | "yathā" vastutvena "tat" sāmānyaṃ "tayā" saṃvṛttibuddhyā kalpitaṃ "tathā'sat paramārthataḥ" || (69)

{3.70}

[3.70,0]

tadevāsattvamāha |

[3.70,1]

"vyaktayo nānuyantyanyadanuyāyi na bhāsate | jñānādavyatiriktaṃ vā kathamarthāntaraṃ vrajet || 70 ||"

[3.70,2]

"vyaktaya"stāva"nna" paraspara"manuyanti" bhedāt | tāsva"nuyāyi" ca kiñcinna "bhāsate" vyaktimātravedanāt | yacca "jñānādavyatirikta"mākārasvarūpaṃ tatka"thamarthāntaraṃ" jñānāntaraṃ"vā vrajet" svalakṣaṇarūpatvādasya || (70)

{3.71}

[3.71,0]

"tasmānmithyāvikalpoyamartheṣvekātmatāgrahaḥ | itaretarabhedosya bījaṃ saṃjñā yadarthikā || 71 ||"

[3.71,1]

"tasmādartharūpa"sya jñānarūpasya ca sāmānyasya yogā"nmithyāvikalpoyama"rthaśūnya eṣa vikalpoyama"rtheṣvekātmatāyāḥ" sāmānyarūpatāyā "grahaḥ | asya" caikātmatayā pratibhāsino mithyāvikalpasya "bījaṃ" heturitarasmādatatkārya kāriṇo "bhedo" vyāvṛttiḥ | "yadarthikā saṃjñā" śabdopi vijātīyavyāvṛttau saṃketyate tadviṣayaśca || (71)

{3.72}

<kha bhinnānāmabhinnaṃ kāryam>

[3.72,0]

kathaṃ punarbhinnānāmabhinnaṃ kāryamityāha |

[3.72,1]

"ekapratyavamarśārthajñānādyekārthasādhane | kecid bhedepi niyatāḥ svabhāvenendriyādivat || 72 ||"

[3.72,2]

"ekapratyavamarśa" ekākārādhyavasāyo'"rthajñānaṃ" rūpādi"jñānaṃ" ca ta"dādi"ryasya jvaraharaṇādeḥ | tasyaikārthasya "sādhane" karaṇe "svabhāvena" prakṛtyā svahetudattayā "bhedepi" bhedāviśeṣepi "kecid" bāhuleyādayo "niyatā" na karkādaya "indriyādivat" | yathā cakṣūrūpālokamanaskārādayaeva bhedāviśeṣepi rūpavijñānaṃ janayanti na śrotraśabdādayaḥ || (72)

{3.73}

[3.73,0]

etadeva dṛṣṭāntareṇa dṛḍhayannāha |

[3.73,1]

"jvarādiśamane kāścit saha pratyekameva vā | dṛṣṭā yathā vauṣadhayo nānātvepi na cāparāḥ || 73 ||"

[3.73,2]

"jvarādiśamane" karttavye"kāścit" gūḍūcyādayaḥ "saha" parasparaṃ "pratyekamvā dṛṣṭā | " gūḍūcīmustādayo bhinnāstathā trapuṣādayopi | tathāpi kāścijjvaraṃ śamayanti na sarvvāḥ | evaṃ śābaleyādaya ekapratyavamarśaṃ kurvvanti | "na" karkādayaḥ || (73)

{3.74}

[3.74,0]

syādetat | tāsvoṣadhīṣu sāmānyaṃ kiñcidasti tat jvarādiśamanaṃ karoti | tannaiṣa dṛṣṭāntaḥ | ityāha |

[3.74,1]

"aviśeṣānna sāmānyamaviśeṣaprasaṅgataḥ | tāsāṃ kṣetrādibhedepi dhrauvyāccānupakārataḥ || 74 ||"

[3.74,2]

"aviśeṣāt" sāmānyasyākriyāvasthātaḥ kriyāvasthāyāṃ "na sāmānyaṃ" kāñcidarthakriyāmupakalpayati | "tāsāṃ" gūḍūcyādivyaktīnāṃ "kṣetrādibhedepi" sāmānyasya kāryiṇo'viśiṣṭatvāt jvaraśamanādeḥ kāryasyā"viśeṣaprasaṅgataḥ" cirakṣiprapraśamanādyabhāvāsakteḥ |"dhrauvyāccānupakārataḥ" | sāmānyasya nityatvāt | anyebhyaḥ sahakāribhya upakārābhāvāt sakṛt tatkāryāṇi syuḥ || (74)

{3.75}

<ga apohasya vijātīyavyāvarttakatvam>

[3.75,0]

apohaviṣayatve śabdavikalpayoḥ sāmānyaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaṃ dharmidharmabhāvañca vyavasthāpayitumāha |

[3.75,1]

"tatsvabhāvavikalpā dhīstadarthe vāpyanarthikā | vikalpikā'tatkāryārthabhedaniṣṭhā prajāyate || 75 ||"

[3.75,2]

"tasyo"tpalādeḥ śabdādeśca svalakṣaṇasya "svabhāva"grahādūrdhvaṃ yā "vikalpikā dhīḥ " vastuto"'narthi"kāpi "tadartheva" svalakṣaṇaviṣayevā'dhyavasāyānurodhāt paramārthatā"'tatkāryebhyo arthebhyo bhedo" vyāvṛttistatra "niṣṭhā"'vasthānaṃ yasyā sā tathā vijātīyavyāvṛttiviṣayetyarthaḥ || (75)

{3.76–3.77}

[3.76–3.77,0]

"tasyāṃ yadrūpamābhāti bāhyamekamivānyataḥ | vyāvṛttamiva nistatvaṃ parīkṣānaṅgabhāvataḥ || 76 ||"

[3.76–3.77,1]

"arthā jñānaniviṣṭāsta evaṃ vyāvṛttarūpakāḥ | abhinnā iva cābhānti vyāvṛttāḥ punaranyataḥ || 77 ||"

[3.76–3.77,2]

"tasyāṃ" vikalpabuddhau "yad rūpaṃ" ya ākāro dṛśyavikalpayorekatvādhyavasāyābhyāsadāḍhryādabāhyamapi bāhyamivāsādhāraṇamapyekamiva sarvvavyaktiṣu sadṛśavṛtteḥ | yathā yathā vyaktayo dṛśyante tathā tathaivādhyavasāyāt vyāvṛttamiva vijātīyavyāvṛttavastvabhedena niścayāt | na ca tadvyāvṛttaṃ gorūpatvaprasaṅgāt | ata eva nistatvaṃ niḥsvarūpaṃ yathābhūtarūpatirodhānenānyathādhyavasāyāt | tathā cāparīkṣāyā vicārasyā"naṅgabhāvā"danāśrayānnistatvaṃ tat dvividhaṃ tvartho jñānaṃ vā | na caitat tathā | yataḥkāraṇāt tena kalpitena sāmānyarūpeṇa "te'rthā" ekārthakriyākāriṇo'tatkāryebhyo "vyāvṛ"ttasvabhāvā "jñānaniviṣṭā" vikalpabuddhyārūḍhā "abhinnā ivā bhāntyutpalatvādinā" śabdatvādinā "ca" |

[3.76–3.77,3]

etena sāmānyavyavasthoktā | ta evaikajātyavasitā'nyato'nīlāt nityācca nīlamityādivikalpākāreṇa ekena tatkāritā vyāvṛttarūpatā'dhyavasāyaviṣayeṇa viśeṣitā vyāvṛttā ābhānti nīlotpalamiti śabdasyānityatvamiti || (76–77)

{3.78}

[3.78,0]

"ta eva teṣāṃ sāmānyasamānādhāragocaraiḥ | jñānābhidhānairvyavahāro mithyārthaḥ pratanyate || 78 ||"

[3.78,1]

"teṣā"mubhayavyāvṛttiviśeṣitānāṃ vikalpārūḍhānāmarthānāṃ "sāmānyayo"rvviśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhūtayorddharmadharmirūpayośca sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ "samānādhāro" bhāvapradhānatvānnirdeśasya | sa "gocaro" yeṣāntai"rjñānābhidhānai"rvvikalpaśabdairvviśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvasya dharmidharmabhāvasya "vyavahāro mithyārthaḥ pratanyate" vistāryate || (78)

{3.79–3.80}

[3.79–3.80,0]

"sa ca sarvaḥ padārthānāmanyonyābhāvasaṃśrayaḥ | tenānyāpohaviṣayaḥ tadatatkāryakāriṇām || 79 ||"

[3.79–3.80,1]

"vastulābhāśrayo;"

[3.79–3.80,2]

"sa ca" jñānābhidhānalakṣaṇo viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvādivyavahāraḥ "sarvvaḥ padārthānāṃ" tadatatkāryakāriṇā"manyotyasya" itaretarasyā"bhāvo" vyavacchedaḥ"saṃśrayo" viṣayo yasya sa tathā | "tena" vyavacchedaviṣayatvenā"pohaviṣayo" vyavasthāpyate |"vastuno lābhasya" prāpteścā"śrayo" nimittaṃ sa vyavahāro bhavati || (79)

[3.79–3.80,3]

"yatra yathoktānumittau yathā | nānyatra bhrāntisāmyepi dīpatejo maṇau yathā || 80 ||"

[3.79–3.80,4]

yatra vyavahāre vastunaḥ sambandhaḥ paraṃparayā tadutpatterasti"yathoktānumitau" yādṛśī sādhyapratibaddhakāryasvabhāvānupalambhaliṅgajānumitiruktā | tatra "yathā" paraṃparayā vastusambandhād vastuprā"ptirnānyatra bhrāntisāmyepi dīpatejo maṇau " | kuñcikāvivaradeśasthe dīpatejasi bhrāntyā samāropite maṇauparamparayāpi vastusambandhābhāvānna prāptiḥ | evaṃ yadyapi sarvvasya vikalpasya svapratibhāse'nartherthādhyavasāyena vṛtterbhrāntatvaṃ tathāpi yo vastusambandhavān sa tatprāpako netara iti yukto vibhāgaḥ || (80)

{3.81}

[3.81,0]

nanu yadi jñānaniviṣṭānāmarthānāṃ sāmarthyādivyavahārastadā bāhyeṣu sa na syādityāha |

[3.81,1]

"tatrānekopi kāryaikā na tatkāryaparāśrayaiḥ | jñānābhidhānairekatvāt vyavahāraḥ pratāryate || 81 ||"

[3.81,2]

"tatra" gavāśvādivyaktiṣu madhye"'nekopi" sāvaleyabāhuleyādirekamabhedāvasāyādikāryaṃ yasya "jñānābhidhānaiḥ" kīdṛśaistadvāhādyakāryaṃ "kāryaṃ" na bhavati yeṣāṃ karkādīnāṃ tebhyo'nyatā tadvyavacchedaḥ sa "āśrayo" viṣayo yeṣāṃ "tairekatvena " prāpyate | śāvaleyādirvijātīyavyāvṛtau vyāvṛttyāśrayaiḥ śabdajñānairekatvena vyavahniyate ityarthaḥ || (81)

{3.82}

[3.82,0]

"tataścaikopyanekakṛt tadbhāvaparidīpanāt | atatkāryārthabhedena nānādharmaḥ pratīyate || 82 ||"

[3.82,1]

"tataścaikopi dīpādirā"lokāndhakārāpanayanavartidāhā"dyanekakāryakṛt" | "tadbhāvasyā"nekakāryakāritvasya "paridīpana"nimitta"matatkāryārthe"bhya ekaikakāryasamarthebhyo "bhedena" vyavacchedena "nānādharmaḥ pratīyate" śabdavikalpaiḥ | yathā'nālokakāribhyo bhedādālokakṛdanandhakārahantṛbhyo bhedādandhakārahantā dīpa ucyata ityādi || (82)

{3.83}

[3.83,0]

"yathāpratīti kathitaḥ śabdārthosāvasannapi | sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca vastunyasya na sambhavaḥ || 83 ||"

[3.83,1]

tadevaṃ "yathāpratīti" saṃvyavahārānatikrameṇa"śabdārthaḥ" sāmānyalakṣaṇaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ "viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaśca ca śabdāt kathito'sannapi paramārthataḥ | " cāvastveva || (83)

{3.84}

[3.84,0]

"dharmmadharmmivyavasthānaṃ bhedo'bhedaśca yādṛśaḥ | asamīkṣitatatvortho yathā loke pratīyate || 84 ||"

[3.84,1]

tathā "dharma dharmmiṇorvyavasthāniyamaḥ" śabdo dharmyeva kṛtakatvaṃ "dharma eva | tayo" śabdo dharmī kṛtakatvaṃ dharma itya"bheda"śca kṛtako'nityaśca śabda "ityādi | " dharmāntarapratikṣepāpratikṣepābhyāmukto'"samīkṣitatatvortho"'lakṣitatatvo yathā loke "pratīyate" || (84)

{3.85}

[3.85,0]

"taṃ tathaiva samāśritya sādhyasādhanasaṃsthitiḥ | paramārthāvatārāya vidvadbhiravakalpyate || 85 ||"

[3.85,1]

"taṃ" dharmmidharmmādivibhāgaṃ "tathaiva samāśritya sādhyasādhanasaṃsthitirvvidvadbhi" | "paramārthe" vastusvabhāvabhūte kṣaṇikatvādā"vavatārāya" lokasya vastutvakṣaṇikatvayorbhedaḥ paraḥ kalpitaḥ vastu tu kṣaṇikameva | tacca sādhyasādhanakalpanayā śakyaṃ pratyetuṃ || (85)

{3.86}

[3.86,0]

kasmāt punarvvastuni sāmānyadharmidharmādi nāstītyāha |

[3.86,1]

"saṃsṛjyante na bhidyante svatorthāḥ pāramārthikāḥ | rūpamekamanekañca teṣu buddherupaplavaḥ || 86 ||"

[3.86,2]

"pāramārthikā arthāḥ svataḥ" svarūpeṇa "na saṃsṛjyante" | yataḥ sāmānyaṃ vastu syāt | "nāpi bhidyante" kṛtakatvaśabdatvādinā yato dharmidharmabhedo bhavet | yattu "teṣu""rūpamekaṃ" gotvādyanuyāyi | "aneka"ñca śabdakṛtakatvādi vyavahriyate'sau buddheranādivāsanopahatāyā "upalpavo" mithyopadarśanaṃ || (86)

{3.87}

[3.87,0]

"bhedastatopi bauddhe'rthe sāmānyaṃ bheda ityapi | tasyaiva cānyavyāvṛttyā dharmabhedaḥ prakalpyate || 87 ||"

[3.87,1]

"tato"yaṃ viśeṣa idaṃ "sāmānya"miti "bheda" idaṃ sādhyamidaṃ sādhanamityapi bhedo "bauddhe" buddhiparikalpite'"rthe" na vastuni | kathantarhi svalakṣaṇe kṛtakatvādi"bheda" ityāha | "tasyaiva" svalakṣaṇasyānyasmādakṛtakāde"rvyāvṛtyā" tadāśrayeṇa "dharmabhedaḥ "(87)

{3.88}

[3.88,0]

kasmāt kalpitabhedadvāreṇa sādhyasādhanabhāva iṣṭo na vastubhedenetyāha |

[3.88,1]

"sādhyasādhanasaṃkalpe vastudarśanahānitaḥ | bhedaḥ sāmānyasaṃsṛṣṭo grāhyo nātra svalakṣaṇam || 88 ||"

[3.88,2]

"sādhyasādhanasaṃkalpe" idaṃ sādhyamidaṃ sādhanamiti vikalpe kriyamāṇe "vastudarśanasya hānitaḥ" kalpita eva bhedaḥ | na khalu vikalpe vastudarśanamasti kalpitagocaratvāt tasya | ālocanājñānaṃ vastuviṣayaṃ na kiñcit tad vibhajati |

[3.88,3]

nanvācāryādi gnā sya "bhedaḥ sāmānyasaṃsṛṣṭo grāhya" iṣṭaḥ | "atra" bhedaḥ sāmānyasaṃsṛṣṭaḥ pratīyate ityasmin vacane "na svalakṣaṇaṃ" grāhyatayā nirdiṣṭaṃ kintvadhyavaseyatayā || (88)

{3.89}

[3.89,0]

kasmādevamityāha |

[3.89,1]

"samānabhinnādyākārairna tad grāhyaṃ kathañcana | bhedānāṃ bahubhedānāṃ tatraikasminnayogataḥ || 89 ||"

[3.89,2]

"samānabhinnādyākāraiḥ" sāmānyākāradharmidharmabhedākārasāmānādhikaraṇyādyākāraiśca "tat" svalakṣaṇaṃ "kathañcana grāhyaṃ" na bhavati | kiṃ kāraṇamityāha | "bhedānāṃ"dharmāṇāṃ kṛtakatvādīnāṃ "bahubhedā"nāmanekaprakārāṇāṃ "tatra" svalakṣaṇa "ekasminna" || (89)

{3.90}

[3.90,0]

"tadrūpaṃ sarvato bhinnaṃ tathā tatpratipādikā | na śrutiḥ kalpanā vāsti sāmānyenaiva vṛttitaḥ || 90 ||"

[3.90,1]

tasmāt tasya svalakṣaṇasya "rūpaṃ sarvvataḥ" sajātīyavijātīyād "bhinnaṃ tathā" tena sarvvato bhinnena rūpeṇa "tatpratipādikā śrutiḥ kalpanā vā nāsti | sāmānyenaiva" kalpitena rūpeṇa śabdavikalpayo"rvṛttitaḥ" || (90)

{3.91}

[3.91,0]

kiṃ punaḥ svalakṣaṇameva śabdairnocyate ityāha |

[3.91,1]

"śabdāḥ saṃketitaṃ prāhurvyavahārāya sa smṛtaḥ | tadā svalakṣaṇaṃ nāsti saṅketastena tatra na || 91 ||"

[3.91,2]

"śabdāḥ saṃketita"marthamā"hurna" yaṃ kañcit |"sa" saṃketo "vyavahārāya " | saṃketitamarthaṃ śabdāduccaritāt pratipadyeyamiti saṃketagrahaṇaṃ | "tadā" vyavahārakāle ca "svalakṣaṇaṃ" saṃketaviṣayo "nāsti tena tatra" svalakṣaṇe "saṃketo " yuktaḥ || (91)

{3.92}

[3.92,0]

evantarhi sāmānye vyavahārakālānuyāyini saṃketaḥ syādityāha |

[3.92,1]

"api pravartteta pumān vijñāyārthakriyākṣamān | tatsādhanāyetyartheṣu saṃyojyante'bhidhākriyāḥ || 92 ||"

[3.92,2]

"apipravartteta pumān" śabdād "vijñāyārthakriyākṣamān" | tasyā arthakriyāyāḥ "sādhanāyeti" | etadarthama"rtheṣu saṃyojyante" saṃketyante śabdā na vyasanitayā || (92)

{3.93}

[3.93,0]

"atrānarthakriyāyogyo nāsti tadvānalaṃ sa ca | sākṣānna yojyate kasmādānantyāccedidaṃ samam || 93 ||"

[3.93,1]

tatraivaṃ satyanarthakriyāyāṃ yogyo'rthakriyāyāṃ śaktā jātiriti na tatra saṅketo yuktaḥ | "tadvān" jātimān viśeṣo"'laṃ" śaktorthakriyāyāmiti tatra saṃketa iti cet | "sa" viśeṣaśca "sākṣāt" saṃṅkete "kasmānna yojyate" | kiṃ jātivyavadhisvīkāreṇa anarthakriyākāritvādasyāḥ svalakṣaṇasya ca viparyayāt | vyaktīnā"mā" tatra śakya iti "cet | ida"mānantyaṃ "samaṃ" jātimadvyaktiṣvapi || (93)

{3.94}

[3.94,0]

"tatkāriṇāmatatkāribhedasāmye na kiṃ kṛtaḥ | tadvaddoṣasya sāmyāccedastu jātiralaṃ parā || 94 ||"

[3.94,1]

kiñca yāmarthakriyāmuddiśya śabdaniyoga"statkāri"marthānā"matatkāri"bhyo yo "bhedo" vyavacchedastadeva "sāmyaṃ" sāmānyamanyāpohaḥ sādhāraṇatvāt | tatra "kiṃ" saṃketo na kṛtaḥ sāmānyavadapohopi sādhāraṇo'narthakriyākārī svalakṣaṇasambandhāt tadupalabhyarūpaścaḥ | "tadvaddoṣasya" jātimati saṃketaviṣaye ānantyāt saṃketākaraṇasya "sāmyāccedastu" doṣaḥ samānatvāt | dvayorasta "jātiḥ parā'lamanu"payuktā jātimabhyupetyāpi vijātīyavyavacchedo' vaśyāśrayaṇīyaḥ | yadi gauraśvādibhyo na vyavacchinnastadā'śva eva syāt | yaścaikasya vyavacchedaḥ sa sarvvasya | sa eva saṅketaviṣayo'stu kiṃ pramāṇabādhitajātisvīkāreṇa | ata eva tadvaddoṣopi na sambhavati | abhyupagamya tu sāṃpratamāpāditaṃ || (94) kiñca |

{3.95}

[3.95,0]

"tadanyaparihāreṇa pravartteteti ca dhvaniḥ | tena tebhyo'vyavacchede pravartteta kathañca saḥ || 95 ||"

[3.95,1]

tasmādekārthakriyākāriṇo"'nya"sya "parihā"reṇa śabdāt "pravarttateti "nirucyate | "tena" dhvaninā "tebhyo"'tatkāribhyo'"sya" tatkāriṇo'vyavacchede vyavacchede'kriyamāṇe "kathaṃ" sa śrotā pratiniyatapadārthārthī pravartteta "viṣayānabhi" || (95)

{3.96}

[3.96,0]

atha śabdairvyavacchedaḥ kriyata eva pravṛttiviṣayastu jātirucyata ityāha |

[3.96,1]

"vyavacchedosti cedasya nanvetāvat prayojanam | śabdānāmiti kiṃ tatra sāmānyenāpareṇa vaḥ || 96 ||"

[3.96,2]

"asya" jātimato "vyavacchedo'sti cet | nanvetāvadanyavyavacchedena pravarttanaṃ "miṣṭa"miti sāmānyenāpareṇa" kiṃ kāryaṃ vaḥ | tadantareṇa ca śabdādanyavyavacchedābhidhānepi pravṛttisaṃbhavāt || (96)

{3.97}

<(6) sāmānyābhāve pratyabhijñāsaṃgatiḥ>

[3.97,0]

yadi nāsti jātistadā bhinnasvabhāveṣu bhāveṣu sa evāyaṃ gaurityādi pratyabhijñānaṃ na syādityāha |

[3.97,1]

"jñānādyarthakriyāṃ tāṃstāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhedena kurvataḥ | arthāntadanyaviśleṣaviṣayairdhvanibhiḥ saha || 97 ||"

[3.97,2]

"jñānamādi"ryasyā bāhā"dyarthakriyā"yāstāmekākāraparāmarśaviṣayāṃ "bhedena" nānātvepi "kurvvato"rthān "dṛṣṭvā tadanya"smād yo "viśleṣaḥ" sa "viṣayo" yeṣāṃ "tairddhvanibhiḥ " || (97)

{3.98}

[3.98,0]

"saṃyojya pratyabhijñānaṃ pūrvadṛṣṭānyadarśane | parasyāpi na sā buddhiḥ sāmānyādeva kevalāt || 98 ||"

[3.98,1]

"saṃyojya" sa evāyaṃ gaurityādi"pratyabhijñānaṃ pūrvadṛṣṭā"darthād vilakṣaṇasya "darśanepi" kuryāt | tadanyaviśleṣasya sarvvatra sāmyāt ||

[3.98,2]

kiñca | yadi nānātvāt pratyabhijñānamayuktaṃ tadā "parasyāpi na sā" pratyabhijñā "buddhiḥ sāmānyādeva kevalādiṣṭā" kintu sāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ | (98)

{3.99–3.101}

[3.99–3.101,0]

kasmādityāha |

[3.99–3.101,1]

"nityaṃ tanmātravijñāne vyaktayajñānaprasaṅgataḥ |"

[3.99–3.101,2]

"nitya"tayā "tasya" sāmānya"mātrasya vijñāne vyaktyajñānaprasaṅgataḥ" ||

<ṅa tadvattāniścayaḥ>

[3.99–3.101,3]

"tadā kadācit sambaddhasyāgṛhītasya tadvataḥ || 99 ||"

[3.99–3.101,4]

"tadvattāniścayo na syād vyavahārastataḥ katham |"

[3.99–3.101,5]

yadā sāmānyajñānasya na viśeṣo viṣaya"stadā kadācidagṛhītasya sambaddhasya" sāmānyena "tadvato" viśeṣasya (99) "tadvattāniścaya" idamasya sāmānyamiti jñānaṃ "na " | tatastadvattāvyavahāraḥ kathaṃ tvanmate ||

[3.99–3.101,6]

"ekavastusahāyāśced vyaktayo jñānakāraṇam || 100 ||"

[3.99–3.101,7]

"tadekaṃ vastu kiṃ tāsāṃ nānātvaṃ samapohati | nānātvāccaikavijñānahetutā tāsu neṣyate || 101 ||"

[3.99–3.101,8]

ekaṃ vastu sāmānyaṃ tatsahāyāśced vyaktayo jñānasya pratyabhijñānasya kāraṇamiṣyante | "tadekaṃ" sāmānyaṃ "vastu kintāsāṃ" vyaktīnāmamiśrasvabhāvānāṃ "nānātvaṃ " | yena pratyabhijñānahetutve |"nānātvāccaikasya" pratyabhijñā"jñānasya hetutā tāsu" tvayā "neṣyate" | taccet tathaiva na syātpratyabhijñānam || (100–101)

{3.102}

[3.102,0]

"anekamapi yadyekamapekṣyābhinnabuddhikṛt | tābhirvināpi pratyekaṃ kriyamāṇāndhiyaṃ prati || 102 ||"

[3.102,1]

"tenaikenāpi sāmānyāt tāsāṃ netyagrahe dhiyā |"

[3.102,2]

"anekamapi" vyaktirūpaṃ "yadyekaṃ" sāmānya"mapekṣyābhinnabuddhikṛt" pratyabhijñānakārīṣyate | "tābhi"rvyaktibhiḥ pratyekaṃ"vinaikai"kayā preritena sāmānyenaikena "kriyamāṇāṃ " pratyabhijñāṃ pratibhāsāṃ vyaktīnāṃsāmarthyaṃ neti tayā dhiyā tāsāmagrahaḥ | kevalaṃ sāmānyagrahaṇe ca tadvattā niścayo na syāditi duḥpariharaṃ || (102)

{3.103}

[3.103,0]

nanu yathā nīlādīnāmekaikāpāyepi cakṣurvvijñānaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tatsamudāyepi dṛśyate | evaṃ yadyapi pratyekaṃ vyaktīnāṃ vyabhicārastathāpi yadā satvaṃ tadā viṣayatvamityāha ||

[3.103,1]

"nīlādernetravijñāne pṛthak sāmarthyadarśanāt || 103 ||"

[3.103,2]

"nīlādernetravijñāne" kārye "pṛthak" pratyekaṃ "sāmarthyadarśanāt" | (103)

{3.104}

[3.104,0]

"śaktisiddhiḥ samūhepi naivaṃ vyakteḥ kathañcana |"

[3.104,1]

"śaktisiddhiḥ samūhepi yuktā | evaṃ vyakternna" pratyabhijñānajanane sāmarthyaṃ kathañcana dṛṣṭaṃ yena samudāyepi sāmarthyakalpanā syāt ||

[3.104,2]

"tāsāmanyatamāpekṣyaṃ taccecchaktaṃ na kevalam || 104 ||"

[3.104,3]

"tāsāṃ" vyaktī"nāmanyatamāpekṣyaṃ" tat sāmānyaṃ pratyabhijñāne "śaktaṃ" na "kevalamiti " || (104)

{3.105}

[3.105,0]

"tadekamupakuryustāḥ kathamekāndhiyañca na | kāryaśca tāsāṃ prāptosau jananaṃ yadupakriyā || 105 ||"

[3.105,1]

tatsāmānya"mekaṃ" kathantā vyaktaya "upakuryuḥ" | "na tvekā"ndhiyamanupakriyamāṇasya samavetatve'tiprasaṅgād vyaktibhiḥ sāmānyamupakarttavyaṃ | tathā dhīrapyekopakarttavyā | yacca sāmānyādirupakriyate vyaktibhiḥ "kāryaśca tāsāṃ prāptosau "smā"dupakriyā" jananameva | na hyupakriyamāṇādanyasminnupakārākhye vastuni kṛtepi tasya kiñcit | tatsambandhāccet | sambandho bhinna eveti kintasya jātaṃ | "abhinne" tūpakāre sa eva kṛtaḥ syāt | tathā jananamevopakāraḥ || (105)

{3.106}

[3.106,0]

"abhinnapratibhāsā dhīrna bhinneṣviti cenmatam | pratibhāso dhiyā bhinnaḥ samānā iti tadgrahāt || 106 ||"

[3.106,1]

ekasāmānyābhāve"'bhinnapratibhāsā" ekākārā "dhīrna bhinneṣviti cenmataṃ" | nanu "pratibhāso dhiyā bhinno" naikākāraḥ "samānā" imā "iti tā"sāṃ vyaktīnāṃ "grahāt" | na hi bhūta kaṇṭhaguṇavadekaṃ sāmānyaṃsarvvānupāyi vyaktivyatiriktaṃ pratibhāti | kintu gaurgauriti sāmānyamavasīyate tacca bhedādhiṣṭhānameva || (106)

{3.107}

[3.107,0]

"kathantā bhinnadhīgrāhyāḥ samāścedekakāryatā | sādṛśyaṃ nanu dhīḥ kāryaṃ tāsāṃ sā ca vibhidyate || 107 ||"

[3.107,1]

nanu samāśced vyaktayodhyavasīyante | "kathaṃ tā bhinnadhīgrāhyāḥ" | na khalu "sama"tvamekatvaṃ ki"ntvekakāryatāsādṛśyaṃ" | na hi sa evāyaṃ tadatra veti ni"ścayaḥ" | api tvayamapi gaurityadhyavasāyaḥ | tathā caikārthakriyākāritvameva sādṛśyaṃ | "nanu dhīḥ kāryaṃ tāsāṃ" vyaktīnāṃ "sā ca" prativyakti "bhidyate" tatkathamekārthakriyākāritvaṃ sādṛśyaṃ | (107)

{3.108}

[3.108,0]

ata āha |

[3.108,1]

"ekapratyavamarśasya hetutvād dhīrabhedinī | ekadhīhetubhāvena vyaktīnāmapyabhinnatā || 108 ||"

[3.108,2]

yadyapi prativyakti bhinnā tathāpyeka"pratyavamarśasya" hetutvād dhīrabhedinyekā'bhidhīyate | tathāvidhāyāścaikasyā dhiyo hetubhāvena "vyaktīnāmabhinnato"cyate || (108)

{3.109}

[3.109,0]

"sā cātatkāryaviśleṣastadanyasyānuvartinaḥ | adṛṣṭeḥ pratiṣedhācca saṃketastadvidarthikaḥ || 109 ||"

[3.109,1]

"sā cā"bhinnatā"'tatkā"ryebhyaḥ padārthebhyo "viśleṣo" vyavacchedastatkāriṇāṃ vastubhūtajātireva kinneṣyate ityāha | "tato" vyavacchedā"danyasya" anuvarttinaḥ sāmānyasya "vastusato'dṛṣṭeḥ" svabhāvānupalabdhyā "pratiṣedhācca" | tataśca "saṃketastadvidarthika"stasya vyavacchedasya vidartho yasyāsti sa tathā || (109)

{3.110}

[3.110,0]

"atatkārivivekena pravṛtyarthatayā śrutiḥ | akāryakṛtitatkāritulyarūpāvabhāsinīm || 110 ||"

[3.110,1]

saṃketa"ścātatkārivivekena pravṛttyaryatayā" pravṛttiprayojanatvena kṛtaḥ | tataśca śrutirapi dhiyaṃ janayantyarthena visaṃvādiketi sambandhanīyaṃ | kīdṛśīṃ "dhiyaṃ" | svākāre"'kāryakṛti" | kāryakāraṇāsamarthe "tatkāri" tulyarūpāvabhāsinīmekārthakriyākārisarvvavastusādhāraṇaikarūpādhyavasāyinīṃ || (110)

{3.111}

[3.111,0]

"dhiyaṃ vastupṛthagbhāvamātrabījāmanarthikām | janayantyapyatatkāriparihārāṅgabhāvātaḥ || 111 ||"

[3.111,1]

"vastu" nastatkāriṇo'tatkāribhyaśca "pṛthagbhāva" eva kevalaḥ "sa bījaṃ kāraṇaṃ yasyā"stā"manarthikā"marthaśūnyāṃ paramārthataḥ |

[3.111,2]

kathamavisamvādikā tarhi setyāha |

[3.111,3]

"atatkā"riṇāṃ vijātīyānāṃ "parihāra"syā"ṅgabhāvataḥ" kāraṇatvāt "tadvyavacche"dasya viṣayatvāttatra pravṛttiḥ || (111)

{3.112}

[3.112,0]

"vastubhedāśrayāccārthe na visaṃvādikā matā | tatonyāpohaviṣayā tatkartrāśritabhāvataḥ || 112 ||"

[3.112,1]

vastubhedāśrayācca vastuviṣayasya paraṃparayā hetutvāt tatra pravarttayantī śrutirarthe na visaṃvādikā matā | tatonyāyohaviṣayā tatkartrāśritabhāvataḥ | tatkāryakartṛ vastvāśritatvāt || (112)

{3.113}

[3.113,0]

"avṛkṣavyatirekeṇa vṛkṣārthagrahaṇe dvayam | anyonyāśrayamityekagrahābhāve dvayāgrahaḥ || 113 ||"

[3.113,1]

nanu saṃketakāle"'vṛkṣavyatirekeṇa vṛkṣārtha"sya "grahaṇe dvayamanyonyāśrayaṃ" vṛkṣo'vṛkṣaścānyonyāpekṣa ityekasya vṛkṣasyāvṛkṣasya cāvyavasthitatvāt "grahābhāve dvayāgrahaḥ" prāptaḥ | niścite hi vṛkṣe tadabhāvaḥ śakyo niścetuṃ | avṛkṣatve ca niścite vṛkṣo niśceya ityekāniścayād dvayāniścayaḥ || (113)

{3.114–3.115}

[3.114–3.115,0]

"saṅketāsambhavastasmāditi kecit pracakṣate | teṣāmavṛkṣāssaṅkete vyavacchinnā na vā;"

[3.114–3.115,1]

"seṅketāsambhavastasmāditi keci" jjai mi nī yāḥ "pracakṣate | teṣāmeva" vādināṃ jātāvapi "saṅkete" kriyamāṇe'"vṛkṣā vyavacchinnā na vā" |

[3.114–3.115,2]

"yadi || 114 ||"

[3.114–3.115,3]

"vyavacchinnāḥ kathaṃ jñātāḥ prāgvṛkṣagrahaṇādṛte | anirākaraṇe teṣāṃ saṅkete vyavahāriṇām || 115 ||"

[3.114–3.115,4]

"yadi vyavacchinnā" iṣyante "kathaṃ" saṃketāt prāk "jñātā vṛkṣagrahaṇā"dṛte saṃketād vṛkṣasyājñātatvād avṛkṣāḥ kathaṃ jñātāḥ | atha na vyavacchinnāḥ tadā'nirākaraṇe "teṣāṃ" saṃkete "vyavahāriṇāṃ" vyavahārakāle || (115)

{3.116–3.120}

[3.116–3.120,0]

"na syāt tatparihāreṇa pravṛttirvṛkṣabhedavat | avidhāya niṣidhyānyat pradarśyaikaṃ puraḥ sthitam || 116 ||"

[3.116–3.120,1]

"vṛkṣoyamiti saṃketaḥ kriyate tat prapadyate | byavahārepi tenāyamadoṣa iti cet;"

[3.116–3.120,2]

teṣāmavṛkṣāṇāṃ "parihāreṇa na syāt pravṛttiḥ vṛkṣabhedavad" | yathā vṛkṣaviśeṣāṇāṃ vṛkṣasaṃkete'vyavacchinnatvāt pravṛttiviṣayatvamevamavṛkṣāṇāmapi syāt | nanve"kaṃ" śākhādimantaṃ "puraḥsthitaṃ pradarśya" tasmā"danyadavidhāya niṣidhya" ca | (116) "vṛkṣoyamiti ca saṃketaḥ kriyate" vastusāmānyādibhiḥ "tat" saṃketaviṣayaṃ sāmānyaṃtatsambandhibāhyalakṣaṇaṃ "vyavahāre prapadyate tenāyama"nantarokta"doṣo na" bhavatīti "cet" ||

[3.116–3.120,3]

"taruḥ || 117 ||"

[3.116–3.120,4]

"ayamapyayameveti prasaṅgo na nivarttate | ekapratyavamarśākhye jñāne;"

[3.116–3.120,5]

atra cā"yamapi" śākhādimāṃstarura"yameva" taru"riti" pūrvvako'vṛkṣāvyavaccheda"prasaṅgo na" nivarttate'tra cokta eva doṣa iti dvayorapyeṃkāgrahāt dvayāsambhavāt saṅketāsambhavaḥ samānaḥ | idānīṃ parihartumāha |"ekapratyavamarśā"khye "jñāne" bhedāviśeṣepi kecideva bhāvā ekākārādhyavasāyahetavo netare || (117)

[3.116–3.120,6]

"ekatra hi sthitaḥ || 118 ||"

[3.116–3.120,7]

"prapattā tadataddhetūnarthān vibhajate svayam | tadbuddhivartino bhāvān bhāto hetutayā dhiyaḥ || 119 ||"

[3.116–3.120,8]

"aheturūpavikalānekarūpāniva svayam | bhedena pratipadyetetyuktirbhede niyujyate || 120 ||"

[3.116–3.120,9]

ta"traika"sminnekākārajñānādhyavasāye "sthitaḥ pratipattā" puruṣa"stada" | yānekākāraparāmarśaviṣayabuddhyādihetūnadhyavasyati | yāṃścānyathā tān yathākramaṃ taddhetūnataddhetūścaṃ bhedena vyavasthāpayati saṃketāt "prāgeva" ekākāraparāmarśaviṣayān "bhavān" śākhādimato "dhiya" ekākārāyā "hetutayā bhātaḥ" pratibhāsamānā "na heto"rekākārabuddhyakāraṇasya śākhādimatvarahitasya "rūpeṇa vikalān" paramārthabhinnā"napyekarūpāniva svayamā"tmanā saṃketayitā manyamānaḥ pratipādyopi tānatatkāribhyaḥ śākhādimatvarahitebhyo "bhede"nāsaṃkareṇa "pratipadyeteti | " śabdo "bhede'"nyāpohe "niyujyate" | (118–20)

{3.121–3.122abc}

[3.121–3.122abc,1]

{3.145–3.146}

[3.145–3.146,1]

[3.145–3.146,5]

"tad vyaṅgyaṃ yogyatāyāśca kāraṇaṃ kārakaṃ matam | prāgevāsya ca yogyatve tadapekṣā na yujyate || 146 ||"

[3.145–3.146,6]

"yat" svarūpeṇa sthitameva sāmānyaṃ svaviṣaya"vijñānotpattiyogyatvāyātmanya" parāpekṣaṃ "tad vyaṅgyamu"cyate | yacca yogyatāyāḥ svarūpabhūtāyāḥ kārakaṃ tat kāraṇaṃ mataṃ | vyatiriktayogyatākaraṇe tu na syāt sāmānya syopalabdhiḥ | upalambhāyogyasvabhāvatvāt | yogyatāsambandhepyanupalabhyasvabhāvānapāyāt tadavastho'nupalambhaḥ | atha vyañjakābhimatairvviśeṣairna yogyatā kriyate tadā sā prāgevāstīti syāt | tathā "ca prāgevāsya yogyatve tadapekṣā" vyañjakāpekṣā "na " | (145–146)

[3.147,0]

"sāmānyasyāvikāryasya tatsāmānyavataḥ kutaḥ |"

[3.147,1]

[3.147,2]

atha na sāmānyasya saṃskārād vyaktirvyañjikā kintvindriyasyāñjanavadityāha |

[3.147,3]

"añjanāderiva vyakteḥ saṃskāro'kṣasya na bhavet || 147 ||"

[3.147,4]

"tatpratipatterabhinnatvāt tadbhāvābhāvakālayoḥ |"

[3.147,5]

"añjanāderive"ndriyasya "na" saṃskāro "vyakteḥ" sakāśāt | "tatpratipatte"stasyā vyakte"rbhāvābhāvakālayorabhinnatvāt" | na hi yathendriyasyāñjanasaṃskārabhāvābhāvayorarthapratipatteḥ spaṣṭāspaṣṭalakṣaṇo viśeṣaḥ tathā vyaktibhāvābhāvakālayoḥ sāmānyapratīteḥ sarvvadā tulyākāratvāt tasyāḥ ||

[3.148–3.156,3]

"na yāti na ca tatrāsīdasti paścānna cāṃśavat || 151 ||"

pratyayaścānuyāyī | karma pacanādi taddheturiti cet | āha |

{3.157–3.173}

[3.157–3.173,0]

"bhedānna hetuḥ karmāsya na jātiḥ karmasaṃśrayāt |"

[3.157–3.173,1]

bhedānna hetuḥ karmādi | karmāpi prativyaktyekasyāmapi paurvvāparyeṇa bhinnameva tatkathaṃ vyaktivadekābhidhānahetuḥ | karmasāmānyaṃ hetuścedāha | asya karmaṇo jātirnābhinnā'bhidhānahetuḥ | tasyāḥ karmasaṃśrayāt | karmaṇi samavetatvāt tatraivābhidhānahetutā syānna dravye |

[3.157–3.173,2]

atha karmasāmānyaṃ karmaṇi sambaddhaṃ tacca dravya iti paramparayā tatsambaddhaṃ tannimittaḥ śabdo dravye varttata ityāha |

[3.157–3.173,3]

"śrutyantaranimittatvāt karmaṇo na nimittatā || 157 ||"

[3.157–3.173,4]

"asaṃbaṃdhānna sāmānyaṃ nāyuktaṃ śabdakāraṇāt | atiprasaṃgāt ;"

[3.157–3.173,5]

"śrutyantarasya" pācakādiśabdādanyasya pāka ityādiśabdasya "nimitatvā"t "karmaṇo" dravye pācakaśabdavṛttau nāsti nimittatā paraṃparayāpi | tathā'nityatvāt sthityabhāvācca karmaṇastasminnivṛtte pācakādipratipattirnna syāt | apacatyapitadvyapadeśo dṛśyate | nityatvāt karmasāmānyaṃ pācakavyapadeśe hetuścedāha | asambandhāt | dravyeṇa karmasāmānyasya na sambandhaḥ sākṣāt tatrāsamavāyāt | nāpi paraṃparayā karmaṇā tatsamavetasya naṣṭatvātsamavāyinā sāmānyena sambandhābhāvāt | nasāmānyaṃ "śabda"sya pācakādeḥ "kāraṇānnāyuktaṃ" kiṃtvayuktamevāti"prasaṅgāt" | karmatvasya sambandhavyatirekeṇa vyapadeśahetutve sarvvatra tathātvaprasaṅgaḥ (157) ||

[3.157–3.173,6]

apacatyapi puruṣe'tītānāgataṃ karma tadvyapadeśanimittamiti cet | āha |

[3.157–3.173,7]

"karmāpi nāsajjñānābhidhānayoḥ || 158 ||"

[3.157–3.173,8]

"anaimittikatāpatteḥ ;"

[3.157–3.173,9]

na karmāsadapi jñānābhidhānayorheturanaimittikatāyā āpatteḥ | hetuṃ vinā bhavato'hetukatvaprasaṅgāt | atītānāgatañca karmāvidyamānatvādasadeva |

[3.157–3.173,10]

pākādinirvarttikā śaktiḥ pācakādivyapadeśaheturiti cet | āha |

[3.157–3.173,11]

"na ca śaktirananvayāt |"

[3.157–3.173,12]

"śakti"rhi dravyādabhinnā bhinnā vā pratipannā | abhinnā cet tadā dravyava"dananvayānna" cānvayino'nvayiśabdahetutā | atha bhinnā tadā'nupakārakayoḥ sambandhānupapatterdravyeṇopakriyamāṇā śaktistatsambandhinīti vaktavyaṃ | atrāpi dravyaṃ śaktyantareṇa svayamevāsamarthasvabhāvatayā śaktimupakarotīti vācyaṃ | ādye'navasthā dvitīye tu kāryameva kinna karotītyalaṃ śaktisvīkāreṇa ||

[3.157–3.173,13]

"sāmānyaṃ pācakatvādi yadi prāgeva tadbhavet || 159 ||"

[3.157–3.173,14]

"vyaktaṃ sattādivanno cenna paścādaviśeṣataḥ | kriyopakārāpekṣasya vyañjakatve'vikāriṇaḥ || 160 ||"

[3.157–3.173,15]

"atiśaye vā hyapyasya kṣaṇikatvāt kriyā kutaḥ |"

[3.157–3.173,16]

abhinnābhidhāne nimittaṃ "sāmānya"meva"pācakatvādi yadī"ṣyate tadā pākādikriyātaḥ "prāgeva tat" pācakatvādi sāmānyaṃ dravyotpattāveva "vyaktaṃ bhavet" | no cet prāgavyaktaṃ na "paścā"dapi vyaktaṃ "syādaviśeṣa"to viśeṣābhāvāt | nityaikarūpasya sāmānyasya kriyāyāḥ karmaṇaḥ pākādi na "upakāra"stadapekṣasya dravyasya pācakatvādisāmānya"vyañjakatve" ceṣyamāṇe"'vikāriṇaḥ" sthirasya dravyasyāpekṣā nāsti | "atiśaye vā" prāgavasthātaḥ svīkriyamāṇe kṣaṇikatvaṃ syāt | "kṣaṇikatvā"dutpattyanantaravināśitvāt "kriyā" karma kutaḥ sambhavati | utpattyanantaraṃ sthitau hi karma kuryāt | sā ca kṣaṇikasya nāstīti na tenopakāropi |

[3.157–3.173,17]

"tulye bhede yayā jātiḥ pratyāsattyā prasarpati || 161 ||"

[3.157–3.173,18]

[3.157–3.173,19]

vastubhūtasāmānyavādinopi vyaktīnāṃ "tulye bhede" parasparamekārthakaraṇādikayā "yayā pratyāsattyā kvacid" vyaktau śāvaleyabāhuleyayo"rjātiḥ" | saiva pratyāsattirabhinnasya "śabdajñānasya nibandhama"stu kiṃ pramāṇāntarabādhitajātisvīkāreṇa ||

<kha. sāṃkhyamatanirāsaḥ>

[3.157–3.173,20]

sāṃ khyā prāhuḥ |

[3.157–3.173,21]

"na nivṛttiṃ vihāyāsti yadi bhāvānvayoparaḥ || 162 ||"

[3.157–3.173,22]

"ekasya kāryamanyasya na syādatyantabhedataḥ |"

[3.157–3.173,23]

"yadi nivṛttiṃ" vijātīyavyavacchedaṃ "vihāya bhāvānāṃ" satvarajastamaḥsāmyāvasthāsvabhāvaprakṛtyātmanā'dvaya ekarūpo'"nvayo'paro nāsti" | "tadekasya kārya"maṅkuro"'nyasya" kṣityāderna "syāt" | bījakṣityādīnāma"tyantabhe" | aṅkurakārakaṃ yad rūpaṃ bījasya taccet kṣityādernnāsti na syādasau tatkārakaḥ | astitve caikarūpānvayaḥ |

[3.157–3.173,24]

siddhāntavādyāha |

[3.157–3.173,25]

"yadyekātmatayānekaḥ kāryasyaikasya kārakaḥ || 163 ||"

"yadyekātmatayā'neko" bījaśalilādiḥ "kāryasyā"ṅkura"syaikasya kārakasta"dāṅkurakāraka "ātmā"'nuyāyī | "ekatrāpi" bīje'nyatra vā"stīti vyarthāḥ sahakāriṇaḥ " ekatra vidyamānenaiva tenātmanā kāryotpatteḥ |

[3.157–3.173,28]

"nāpaityabhinnaṃ tad rūpaṃ viśeṣāḥ khalvapāyinaḥ || 164 ||"

[3.157–3.173,29]

"ekāpāye phalābhāvād viśeṣebhyastadudbhavaḥ |"

[3.157–3.173,30]

sahakāriṇāmabhāvepi bījasatve"'bhinnaṃ tat" pradhānaṃ karttṛ"rūpaṃ nāpaiti"nityatvāt vyaktisatvācca | "viśeṣāḥ khalu nūnamapāyino" na pradhānaṃ |"ekasya" sahakāriṇo viśeṣasyā"pāye"pi phalasyā"bhāvāt | viśeṣebhyasta"sya kāryasya "udbhavo" niścīyate na pradhānāt | viśeṣasyānvayavyatirekānuvidhānāt | sāmānyasyaviparyayāt |

[3.157–3.173,31]

"sa pāramārthiko bhāvo ya evārthakriyākṣamaḥ || 165 ||"

[3.157–3.173,32]

"sa ca nānveti yonveti na tasmāt kāryasambhavaḥ |"

[3.157–3.173,33]

sa eva "pāramārthiko bhāvo yorthakriyākṣamaḥ |" viśeṣorthakriyākṣamo "nānveti" parasparaṃ bhedāt | "yo'nveti" pradhānākhyo bhāvo "na tasmāt kāryasya " |

[3.157–3.173,34]

yadyekarūpānanugamastadā viśeṣeṣvapi kecijjanayanti nāpara iti kutoyaṃvibhāga ityāha |

[3.157–3.173,35]

"tenātmanāpi bhede hi hetuḥ kaścinna cāparaḥ || 166 ||"

[3.157–3.173,36]

"svabhāvoyamabhede tu syātāṃ nāśodbhavau sakṛt |"

[3.157–3.173,37]

yenaikarūpānvaye sahakārivaikalyaprasaṅga"stena" kāraṇenā"tmanā" svarūpeṇa bījajalaśilānalādīnāṃ "bhedepi kaścit" kṣitiśalilabījādiraṅkurasya "heturna " śilānalādiḥ | "hi" yasmāt "svabhāvoyama"ṅkurajananaśaktaḥ | "taditaraśca" pramāṇadṛṣṭo bījādīnāṃ śilādīnāñca nātra paryanuyogāvatāraḥ | kuta utpanna iti cet | svasvahetoḥ | sopi kasmāt tajjanaka iti cet | svahetoḥ | "tatrāpi""praśne tadevottaraṃ" | anādiśca hetuphalaparaṃparaikarūpānugamād | viśeṣāṇā"mabhedetu" svīkriyamāṇe "sakṛde"kasya "nāśodbha" | viśeṣāntarayoryathāsaṃbhavaṃ nāśo janmani ca tadaparasya viśeṣasya tadabhinnarūpatayā nāśodbhavau syātā |

[3.157–3.173,38]

"bhedopi tena naivaṃ ced ya ekasmin vinaśyati || 167 ||"

[3.157–3.173,39]

"tiṣṭhatyātmā na tasyāto na syāt sāmānyabhedadhīḥ |"

[3.157–3.173,40]

atha parasparaṃ viśeṣāṇāmekāntena nābhedaḥ | kintarhi "bhedo" viśeṣarūpatayā | "tena" bhede"naivaṃ" sakṛnnāśodbhavaprasaṅgo "na cet" | yadyeka"smin" viśeṣe "vinaśyati" | "tiṣṭhatyātmā"nuyāyī pradhānākhyastadā sa "tasya" viśeṣasyātmā na bhavati | na hi yasmin vinaśyati yo "na" naṣṭaḥ sa tasya svabhāvo viruddhadharmādhyāsalakṣaṇatvādabhedasya | "ataḥ" parasparaṃ sarvvathā bhedā"nna syāt sāmānyabhedadhīḥ" | anvayi sāmānyamananvayī bheda ucyate | yadā ca sāmānyaṃ bhedād bhinnaṃ tadā'nugāmivyaktisvarūpaṃ na sāmānyaṃ | na ca tadātmako bhedaḥ | atastadbuddhirapi na bhavet |

[3.157–3.173,41]

nanvanyanivṛttāvapi samānametat | bhāve naśyati anyanivṛttirnaśyati na vā | yadi naśyati na syād vyaktyantare tadbuddhiḥ | atha na naśyati tadā'tyantabhedāta sāmānyabhedabuddhirna syādityāha |

[3.157–3.173,42]

"nivṛtterniḥsvabhāvatvāt na sthānāsthānakalpanā || 168 ||"

[3.157–3.173,43]

"upaplavaśca sāmānyadhiyastenāpyadūṣaṇā |"

[3.157–3.173,44]

"nivṛtterniḥsvabhāvatvāt na sthānāsthānayoḥ" sthitinivṛttyoḥ "kalpanā" yuktā | kalpitā hyanyanivṛttiḥ niḥsvabhāvā sā kiṃ bhāvād bhinnā'bhinnā veti na yuktā kalpanā | na hi śaśaviṣāṇaṃ bhinnamabhinnamveti yuktaṃ kalpiyituṃ | upaplavo mithyātvañca sāmānyadhiyo viṣayābhāvāt | tena nāpyadūṣaṇā ||

[3.157–3.173,45]

"yattasya janakaṃ rūpaṃ tatonyo janakaḥ katham || 169 ||"

[3.157–3.173,46]

"bhinnā viśeṣā janakāḥ ;"

[3.157–3.173,47]

nanūktaṃ yadi bhāvāḥ sarvvathā bhinnāstadā "yattasya" bījasya "janakaṃ rūpaṃ na" tadanyasya kṣityāderiti "tatonyo janakaḥ katha"miti | atrottaramapyuktamabhinnarūpānvayavyatirekānuvidhānābhāvād bhinnā"viśeṣā" eva "janakā"stadanvayavyatirekānuvidhānāt kāryasya sarvva eva te tatkāryasyotpādakatayotpannāstadutpādayanti |

[3.157–3.173,48]

"apyabhedopi teṣu cet | tena te'janakāḥ proktāḥ ;"

[3.157–3.173,49]

teṣu viśeṣeṣvanvayinā rūpeṇābhedopyasti tenaiva te janakā iti cet | tenānvayirūpeṇa te viśeṣā ajanakāḥ proktāḥ ekatrāpi viśeṣe tadbhāvāt sahakārivaiphalyaprasakteḥ | tadanvayavyatirekānarthavidhānād viśeṣasya viparyayācceti |

[3.157–3.173,50]

kiñca |

[3.157–3.173,51]

"pratibhāsopi bhedakaḥ || 170 ||"

[3.157–3.173,52]

"ananyabhāk sa evārthastasya vyāvṛttayopare |"

[3.157–3.173,53]

"pratibhāsopyananyabhāg bhedako" viśeṣāṇāmasaṃkīrṇṇarūpavyavasthāpanāt | api śabdādutpattisthitivināśādayaśca samānāḥ | tataśca viśeṣa evārthaḥ pāramārthikaḥ | ye "tvapare" sāmānyādayo dharmāste "tasya" śeṣasya vijātīyād "vyāvṛttayaḥ" kalpitā anarthakriyākāriṇaḥ |

[3.157–3.173,54]

"tat kāryaṃ kāraṇañcoktaṃ tatsvalakṣaṇamiṣyate || 171 ||"

[3.157–3.173,55]

[3.157–3.173,56]

arthakriyākāri tu yad rūpaṃ tatkārya "kāraṇañcoktaṃ tatsvalakṣaṇamiṣyate | "rthānarthaprāptiparihāraiṣiṇāṃ "pravṛttayaḥ sarvvāḥ" |

[3.157–3.173,57]

kiñca |

[3.157–3.173,58]

"yathā'bhedāviśeṣepi na sarvaṃ sarvvasādhanam || 172 ||"

[3.157–3.173,59]

"tathā'bhedāviśeṣepi na sarvvaṃ sarvvasādhanam |"

[3.157–3.173,60]

sāṃ khya syāpi mate "yathā'bheda"sya pradhānātmatayā sarvvabhāveṣva"viśeṣepi na sarvva" vyaktaṃ "sarvva"sya kāryasya "sādhanaṃ" hetuḥ | "tathā bhedāviśe" kṣitibījānalaśilādikaṃ "sarvva"sya tāpāṅkurādeḥ "sādhanaṃ" |

[3.157–3.173,61]

"bhede hi kārakaṃ kiñcid vastudharmatayā bhavet || 173 ||"

[3.157–3.173,62]

viśeṣāntarād "bhede hi" sati "vastudharmatayā" vastusvabhāvatvāt "kiñcid" vastu "kārakaṃ bhavet" | na sarvvamiti yuktaṃ svahetubalāyātatvād bhinnaśaktikatvasya | (173)

{3.174}

[3.174,0]

"abhede tu virudhyete tasyaikasya kriyākriye |"

[3.174,1]

"abhede tu" sarvvabhavānāṃ "virudhyete tasyaikasyā"ṅkurādeḥ "kriyākriye" bījarūpatayā pradhānamaṅkurakārakamakārakañca dahanarūpatayā | vipratiṣiddhañcaitat kathamekasya yuktaṃ ||

[3.174,2]

"bhedopyastyakriyātaścet na kuryuḥ sahakāriṇaḥ || 174 ||"

[3.174,3]

vyaktīnāṃ mitho vyaktirūpatayā "bhedopyasti" | vyaktyantarasādhyasya kāryasyā"kriyātaścet" | tadā bhedāt "sahakāriṇaḥ" kāryaṃ "na kuryuḥ" | ekasya yaḥ kārakaḥ svabhāvastasyānyatrābhāvāt | (174)

{3.175}

[3.175,0]

"paryāyeṇātha karttṛtvaṃ sa kiṃ tasyaiva vastunaḥ |"

[3.175,1]

atha kārakaikasvabhāvānugamāt sahakāriṇāṃ "paryāyeṇa karttṛtvaṃ" | sa paryāyastasyānvayina ekasya "vastunaḥ kiṃ" kasmāt yuktaḥ | na hyekaṃ vastu kārya kurvvata paryāyeṇa na karotīti yuktaṃ vyapadeṣṭuṃ tenaiva kriyamāṇatvāt | sahakāriṇāṃ bahūnāṃ paryāyeṇa kriyā sambhāvyate | teṣu caikasya kārakaṃ rūpamanyatra nāstīti na te kuryuḥ | sarvveṣāñca svahetuvalāyāta ekakāryakārakaḥ svabhāvo'smābhiriva sāṃ khyai rneṣyate ||

[3.175,2]

kiñca |

[3.175,3]

"atyantabhedābhedau tu syātāṃ tadvati vastuni || 175 ||"

[3.175,4]

"tadvati" sāmānyaviśeṣavati "vastuni" svīkriyamāṇe"'tyantame"kāntena sāmānyaviśeṣayorbhedābhedo "syātāṃ" | sāmānyasvarūpatvād bhedasya sāmānyameva bhavenna bhedo bhedātmatvāt sāmānyasya bheda eva bhavet sāmānyaṃ | (175)

{3.176–3.184aba}

[3.176–3.184aba,0]

atha tayoḥ kathañcana bhedopyastīti cedāha |

[3.176–3.184aba,1]

"anyonyaṃ vā tayorbhedaḥ sadṛśāsadṛśātmanoḥ |"

[3.176–3.184aba,2]

[3.176–3.184aba,3]

etadeva sphuṭayituṃ pūrvvapakṣayati |

[3.176–3.184aba,4]

"tayorapi bhaved bhedo yadi yenātmanā tayoḥ || 176 ||"

[3.176–3.184aba,5]

"bhedaḥ sāmānyamityetad yadi bhedastadātmanā | bheda eva;"

[3.176–3.184aba,6]

na sarvvātmanā'bheda"stayoḥ" sāmānyaviśeṣo"rapi" kathañcid "bhedo " | anyathā sāmānyaviśeṣabhāvānupapattiḥ | atrāha | "yenātmanā" svarūpeṇa sādhāraṇena cāsādhāraṇena ca "tayoḥ" sāmānyaviśeṣayo"rbhedaḥ sāmānyaṃ" viśeṣa "ityetad" vyavasthāpyate | tenātmanā sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇena "yadi bhedastadā" bheda eva "tayoḥ" syāt bhinnalakṣaṇatvāt |

[3.176–3.184aba,7]

"tathā ca syānniḥsāmānyaviśeṣatā || 177 ||"

[3.176–3.184aba,8]

"bhedasāmānyayoryadvad ghaṭādīnāṃ parasparam |"

[3.176–3.184aba,9]

"tathā ca niḥsāmānyaviśeṣatā" samānyaviśeṣarūpatā'bhāvaḥ sāmānyaviśeṣayorabhitayoḥ "syāt | yadvad ghaṭādīnāṃ" viśeṣāṇāṃ "parasparaṃ" na sāmānyaviśeṣatā | viśeṣaḥ svalakṣaṇarūpamanugāmi sāmānyaṃ tadevānugāmi viśeṣa ucyate | yadi tu tayorbheda eva na sāmānyaviśeṣabhāvaḥ syāt |

[3.176–3.184aba,10]

"yamātmānaṃ puraskṛtya puruṣoyaṃ pravartate || 178 ||"

[3.176–3.184aba,11]

"tatsādhyaphalavāñchāvān bhedābhedau tadāśrayau | cintyate svātmanā bhedaḥ ;"

[3.176–3.184aba,12]

api cāyaṃ vyavahārī "puruṣo yama"rthasyā"tmānaṃ" svabhāvaṃ "puraskṛtya" pravṛttiviṣayatvenāgrahaṃ kṛtvā "tatsādhyaphalavāñchāvān" arthasādhyaphalasamīhāyuktaḥ sana "pravarttate | tadāśrayau" tadarthaviṣayau "bhedābhedau" śāstrakāraiścintyete | na tvarthakriyānupayuktasāmānyaviṣayau | teṣāñcārthakriyākāriṇāṃ puruṣapravṛttiviṣayāṇāmarthānāṃ "svātmanā" svarūpeṇa "bhedaḥ" |

[3.176–3.184aba,13]

kathaṃ tarhyekabuddhiśabdaviṣayatetyāha |

[3.176–3.184aba,14]

"vyāvṛttyā ca samānatā || 179 ||"

[3.176–3.184aba,15]

<3. śabdacintā>

{3.184cd–3.200}

[3.184cd–3.200,0]

"dravyābhāvādabhāvasya śabdā rūpābhidhāyinaḥ || 184 ||"

[3.184cd–3.200,1]

"nāśaṅkyā eva siddhāste'tovyavacchedavācakāḥ |"

[3.184cd–3.200,2]

uktaṃ tāvad bhāvādiśabdānāṃ vyavacchedaviṣayatvaṃ | yepyabhāvādiśabdā "abhāvasya" svarūpā"bhāvāt" tepi "rūpābhidhāyino" vastuvācakā "nāśaṅakyā eva" | sambhavad vastu vācyaṃ syānna veti cintyetāpi | yatra tu vastveva nāsti tatra kā cintā | "ataste"'bhāvādiśabdā "vyavacchedasya" bhāvavyāvṛtte"rvvācakāḥ siddhāḥ" | tasmāt sthitametat svabhāvahetorvvastutaḥ sādhyātmakatvepi na pratijñārthaikadeśo hetuḥ | sādhyasādhanadharmidhvanivikalpānāṃ bhinnavyavacchedaviṣayatvāt | na ca sādhyādīnāṃ kalpitatvaṃ bhedasya kalpanāt | śabdatvena niścito dharmī sattvena ca hetuḥ | kṣaṇikatvena niścitaḥ sādhyaḥ | ityakalpitā eva dharmyādaya ityuktaṃ |

[3.184cd–3.200,3]

sa cāyaṃ svabhāvo hetuḥ ||

[3.184cd–3.200,4]

"upādhibhedāpekṣo vā svabhāvaḥ kevalo'thavā || 185 ||"

[3.184cd–3.200,5]

"ucyate sādhyasidhyarthaṃ nāśe kāryatvasattvavat |"

[3.184cd–3.200,6]

kvacidupādhibhedo viśeṣaṇaviśeṣo bhinno'bhinno vā tadapekṣaḥ | "kevalo" viśeṣaṇarahitaḥ śuddho"thavā sādhyasidhyarthamucyate nāśe kāryatvasattvavat" | nāśe sādhye kāryatvaṃ bhinnaviśeṣaṇā"pekṣaḥ svabhāvaḥ" tajjanmanyapekṣitaparavyāpārasya kāryatvāt | evaṃ pratyayabhedabheditvādayo draṣṭavyāḥ | utpattimatvaṃ punarabhinnaviśeṣaṇamutpattyā svabhāvabhūtayā kalpitabhedayā viśeṣaṇāt | sattvantu kevalaṃ nāśa eva sādhye svabhāvo viśeṣaṇānupādānāt |

[3.184cd–3.200,7]

"sattāsvabhāvo hetuścet sā sattā sādhyate katham || 186 ||"

[3.184cd–3.200,8]

[3.184cd–3.200,9]

[3.184cd–3.200,10]

arthānanvayinaḥ sādhyatā na yuktā tathā sādhanatāpi | tat kathaṃ sattvaṃ sādhanaṃ | tasmāt sattā sāmānyaṃ sādhyañca sādhanañcānanvayāt syāt |

[3.184cd–3.200,11]

atrāha |

[3.184cd–3.200,12]

"bhāvopādānamātre tu sādhye sāmānyadharmiṇi || 187 ||"

[3.184cd–3.200,13]

"na kaścidarthaḥ siddhaḥ syādaniṣiddhañca tādṛśam |"

[3.184cd–3.200,14]

asmākantu |

[3.184cd–3.200,39]

"bāhulyepīti cet tasya hetoḥ kvacidasambhavaḥ |"

[3.184cd–3.200,40]

"sāpekṣāṇāṃ bhāvānāṃ hi" yasmāda"vaśyaṃbhāvitā nekṣyate" rāgasyeva vāsasi | tataśca kaścid ghaṭo na vinaśyedapi | vināśakānāṃ hetūnāṃ bāhulyādavaśyaṃ iti cet | "bāhulyepi" tasya nāśakasya hetoḥ kvacid ghaṭādāvasambhavaḥ syāt | tadvyāghātakānāmapi bāhulyāt |

[3.184cd–3.200,41]

"etena vyabhicāritvamuktaṃ kāryāvyavasthiteḥ || 194 ||"

[3.184cd–3.200,42]

"sarveṣāṃ nāśahetūnāṃ hetumannāśavādinām |"

[3.184cd–3.200,43]

"etena" nāśahetūnāṃ pratirodhasambhavena hetumannāśavādināṃ matena "nāśahetūnāṃ" mudgarādīnāṃ "sarvveṣāṃ" nāśe kārye'numāpayitavye "vyabhicāritvamuktaṃ" boddhavyaṃ | "kāryā" | vināśahetorvināśasyotpattiniyamābhāvāt |

[3.184cd–3.200,44]

kathaṃ punarvvināśasyāhetutetyāha |

[3.184cd–3.200,45]

"asāmarthyācca taddhetorbhavatyeva svabhāvataḥ || 195 ||"

[3.184cd–3.200,46]

"yatra nāma bhavatyasmādanyatrāpi svabhāvataḥ |"

[3.184cd–3.200,47]

"asāmarthyācca taddheto"rvvinaśvarasya vā bhāvasya vināśaḥ kriyate nāśahetunā | tatra vinaśvarasya svayameva vināśādalaṃ nāśahetunā | avinaśvarasya nāśaṃ karttuṃ na kaścit samarthaḥ | ca śabdāt kriyāpratiṣedhaḥ syāt | tathā hyabhāvo yadi paryudāso bhāvāntaraṃ kapālādikaṃ tadā tasya mudgarādihetuteṣyata eva | tadutpādepi ghaṭasya na kiñciditi prāgvadupalabdhyādiprasaṅgaḥ | tasmādabhāvaṃ karoti. bhāvaṃ na karotīti syāt | tathā cākartturahetutaiva | tasmād vināśahetorayogāt eva vināśaḥ svabhāvataḥ svahetorbhavati "asmādi"ti bhāvo hetuḥ | "yatra nāma" vināśo "bhava"tīti mudgarāt kapālotpattau lokābhimānastatra vināśakāyogāt svahetoreva vinaśvarasvabhāvatayotpatterdvitīye kṣaṇe na bhavatīti vaktavyaṃ | tasmādahetutvavyavasthānādanyatrāpi yatra visadṛśānutpattyā vināśotpattyabhimāno nāsti tatrāpi "svabhāvataḥ" svahetoreva vinaśyatīti vināśa ekakṣaṇasthāyī bhāvo jāyate |

[3.184cd–3.200,48]

tathāvidhe ca bhāvamātrānurodhini vināśe satvaṃ heturavyabhicāraḥ kāryasya kāraṇe tadadhīnatvādityuktaṃ | tadevāha |

[3.184cd–3.200,49]

"yā kācid bhāvaviṣayā'numitirdvividhaiva sā || 196 ||"

[3.184cd–3.200,50]

"svasādhye kāryabhāvābhyāṃ sambandhaniyamāt tayoḥ |"

[3.184cd–3.200,51]

"yā kācid bhāvaviṣayānumitiḥ" sā "dvividhaiva kāryabhāvābhyāṃ" hetubhyāṃ kāraṇavyāpakaviṣayā bhavantī "tayoḥ" kāryasvabhāvayoḥ eva "svasādhye sambandhasya niyamāt |" anyasya tu sādhye'nāpatteratadātmatvācca nāvyabhicāraniyamaḥ |

<(2) anupalabdhicintā>

<ka. anupalabdheḥ prāmāṇyam>

[3.184cd–3.200,52]

anupalabdherapyupalabdhinivṛttimātralakṣaṇāyāḥ prāmāṇyamākhyātumāha |

[3.184cd–3.200,53]

"pravṛtterbuddhipūrvatvāt tadbhāvānupalambhane || 197 ||"

[3.184cd–3.200,54]

"pravarttitavyaṃ netyuktā'nupalabdheḥ pramāṇatā |"

[3.184cd–3.200,55]

sajjñānaśabdavyavahārāṇāṃ"pravṛtterbuddhipūrvvakatvāt ta"syā buddhe"rbhāvānupalambhane" kāraṇābhāvāt pravartitavyaṃ neti sāmarthyāt sidhyati | na hi kāraṇābhāvaṃ kāryaṃ yuktaṃ | ato'nupalabdherupalabdhinivṛttirupāyāḥ pravṛttiniṣedhe sādhye pramāṇatoktā cā rye ṇa | na piśācādikaṃ ghaṭādikaṃ saditi vaktavyamanupalabdheriti sadvyavahārapratiṣedhamātraṃ sādhyate na tvasattvavyavahāraḥ |

[3.184cd–3.200,56]

yatra tarhi pratyakṣānumānayoḥ śāstrasya nivṛttistasyābhāva eva sādhayituṃ yukta ityāha |

[3.184cd–3.200,57]

"śāstrādhikārāsambaddhā bahavorthā atīndriyāḥ || 198 ||"

[3.184cd–3.200,58]

"aliṅgāśca kathanteṣāmabhāvonupalabdhitaḥ |"

[3.184cd–3.200,59]

"śāstrādhikāre'sambaddhā" anena śāstraviṣayatvamāha | "bahavo'rthā" aniyatakāraṇopanipātajanyāḥ sūkṣmā durllakṣabhedā manovṛttayo janmināṃ | deśaphalavyavahitā vā'nutpannā dravyaviśeṣā "atīndriyāḥ" | anena pratyakṣāviṣayatāmāha | liṅgāccānanumeyatāmāha | "teṣāma"rthānāṃ pratyakṣānumānaśāstranivṛttilakṣaṇāyā "anupalabdhitaḥ " sādhayituṃ yuktaḥ | satyapyanupalambhe teṣāṃ sattvasambhavāt |

[3.184cd–3.200,60]

ata īdṛśyanupalabdhiḥ |

[3.184cd–3.200,61]

"sadasanniścayaphalā neti syād vā'pramāṇatā || 199 ||"

[3.184cd–3.200,62]

"pramāṇamapi kācit syād liṅgātiśayabhāvinī |"

[3.184cd–3.200,63]

"sato'sanniścayaphalā neti apramāṇatā" vā'syāḥ syāt | sattvapratiṣedhe sādhye "kācit" tvanupalabdhirlliṅgajā pratītirasminneva sādhye "pramāṇamapi" liṅgaviśeṣaprabhavā | yathoktaṃ prāgghetubhedavyapekṣayeti | upalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptānupalabdhiliṅgajetyarthaḥ |

[3.184cd–3.200,64]

"svabhāvajñāpakājñānasyāyaṃ nyāya udāhṛtaḥ || 200 ||"

[3.184cd–3.200,65]

yat punaruktamapramāṇamanupalabdhiriti | yasya kasyacit "svabhā"vasya jñāpakasyaliṅgasya cā"jñānasyā"nupalabdhe"rayaṃ nyāya udāhṛtaḥ" | na hi svabhāvo nopalabhyataityeva nāsti | deśakālasvabhāvaviprakṛṣṭānāmadarśanepi sattvāvirodhāt | tato nāsti viraktaceta ityādyayuktaṃ | na ca kāraṇamityeva kāryāṇyavyavadhānato bhavanti | tato nāsti dānahiṃsāviraticetanānāmabhyudayahetutā "phalānantaryā"bhāvādityayuktaṃ | (200)

{3.201–3.212aba}

[3.201–3.212aba,0]

"kārye tu kārakājñānamabhāvasyaiva sādhakam |"

[3.201–3.212aba,1]

kārakājñānantu kārye'bhāvasyaiva sādhakaṃ | na hyasati kāraṇe kāryasaṃbhavaḥ ||

[3.201–3.212aba,2]

"svabhāvānupalambhaśca svabhāverthasya liṅgini || 201 ||"

[3.201–3.212aba,3]

"tadabhāvaḥ pratīyeta hetunā yadi kenacit ||"

[3.201–3.212aba,4]

tathā"rthasya" vyāpakatayā niścitasya "svabhāvasyānupalambhaśca svabhāve" vyāpye liṅginyasattayā sādhye sādhanaṃtadā ca kāraṇavyāpakānupalabdhī gamike "yadi kena" ciddhetunopalabdhilakṣaṇaprāptānupalambhenānyena vā tayoḥ kāraṇavyāpakayorabhāvaḥ pratīyate | na tūpalambhābhāvamātreṇa sandigdhāsiddhatvāt |

<kha. svabhāvānupalabdhiḥ>

[3.201–3.212aba,5]

svabhāvānupalambhamāha |

[3.201–3.212aba,6]

"dṛśyasya darśanābhāvakāraṇā'sambhave sati || 202 ||"

[3.201–3.212aba,7]

"bhāvasyānupalambhasya bhāvābhāvaḥ pratīyate |"

[3.201–3.212aba,8]

"dṛśyasya" vastuno "darśanābhāva"sya yat "kāraṇaṃ" vyavadhānendriyavaikalyādi tasyā"sambhave" sati "bhāvasyā"nupalabdhasya "bhāva" "ābhāvaḥ" svabhāvānupalabdheḥ "pratīyate" ||

<ga. anupalabdhirevābhāvaḥ>

[3.201–3.212aba,9]

"viruddhasya ca bhāvasya bhāve tadbhāvabādhanāt || 203 ||"

[3.201–3.212aba,10]

"tadviruddhopalabdhau syādasattāyā viniścayaḥ |"

[3.201–3.212aba,11]

"viruddhasya" nivarttakasya vahnayāde"rbhāvasya bhāve ta"sya "śa"lilādernivarttyasya "bhāvabādhanāt | tadviruddhopalabdhau" satyāma"sattāyā viniścayaḥ" syāt |

[3.201–3.212aba,12]

nanvanupalabdherabhāvasādhane ko dṛṣṭāntaḥ | vyomakusumādiriti cet | atrāpi yadyanupalabdherabhāvasiddhistadā dṛṣṭāntāntarāpekṣāyāmanavasthāprasaṅgaḥ | tadanapekṣāyāṃ tadanupalabdhirabhāvākhyaṃ pramāṇamastu |

[3.201–3.212aba,13]

asambaddhametat | na hyabhāvo'nupalabdhyā sādhyate | anupalabdhireva hyabhāvaḥ sa ca siddha eva | tathāpi tu mūḍhaḥ tamavyavaharan nimittopadarśanena vyavahāryate | tathā ca bhāvo'bhāvasya daṣṭāntaḥ | tayoḥ svanaimittikapravarttanasya siddhatvāt |

[3.201–3.212aba,14]

nanu yadidaṃna santi pradhānādayo'nupalabdheriti tatra kathamasadvayavahāravidhiḥ sadvyavahārapratiṣedho vā | pradhānādiśabdavācyasya pratiṣedhe tacchabdāprayogāt |

[3.201–3.212aba,15]

atrāha |

[3.201–3.212aba,16]

"anādivāsanodbhūtavikalpapariniṣṭhitaḥ || 204 ||"

[3.201–3.212aba,17]

"śabdārthastrividho dharmo bhāvābhāvobhayāśrayaḥ |"

[3.201–3.212aba,18]

"anādivi"kalpābhyāsa"vāsanāyā udbhūtavikalpe pariniṣṭhitaḥ" pratibhāsamānaḥ śabdārtho dharmo trividhaḥ | kathamityāha | "bhāvābhāvobhayāśrayaḥ" | sadasadubhayavikalpavāsanāprabhavatvāt | tadadhyavasāyena tadviṣayatvāt | "tatra bhāvopādāno" vikalpaḥ paṭādirabhāvopādānaḥ śaśavi"śā"ṇādiḥ | "ubhayopādānaḥ pradhāne"śvarādiḥ |

[3.201–3.212aba,19]

"tasmin bhāvānupādāne sādhye'syānupalambhanam || 205 ||"

[3.201–3.212aba,20]

"tathā heturna tasyaivābhāvaḥ śabdaprayogataḥ |"

[3.201–3.212aba,21]

"tasmi" śabdārthe pradhānādau "bhāvānupādāne" bhāvabhūtapradhānāśraye "sādhye"'syapradhānāde"stathā" bāhyabhāvāśrayatvenā"nupalambhanaṃ hetu"rvyavahārasādhanaḥ | na tu "tasya" śabdārthasyaivābhāvaḥ pradhānādi"śabda"sya tatpratipādakasya "prayogataḥ" ||

[3.201–3.212aba,22]

yadi tu vastveva śabdaviṣayastadā |

[3.201–3.212aba,23]

"paramārthaikatānatve śabdānāmanibandhanā || 206 ||"

[3.201–3.212aba,24]

"na syāt pravṛttirartheṣu darśanāntarabhediṣu |"

[3.201–3.212aba,25]

"paramārthaikatānatve" paramārthaikaparavṛttitve "śabdānāmartheṣu darśanāntarabhediṣu" pratidarśanaṃ bhinnābhyupagamena nityatvānityatvatriguṇīmayatvādikalpi"tabhedeṣu " paramārthanibandhanarahitā "pravṛttirna syāt" | na hi parasparaviruddhā bahavo dharmā ekatra santi |

[3.201–3.212aba,26]

"atītājātayorvāpi na ca syādanṛtārthatā || 207 ||"

[3.201–3.212aba,27]

"vācaḥ kasyāścidityeṣā bauddhārthaviṣayā matā |"

[3.201–3.212aba,28]

"atītājātayorvvapyasatorna" syācchabdavṛttiḥ | "na ca kasyāścid vāco'nṛ" | arthamantareṇa śabdābhāvāt | yasmādete doṣā vastuviṣayatve vāca iti tasmādeṣā "bauddhārthaviṣayā" kalpitārthagocarā matā |

[3.201–3.212aba,29]

yaśca śabdārthaḥ tasya bhāvānupādānatvaṃ sādhyate na tu sa eva niṣidhyate'nyathā |

[3.201–3.212aba,30]

"śabdārthāpahnave sādhye dharmādhāranirākṛteḥ || 208 ||"

[3.201–3.212aba,31]

"na sādhyaḥ samudāyaḥ syāt siddho dharmaśca kevalaḥ |"

[3.201–3.212aba,32]

"śabdārthasyāpahnave sādhye dharmādhāra"sya dharmiṇo"nirākṛteḥ samudāyaḥ sādhyo " | dharmidharmasamudāyaścānumeyaḥ | dharma eva kevalaḥ sādhyate iti cet "siddho"bhāvādiḥ "kevalaḥ" | kimarthaṃ sādhanīyaḥ pradhānādivikalpasya bhāvānupādānatvaṃ tu na siddhaṃ tadeva sādhyaṃ yuktaṃ |

[3.201–3.212aba,33]

kiñca |

[3.201–3.212aba,34]

"sadasatpakṣabhedena śabdārthānapavādibhiḥ || 209 ||"

[3.201–3.212aba,35]

"vastveva cintyate hyatra pratibaddhaḥ phalodayaḥ |"

[3.201–3.212aba,36]

[3.201–3.212aba,37]

tataśca |

[3.201–3.212aba,38]

"arthakriyā'samarthasya vicāraiḥ kiṃ tadarthinām || 210 ||"

[3.201–3.212aba,39]

"ṣaṇḍhasya rūpe vairūpye kāminyā kiṃ parīkṣayā |"

[3.201–3.212aba,40]

"arthakriyāyāmasamarthasya" śabdārthāde"rvvicāraiḥ" sadasatpakṣacintābhi"stadarthinā"marthakriyārthināṃ "kiṃ" na kiñcit prayojanaṃ | "ṣaṇḍhasya" napunsakasya "rūpe vairūpye" vā kāminyā vṛṣasyantyā yoṣitaḥ "kiṃ parīkṣayā" |

<gha. kalpitasyānupalabdhirdharmaḥ>

[3.201–3.212aba,41]

[3.201–3.212aba,43]

{iii.iv}

<4. āgamacintā>

{3.212cd–3.216}

[3.212cd–3.216,0]

nanu yaduktaṃ | pramāṇatrayanivṛttāvapi nārthābhāvaniścaya iti tanmā "bhūt" pratyakṣānumānayorasarvvaviṣayatvāt tannivṛttyā (') bhāvaniścayaḥ | āgamastu sarvvaviṣaya iti tannivṛttau yukto'rthāsattvaniścaya ityāha |

[3.212cd–3.216,1]

"nāntarīyakatā'bhāvācchabdānāṃ vastubhissaha || 212 ||"

[3.212cd–3.216,2]

"nārthasiddhistataste hi vakttrabhiprāyasūcakāḥ ||"

[3.212cd–3.216,3]

"nāntarīyakatā"yā avinābhāvasyā"bhāvād vastubhiḥ saha śabdānāṃ | tataḥ" śabdebhyo "nārthasya siddhi"rniścayaḥ | kintarhi tebhyo gamyata ityāha | "vakturabhiprāyasya" vivakṣāyā"ste" śabdāḥ "sūcakā"stadanvayavyatirekānuvidhāyitvāt | na ca vivakṣā yathārthaṃ bhavatiyena paraṃparayā tatsamvādaḥ syāt | visamvādābhiprāyādajñānād vā'nyathāpi vivakṣāsambhavāt |

[3.212cd–3.216,4]

"āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyādanumānatā || 213 ||"

[3.212cd–3.216,5]

yadyevaṃ sarvvameva vacanaṃ pravṛttikāmānāṃ parīkṣārhaṃ syāt | kaśca samvādārthaḥ kathañcāptavādasāmānyādanumānatāsyā cā rye ṇoktetyāha |

[3.212cd–3.216,6]

"sambaddhānuguṇopāyaṃ puruṣārthābhidhāyakam | parīkṣādhikṛtaṃ vākyamatonadhikṛtamparam || 214 ||"

[3.212cd–3.216,7]

"sambaddha"vākyānāṃ parasparābhisambaddhānāmekārthopasaṃhārāt | na ca daśadāḍimādivākyamivaikārthānabhidhāyi | "anuguṇoṇāyaṃ" śakyānuṣṭhānopeyasādhanaṃ na tu viṣaśamanatakṣakaphaṇāratnālaṅkāropadeśakamiva "puruṣārthasya" svargāpavargasyā"bhidhāyakaṃ" na tu kākadanta"parīkṣo"padeśakamiva parīkṣāyāṃ pravṛttyarhaviṣayama"dhikṛtaṃ vākyaṃ | "navadhānārhatvāt |

[3.212cd–3.216,8]

"pratyakṣeṇānumānena dvividhenāpyabādhanam | dṛṣṭādṛṣṭārthayorasyāvisaṃvādaḥ tadarthayoḥ || 215 ||"

[3.212cd–3.216,9]

asya ca parīkṣārhasya vākyasyāvisamvādaḥ "tadarthayo" rāgamābhidheyayo"rdṛṣṭā"pratyakṣāpratyakṣa yorarthayoḥ "pratyakṣeṇānumānena" ca "dvividhene"ti vastubalabhāvinā'gamāśrayeṇa cā"bādhana"manyeṣāñca bādhanaṃ nāma | yathā pratyakṣatvena sammatānāṃ pañcānāṃ skandhānāṃ pratyakṣeṇābādhanaṃ siddhireva apratyakṣatveneṣṭānāṃ śabdāditriguṇamayatvadravyakarmasāmānyasaṃyogādīnāñca tena bādhanaṃ | anumeyatveneṣṭānāṃ caturāryasatyānāṃ vastubalapravṛttenānumānenābādhanaṃ siddhireva | ananumeyatveneṣṭānāñcātmeśvarādīnāmanumānena bādha eva | atyantaparokṣāṇāṃ rāgādihetukā'dharmaprahāṇādīnāmāgamāśrayānumānenābādhanaṃ siddhirevaṃ rāgādihetutveneṣṭasya hetutvānuparodhinaḥ snonovāsāgnihotrādeḥ prahāṇopāyatayā'nupadeśāt hetuvyāghātasyopāyatvenopadeśāccaivaṃ vidhamabādhanama"visamvāda" iṣṭaḥ |

[3.212cd–3.216,10]

"āptavādāvisaṃvādasāmānyādanumānatā | buddheragatyā'bhihitā niṣiddhāpyasya gocare || 216 ||"

[3.212cd–3.216,11]

tasyaivaṃ bhūtasyā"ptavāda"syādṛṣṭavyabhicārasyā"visamvādasāmānyāt" pratyakṣānumānāgamyepyarthe utpannāyā "buddhe"ravisamvādā"danumānatā" cā cārya di gnā ge nā"bhihitā""gatyā" | atyantaparokṣeṣvartheṣu dānahiṃsācetanādiṣvarthānarthaśravaṇādāgamaprāmāṇyamanāśritya sthātumasāmarthyādetadbhāve virodhābhāvācca satyāṃ pravṛttau varamevaṃ pravṛttirityagatyā'numānatoktā | na tu vastuto vacanānāmartheṣu nāntarīyakatvābhāvāt | (216)

{3.217}

[3.217,0]

kimvā |

[3.217,1]

"heyopādeyatattvasya sopāyasya prasiddhitaḥ | pradhānārthāvisamvādādanumānamparatra vā || 217 ||"

[3.217,2]

"heya"sya duḥkhasatyasya "upāde"yasya nirodhasatyasya"sopāyasya" yathākramaṃ samudayasatyasya samārgasatyasya cāgamoktavastubalapravṛttenānumāne "prasiddhito" niścayāt | satyacatuṣṭayādhigamasya nirvvāṇahetutvena "pradhānārtha"syā"visamvādāt" | "paratrā"tyantaparokṣepyarthe bhaga vadvacanādutpannaṃ jñānama"numānaṃ" yuktamiti vā pakṣāntaraṃ | (217)

{3.218}

[3.218,0]

"puruṣātiśayāpekṣaṃ yathārthamapare viduḥ | iṣṭoyamarthaḥ pratyetuṃ śakyaḥ sotiśayo yadi || 218 ||"

[3.218,1]

"apare" nai yā yi kā dayaḥ "puruṣa"syā"tiśayāpekṣaṃ" yathābhūtārthadarśi tadākhyāt puruṣapraṇītaṃ vacanaṃ "yathārthaṃ" satyārthaṃ pratijānīyuḥ |

[3.218,2]

siddhāntamāha | puruṣātiśayapraṇītaṃ vacanama pramāṇamitī"ṣṭo'yamartho yadi" puruṣāṇāṃ "sotiśa"yo jñātuṃ śakyaḥ syāt |

{3.219–3.223}

<(1) pauruṣeyatve>

<ka. puruṣātiśayapraṇītaṃ vacanaṃ pramāṇam>

[3.219–3.223,0]

kintu |

[3.219–3.223,1]

"ayamevaṃ na vetyanyadoṣānirdoṣatāpi vā | durlabhatvāt pramāṇānāṃ durbodhetyapare viduḥ || 219 ||"

[3.219–3.223,2]

"ayaṃ" pumā"nevaṃ"doṣavān "na vā" nirdoṣa ityanyasya"doṣā nirdoṣatāpi vā pramā" sau ga tā "viduḥ" | durbbodhetyanyadoṣā ityanenaliṅga vacanavipariṇāmena sambandhanīyaṃ |

[3.219–3.223,3]

tatkimaśakyocchedā doṣā netyāha |

[3.219–3.223,4]

[3.219–3.223,5]

"sarvveṣā"māsravāṇāṃ rāgādīnāṃpratipakṣasaṃmukhībhāvābhāvayornnirhrāsātiśayāvupacayāpacayau śrayanta iti "nirhrāsātiśayaṃ śrita"steṣāṃ "savipakṣatvāt" pratipakṣasambhavāt tasya pratipakṣasyā"bhyāsāt sātmībhāvādāsravā" kva1ciccittasantāne "hīyeranni"ti khalu nirdoṣapuruṣāpalāpaḥ kriyate kintu tadavadhāraṇopāyo nāstītyucyate | icchādhīnasya vyāhārasyānyathāpi karttuṃ śakyatvāt | na tatastathārthaniścayaḥ |

[3.219–3.223,6]

atha sātmīyabhūtapratipakṣasya mārgābhyāsānnirdoṣatāyāmapi satyāṃ vipakṣābhyāsāt punardoṣotpattirityāha |

[3.219–3.223,7]

"nirupadravabhūtārthasvabhāvasya viparyayaiḥ | na bādhā yatnavatve'pi buddhestatpakṣapātataḥ || 221 ||"

[3.219–3.223,8]

"nirupadrava"sya doṣarāśerudvejakasya prahāṇāt | "bhūtārtha"sya pramāṇaparidṛṣṭārthaviṣayatvāt | "svabhāva"syānāropitatvāt | mārgasātmyasya vipakṣeṇa "na bādhā " | yatna eva tāvanna sambhavati vipakṣābhyāse doṣadarśanāt | "yatnavatvepi" tu "buddhestatra" mārgasātmye'bhiruciviṣayatvena "pakṣapātato na bādhā" | na hi rajvāṃ nivṛttasarppabhramaḥ sarppaṃ bhāvayituṃ yatate kaścit | bhūtārthasya darśanāt |

<kha. satkāyadarśanaṃ doṣakāraṇam>

[3.219–3.223,9]

kaḥ punardoṣāṇāṃ heturyatprahāṇādamī prahīyanta ityā3ha |

[3.219–3.223,10]

"sarvvāsāṃ doṣajātīnāṃ jātiḥ satkāyadarśanāt |"

[3.219–3.223,11]

"sarvvāsāṃ doṣajātīnāṃ" doṣaprakārāṇāṃ "jāti"rjanma "satkāyadarśanādā"tmābhiniveśāt |

[3.219–3.223,12]

nanvavidyāhetukāḥ kleśā bha ga va to kto ityāha |

[3.219–3.223,13]

"sā'vidyā tatra tatsnehastasmād dveṣādisambhavaḥ || 222 ||"

[3.219–3.223,14]

"sā'vidyā" satkāyadarśanamevāvidyā'nyatrocyata iti nāsti virodhaḥ | "tatra" satkāyadarśane sati teṣvātmīyeṣu "snehastasmā"dātmīyeṣu snehāt tadapakāriṣu "dveṣā"nāṃ "sambhava" iti doṣotpattikramaḥ | ato nairātmyadarśanaṃ mārgo yuktaḥ satkāyadṛṣṭipratipakṣatvāt |

[3.219–3.223,15]

yataśca sattvadṛṣṭiravidyā |

[3.219–3.223,16]

"moho nidānaṃ doṣāṇāṃ atra evābhidhīyate | satkāyadṛṣṭiranyatra;"

[3.219–3.223,17]

"ata eva moho"'vidyā "doṣāṇāṃ nidānamabhidhīyate" | bhagavatā"'vidyā hetukāḥ " iti punaranyatra pradeśe "satkāyadṛṣṭirdoṣanidānama""bhidhīyate" |

[3.219–3.223,18]

nanvanyepīndriyaviṣayā yoniśomanaskārādayo doṣahetavastatkimavidyāsatkāyadṛṣṭī evābhihite ityāha |

[3.219–3.223,19]

"tatprahāṇe prahāṇataḥ || 223 ||"

[3.219–3.223,20]

tasya mohasya "satkāyadṛṣṭi"lakṣaṇasya "prahāṇe" doṣāṇāṃ "prahāṇataḥ" prādhānyāt sa evokto netara ityarthaḥ || (223)

{iii.v}

<5. apauruṣeyatve>

{3.224}

<(1) vedaprāmāṇyanirāsaḥ>

[3.224,0]

vedapramāṇyaṃ nirācikīrṣan paramatamutthāpayati |

[3.224,1]

"girāmmithyātvahetūnāṃ doṣāṇāṃ puruṣāśrayāt | apauruṣeyaṃ satyārthamiti kecit pracakṣate || 224 ||"

[3.224,2]

"girāṃ" vācāṃ "mithyātvaṃ"sya "hetūnāṃ doṣāṇāma"jñānavisamvādābhiprāyādīnāṃ vā "puruṣa"syā"śrayā"dāśrayaṇatvāt "apauruṣeyaṃ" vākyaṃ mithyātvahetoḥ puruṣadoṣasyābhāvāt "satyārthamiti kecit" jai mi nī yāḥ "pracakṣate" || (224)

{3.225}

[3.225,0]

"girāṃ satyatvahetūnāṃ guṇānāṃ puruṣāśrayāt | apauruṣeyaṃ mithyārthaṃ kiṃ netyanye pracakṣate || 225 ||"

[3.225,1]

tāneva prati girāṃ "satyatvasya hetūnāṃ" dayādharmaparatvādīnāṃ "guṇānāṃ puruṣa"syā"śrayādapauruṣeyaṃ" vākyaṃ satyatāhetoḥ puruṣaguṇasyābhāvāt "mithyārthaṃ kiṃ na" bhavatītyanye sau ga tāḥ pracakṣate || (225)

{3.226}

[3.226,0]

kiñca |

[3.226,1]

[3.226,2]

saṅketamantareṇāpauruṣeyādapi vākyādarthapratīterabhāvāt | "arthajñāpanahetu"riha"saṅketaḥ" svīkartavyaḥ | sa ca puruṣakṛtatvāt "puruṣāśrayaḥ | ataḥ" saṃketasya puruṣāśrayatvāt "girāmapauruṣeyatvepi mithyātvasya sambhavaḥ" | saṃketavaśena vāco'rthaṃ bruvate | sa ca doṣāśrayeṇa puruṣeṇa kriyata iti tāsāṃ na visaṃvādaśaṅkānirāsaḥ | pauruṣeyavākyavaditi vyarthamapauruṣeyatvakalpanaṃ | (226)

{3.227}

<ka. apauruṣeyatvepyaprāmāṇyam>

[3.227,0]

atha śabdārthayoḥ sambandho na pauruṣeyaḥ kintu svābhāvikaḥ tato na mithyātvasambhavaḥ | tadā |

[3.227,1]

"sambandhāpauruṣeyatve syāt pratītirasaṃvidaḥ |"

[3.227,2]

"sambandhāpauruṣeyatve"pīṣyamāṇe1 "syāda"rthānāṃ "pratītirasaṃvido"'vidyamānasaṅketapratīteḥ puṃsaḥ | na cecchabdārthayoḥ sāṃketiko vācyavācakatāsambandhaḥ kintu svābhāvikaḥ | tadā'gṛhītaśaṅketopi śrutācchabdādarthaṃ pratipadyeteti |

[3.227,3]

atha saṃketāt satopi tasya sambandhasyābhivyakti (ḥ) pradīpādivad ghaṭāderato nāgṛhītavyañjakasya vyaṅgyapratītiḥ | tadā |

[3.227,4]

"saṃketāt tadabhivyaktāvasamarthānyakalpanā || 227 ||"

[3.227,5]

"saṃṅketāt ta"sya sambandhasyā"bhivyaktā"viṣyamāṇāyāṃ saṃketā"danya"sya sambandhasya "kalpanā'samarthā" sambandhavyavasthāpanāya | saṃketādeva vācyavācakabhāvasya kalpitasya ghaṭamānatvāt hastasaṃjñāderivārthapratipādanasya | (227)

{3.228}

[3.228,0]

kiñca | vācā kimekenārthena saha vācyavācakasambandhaḥ | athānekaiḥ | tatra |

[3.228,1]

[3.228,3]

[3.228,4]

{3.229}

[3.229,0]

athānekārthābhidhāyyapi śabdaḥ puruṣeṇa saṅketādabhimatārthābhidhāyitvena niyamyate tadā |

[3.229,1]

[3.229,2]

"apauruṣeyatāyāñca vyarthā parikalpanā syāt" | tadabhyupagamepi puruṣasvātantryābhyupagamāt | tadārthebhyo "bhinnānāṃ" śabdānāṃ taiḥ saha "sambandhasya vyava"sthiteḥ | hetuśca vācyoyenāvyabhicāraḥ | na hi śabdārthayostādātmyaṃ bhedāt | nāpi tadutpattirarthamantareṇāpi vivakṣātaḥ śabdotpatteḥ | anyathā cāvyabhicārābhāvāt | (229)

{3.230}

[3.230,0]

uktamarthaṃ saṃgṛhṇānnāha |

[3.230,2]

yadi saṅketanirapekṣāṇāṃ svata eva vācakatvaṃ śabdānāṃ tadā"puṃbhi" saṅketadvāreṇa niyamyatayā "sarvvathā nirarthatā syāt" | puruṣasaṅketanirapekṣācchabdādarthaṃpratīterabhāvāt | etaddoṣabhayāt "saṃskārasyopagame" svīkāre idamapauruṣeyatvaṃ mukhyamanupacaritaṃ "gajasnānambhavet" | gajo hi snāne paṅkamapanīya punastenātmānaṃ limpati | tathā'pauruṣeyatvaṃ sambandhasya svīkṛtyāpi punaḥ saṅkete puruṣāpekṣeti vyaktaṃ sāmyaṃ | (230)

[3.231–3.236aba,11]

asmanmate tu |

[3.231–3.236aba,15]

sambandhasya"nityatvāt āśraya"sya vācyasyā"pāye"pya"nāśo" yadi jāteriva "sammataḥ" tadā "nityeṣu" jātisambandhādiṣvā"śraya"sya vācyasyā vācakasya "ca kiṃ sāmarthya"mupakāraviśeṣādhāyakaṃ"yena" sāmarthyena sa vācyadirā"śraya iṣṭaḥ" | na hyanupakāryamāśritamatiprasaṅgāt | nityasya copakārāsambhavaḥ | bhedābhedakalpanāyāmayuktatvāt
